      <div class="position-bar" id="posBar">
        <div class="pos-ticker" id="posInfo">No open position</div>
        <div class="pos-detail" id="posDetail"></div>
      </div>
      <div class="action-btns">
        <button class="action-btn buy-btn" id="buyBtn" onclick="enterLong()">â–² LONG</button>
        <button class="action-btn sell-btn" id="shortBtn" onclick="enterShort()">â–¼ SHORT</button>
        <button class="next-btn" onclick="nextCandle()">â†’ NEXT CANDLE</button>
      </div>
      <div class="speed-row">
        <span class="speed-label">Auto Speed</span>
        <div class="speed-btns">
          <button class="spd active" onclick="setSpeed(800,this)">1x</button>
          <button class="spd" onclick="setSpeed(400,this)">2x</button>
          <button class="spd" onclick="setSpeed(150,this)">4x</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div class="panel">
      <div class="panel-title">Trade Log</div>
      <div class="trade-log" id="tradeLog">
        <div style="padding:14px;font-family:'Share Tech Mono',monospace;font-size:0.72em;color:var(--muted);">
          No trades yet. Enter LONG or SHORT to start.
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div class="panel">
      <div class="panel-title">How To Use</div>
      <div class="instructions">
        <strong>1.</strong> Type a ticker and click LOAD TICKER, or pick a scenario and click NEW SESSION<br>
        <strong>2.</strong> Real or synthetic candles reveal one at a time<br>
        <strong>3.</strong> Click LONG or SHORT when you see a setup<br>
        <strong>4.</strong> Advance candles â€” your P&L updates live<br>
        <strong>5.</strong> Close position when target/stop is hit<br>
        <strong>6.</strong> Drag to move, mousewheel or +/- to zoom, arrows to pan, 0/RST to reset<br>
        <strong>7.</strong> Review your win rate at the end<br><br>
        <strong>Goal:</strong> Find setups BEFORE seeing the full chart. This trains your pattern recognition.
      </div>
    </div>

  </div>
</div>

<script>
let candles = [];
let visibleCount = 0;
let position = null;
let trades = [];
let autoPlay = false;
let playInterval = null;
let autoSpeed = 800;
let maxVisible = 80;
let viewSize = 80;
let viewOffset = 0;
let dragState = null;
const minViewSize = 12;
let sourceLabel = 'Synthetic scenario';

const CRYPTO_DATA = {
  BTC:'BTCUSDT', XBT:'BTCUSDT', BITCOIN:'BTCUSDT', ETH:'ETHUSDT', ETHEREUM:'ETHUSDT',
  SOL:'SOLUSDT', SOLANA:'SOLUSDT', DOGE:'DOGEUSDT', XRP:'XRPUSDT', ADA:'ADAUSDT',
  BNB:'BNBUSDT', AVAX:'AVAXUSDT', LINK:'LINKUSDT', SUI:'SUIUSDT', PEPE:'PEPEUSDT', SHIB:'SHIBUSDT'
};

const scenarios = {
  trending_up: { drift: 0.3, vol: 1.5, name: 'Bull Trend' },
  trending_down: { drift: -0.3, vol: 1.5, name: 'Bear Trend' },
  volatile: { drift: 0.05, vol: 4, name: 'High Volatility' },
  choppy: { drift: 0, vol: 1, name: 'Choppy Sideways' },
  breakout: { drift: 0.1, vol: 1.2, name: 'Breakout Setup', breakout: true },
  reversal: { drift: -0.2, vol: 1.8, name: 'Reversal Setup', reversal: true },
};

function cleanSymbol(value) {
  return String(value || '').trim().toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9.-]/g, '') || 'AAPL';
}

function cryptoPairFor(value) {
  const clean = cleanSymbol(value).replace(/[.-]/g, '');
  if (CRYPTO_DATA[clean]) return CRYPTO_DATA[clean];
  if (/^[A-Z0-9]{2,12}USDT$/.test(clean)) return clean;
  if (/^[A-Z0-9]{2,12}USD$/.test(clean)) return clean.replace(/USD$/, 'USDT');
  return null;
}

function cryptoBaseFor(value) {
  const pair = cryptoPairFor(value);
  return pair ? pair.replace(/USDT$/, '') : null;
}

function yahooRangeFor(interval) {
  if (interval === '5m') return '5d';
  if (interval === '15m') return '5d';
  if (interval === '1h') return '1mo';
  return '6mo';
}

async function fetchJson(url, label = 'feed') {
  const controller = new AbortController();
  const timeout = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), 8500);
  try {
    const response = await fetch(url, { signal: controller.signal });
    if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`${label} returned ${response.status}`);
    return response.json();
  } finally {
    clearTimeout(timeout);
  }
}

async function fetchPublicApiJson(path, label = 'public API') {
  const cleanPath = String(path || '').replace(/^\/+/, '');
  const urls = [`/api/${cleanPath}`, `/.netlify/functions/${cleanPath}`];
  let lastError = null;
  for (const url of urls) {
    try {
      return await fetchJson(url, label);
    } catch (error) {
      lastError = error;
    }
  }
  throw lastError || new Error(`${label} unavailable`);
}

function publicCandleDate(value) {
  if (!value) return null;
  const numeric = Number(value);
  if (Number.isFinite(numeric)) return new Date(numeric > 100000000000 ? numeric : numeric * 1000);
  const parsed = new Date(value);
  return Number.isNaN(parsed.getTime()) ? null : parsed;
}

async function fetchPublicMarketCandles(symbol) {
  if (!/^https?:$/.test(location.protocol)) throw new Error('Public server API requires hosted mode');
  const data = await fetchPublicApiJson(`analyze?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(cleanSymbol(symbol))}`, 'public candle feed');
  const candles = (data?.candles || []).map(candle => ({
    time: publicCandleDate(candle.time),
    open: Number(candle.open),
    high: Number(candle.high),
    low: Number(candle.low),
    close: Number(candle.close),
    volume: Number(candle.volume)
  })).filter(c => Number.isFinite(c.open) && Number.isFinite(c.close) && Number.isFinite(c.high) && Number.isFinite(c.low));
  if (!candles.length) throw new Error(data?.error || 'Public candle feed returned no candles');
  return { candles, source: data?.candleSource || 'Public server candle feed' };
}

function parseYahooCandles(data) {
  const result = data.chart?.result?.[0];
  const quote = result?.indicators?.quote?.[0];
  if (!quote?.close?.length) throw new Error('No candles returned');
  return quote.close.map((close, index) => ({
    open: Number(quote.open?.[index]),
    close: Number(close),
    high: Number(quote.high?.[index]),
    low: Number(quote.low?.[index]),
    volume: Number(quote.volume?.[index]) || 0,
    time: result.timestamp?.[index] ? new Date(result.timestamp[index] * 1000) : null
  })).filter(c => Number.isFinite(c.open) && Number.isFinite(c.close) && Number.isFinite(c.high) && Number.isFinite(c.low));
}

async function fetchStockCandles(symbol, interval) {
  const yahooUrl = `https://query1.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/${encodeURIComponent(symbol)}?range=${yahooRangeFor(interval)}&interval=${interval}&includePrePost=true`;
  const urls = [
    { url: yahooUrl, label: 'Yahoo direct' },
    { url: `https://api.allorigins.win/raw?url=${encodeURIComponent(yahooUrl)}`, label: 'AllOrigins proxy' },
    { url: `https://corsproxy.io/?${encodeURIComponent(yahooUrl)}`, label: 'CORS proxy' },
    { url: `https://api.codetabs.com/v1/proxy?quest=${encodeURIComponent(yahooUrl)}`, label: 'CodeTabs proxy' }
  ];
  let lastError = null;
  for (const source of urls) {
    try {
      const candles = parseYahooCandles(await fetchJson(source.url, source.label));
      if (candles.length) return { candles, source: source.label };
    } catch (error) {
      lastError = error;
    }
  }
  throw lastError || new Error('Stock candle feed unavailable');
}

async function fetchCryptoCandles(symbol, interval) {
  const pair = cryptoPairFor(symbol);
  const base = cryptoBaseFor(symbol);
  const binanceInterval = interval === '1d' ? '1d' : interval;
  const urls = [
    `https://data-api.binance.vision/api/v3/klines?symbol=${pair}&interval=${binanceInterval}&limit=160`,
    `https://api.binance.us/api/v3/klines?symbol=${pair}&interval=${binanceInterval}&limit=160`,
    `https://api.binance.com/api/v3/klines?symbol=${pair}&interval=${binanceInterval}&limit=160`
  ];
  for (const url of urls) {
    try {
      const rows = await fetchJson(url, 'crypto candles');
      const candles = rows.map(row => ({
        time: new Date(Number(row[0])),
        open: Number(row[1]),
        high: Number(row[2]),
        low: Number(row[3]),
        close: Number(row[4]),
        volume: Number(row[5])
      })).filter(c => Number.isFinite(c.open) && Number.isFinite(c.close) && Number.isFinite(c.high) && Number.isFinite(c.low));
      if (candles.length) return { candles, source: 'Binance candle feed' };
    } catch (error) {}
  }
  if (base) {
    const granularity = interval === '5m' ? 300 : interval === '15m' ? 900 : interval === '1h' ? 3600 : 86400;
    const rows = await fetchJson(`https://api.exchange.coinbase.com/products/${base}-USD/candles?granularity=${granularity}`, 'Coinbase candles');
    const candles = rows.map(row => ({
      time: new Date(Number(row[0]) * 1000),
      low: Number(row[1]),
      high: Number(row[2]),
      open: Number(row[3]),
      close: Number(row[4]),
      volume: Number(row[5])
    })).filter(c => Number.isFinite(c.open) && Number.isFinite(c.close) && Number.isFinite(c.high) && Number.isFinite(c.low)).sort((a, b) => a.time - b.time);
    if (candles.length) return { candles, source: 'Coinbase candle feed' };
  }
  throw new Error('Crypto candle feed unavailable');
}

async function fetchMarketCandles(symbol, interval) {
  try {
    return await fetchPublicMarketCandles(symbol);
  } catch (error) {}
  if (cryptoPairFor(symbol)) return fetchCryptoCandles(symbol, interval);
  return fetchStockCandles(symbol, interval);
}

function generateCandles(scenario) {
  const cfg = scenarios[scenario] || scenarios.trending_up;
  const result = [];
  let price = 150 + Math.random() * 50;
  const total = 100;

  for (let i = 0; i < total; i++) {
    let drift = cfg.drift;

    if (cfg.breakout && i > 60) drift = 0.8;
    if (cfg.reversal && i > 50) drift = 0.5;
    if (cfg.reversal && i < 50) drift = -0.25;

    const change = drift + (Math.random() - 0.5) * cfg.vol * 2;
    const open = price;
    const close = price + change;
    const wm = cfg.vol * 0.5;
    const high = Math.max(open, close) + Math.random() * wm;
    const low = Math.min(open, close) - Math.random() * wm;
    const volume = 50000 + Math.random() * 150000 + (Math.abs(change) > cfg.vol ? 200000 : 0);

    result.push({
      open: parseFloat(open.toFixed(2)),
      close: parseFloat(close.toFixed(2)),
      high: parseFloat(high.toFixed(2)),
      low: parseFloat(low.toFixed(2)),
      volume: Math.round(volume)
    });

    price = close;
  }
  return result;
}

function newSession() {
  const scenario = document.getElementById('scenario').value;
  candles = generateCandles(scenario);
  sourceLabel = scenarios[scenario]?.name || 'Synthetic scenario';
  visibleCount = 20;
  viewSize = 80;
  viewOffset = 0;
  position = null;
  trades = [];
  autoPlay = false;
  clearInterval(playInterval);
  document.getElementById('playBtn').textContent = 'â–¶ AUTO';
  updateStats();
  updatePositionUI();
  renderChart();
  updateHUD();
  renderTradeLog();
  const status = document.getElementById('chartStatus');
  if (status) status.textContent = `${sourceLabel} loaded. Drag chart to pan; wheel or +/- zooms around your cursor.`;
}

async function loadMarketBacktest() {
  const symbol = cleanSymbol(document.getElementById('symbolInput').value);
  const interval = document.getElementById('intervalSelect').value;
  const status = document.getElementById('chartStatus');
  const btn = document.getElementById('loadTickerBtn');
  if (status) status.textContent = `Loading ${symbol} ${interval} candles...`;
  if (btn) {
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.textContent = 'LOADING';
  }
  try {
    const result = await fetchMarketCandles(symbol, interval);
    candles = result.candles.slice(-140);
    sourceLabel = `${symbol} / ${interval} / ${result.source}`;
    visibleCount = Math.min(Math.max(30, Math.floor(candles.length * 0.35)), candles.length);
    viewSize = Math.min(80, visibleCount);
    viewOffset = 0;
    position = null;
    trades = [];
    autoPlay = false;
    clearInterval(playInterval);
    document.getElementById('playBtn').textContent = 'Ã¢â€“Â¶ AUTO';
    updateStats();
    updatePositionUI();
    renderChart();
    updateHUD();
    renderTradeLog();
    if (status) status.textContent = `${sourceLabel} loaded. Backtest reveals only the first ${visibleCount} candles; use NEXT/AUTO to advance.`;
  } catch (error) {
    if (status) status.textContent = `Could not load ${symbol}: ${error.message}. Synthetic scenarios still work.`;
  } finally {
    if (btn) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = 'LOAD TICKER';
    }
  }
}

function nextCandle() {
  if (visibleCount >= candles.length) return;
  visibleCount++;
  if (viewOffset <= 1) viewOffset = 0;
  updatePositionPnL();
  renderChart();
  updateHUD();
}

function clamp(value, min, max) {
  return Math.max(min, Math.min(max, value));
}

function clampView() {
  const revealed = Math.max(1, visibleCount);
  viewSize = clamp(Math.round(viewSize), minViewSize, Math.max(minViewSize, revealed));
  viewOffset = clamp(Math.round(viewOffset), 0, Math.max(0, revealed - viewSize));
}

function getViewRange() {
  clampView();
  const end = Math.max(1, visibleCount - viewOffset);
  const start = Math.max(0, end - viewSize);
  return { start, end };
}

function zoomChart(direction, anchorRatio = 1) {
  if (!candles.length) return;
  const before = getViewRange();
  const oldSize = before.end - before.start;
  const anchorIndex = before.start + clamp(anchorRatio, 0, 1) * oldSize;
  const factor = direction < 0 ? 0.75 : 1.35;
  viewSize = clamp(Math.round(viewSize * factor), minViewSize, Math.max(minViewSize, visibleCount));
  const newStart = clamp(Math.round(anchorIndex - clamp(anchorRatio, 0, 1) * viewSize), 0, Math.max(0, visibleCount - viewSize));
  const newEnd = newStart + viewSize;
  viewOffset = visibleCount - newEnd;
  clampView();
  renderChart();
  updateHUD();
}

function panChart(candlesToMove) {
  if (!candles.length) return;
  viewOffset += candlesToMove;
  clampView();
  renderChart();
  updateHUD();
}

function resetChartView() {
  viewSize = 80;
  viewOffset = 0;
  clampView();
  renderChart();
  updateHUD();
}

function togglePlay() {
  autoPlay = !autoPlay;
  document.getElementById('playBtn').textContent = autoPlay ? 'â¸ PAUSE' : 'â–¶ AUTO';
  if (autoPlay) {
    playInterval = setInterval(() => {
      if (visibleCount < candles.length) {
        nextCandle();
      } else {
        clearInterval(playInterval);
        autoPlay = false;
        document.getElementById('playBtn').textContent = 'â–¶ AUTO';
      }
    }, autoSpeed);
  } else {
    clearInterval(playInterval);
  }
}

function setSpeed(ms, btn) {
  autoSpeed = ms;
  document.querySelectorAll('.spd').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  btn.classList.add('active');
  if (autoPlay) {
    clearInterval(playInterval);
    togglePlay();
    togglePlay();
  }
}

function enterLong() {
  if (position) { closePosition(); return; }
  const price = candles[visibleCount - 1].close;
  position = { dir: 'LONG', entry: price, shares: 100, candle: visibleCount };
  updatePositionUI();
}

function enterShort() {
  if (position) { closePosition(); return; }
  const price = candles[visibleCount - 1].close;
  position = { dir: 'SHORT', entry: price, shares: 100, candle: visibleCount };
  updatePositionUI();
}

function closePosition() {
  if (!position) return;
  const exit = candles[visibleCount - 1].close;
  const mult = position.dir === 'LONG' ? 1 : -1;
  const pnl = (exit - position.entry) * position.shares * mult;
  const rr = Math.abs(pnl / (position.entry * 0.01 * position.shares)).toFixed(2);

  const closedTrade = {
    dir: position.dir,
    entry: position.entry,
    exit: exit,
    pnl: pnl,
    rr: rr,
    candle: position.candle
  };
  trades.push(closedTrade);
  if (window.DTO) DTO.recordTrade({
    source: "backtest",
    symbol: document.getElementById('symbolInput')?.value || sourceLabel || "SIM",
    side: position.dir,
    qty: position.shares,
    entry: position.entry,
    exit,
    pnl,
    rr,
    setupType: sourceLabel,
    closedAt: new Date().toISOString()
  });

  position = null;
  updateStats();
  updatePositionUI();
  renderTradeLog();
}

function updatePositionPnL() {
  if (!position) return;
  updatePositionUI();
}

function updatePositionUI() {
  const posBar = document.getElementById('posBar');
  const buyBtn = document.getElementById('buyBtn');
  const shortBtn = document.getElementById('shortBtn');

  if (position) {
    posBar.classList.add('active');
    const curr = candles[visibleCount - 1].close;
    const mult = position.dir === 'LONG' ? 1 : -1;
    const pnl = (curr - position.entry) * position.shares * mult;
    const pnlStr = pnl >= 0 ? `+$${pnl.toFixed(2)}` : `-$${Math.abs(pnl).toFixed(2)}`;
    const color = pnl >= 0 ? '#26de81' : '#ff5252';

    document.getElementById('posInfo').textContent = `${position.dir} @ $${position.entry.toFixed(2)}`;
    document.getElementById('posDetail').innerHTML = `
      Shares: ${position.shares}<br>
      Current: $${curr.toFixed(2)}<br>
      P&L: <span style="color:${color};font-weight:700">${pnlStr}</span>
    `;

    buyBtn.textContent = 'âœ• CLOSE';
    buyBtn.style.gridColumn = 'span 2';
    shortBtn.style.display = 'none';
  } else {
    posBar.classList.remove('active');
    buyBtn.textContent = 'â–² LONG';
    buyBtn.style.gridColumn = '';
    shortBtn.style.display = '';
  }
}

function updateStats() {
  const wins = trades.filter(t => t.pnl > 0);
  const losses = trades.filter(t => t.pnl <= 0);
  const netPnl = trades.reduce((s, t) => s + t.pnl, 0);
  const wr = trades.length > 0 ? (wins.length / trades.length * 100).toFixed(0) : null;
  const avgRR = trades.length > 0 ? (trades.reduce((s,t) => s+parseFloat(t.rr),0)/trades.length).toFixed(2) : null;

  document.getElementById('sTrades').textContent = trades.length;
  document.getElementById('sWins').textContent = wins.length;
  document.getElementById('sLosses').textContent = losses.length;
  document.getElementById('sWinRate').textContent = wr ? `${wr}%` : 'â€”';
  document.getElementById('sNetPnl').textContent = netPnl >= 0 ? `+$${netPnl.toFixed(2)}` : `-$${Math.abs(netPnl).toFixed(2)}`;
  document.getElementById('sNetPnl').className = `stat-val ${netPnl >= 0 ? 'green' : 'red'}`;
  document.getElementById('sAvgRR').textContent = avgRR ? `${avgRR}x` : 'â€”';
}

function renderTradeLog() {
  const el = document.getElementById('tradeLog');
  if (!trades.length) {
    el.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:14px;font-family:\'Share Tech Mono\',monospace;font-size:0.72em;color:var(--muted);">No trades yet.</div>';
    return;
  }

  el.innerHTML = [...trades].reverse().map((t, i) => {
    const pnlStr = t.pnl >= 0 ? `+$${t.pnl.toFixed(2)}` : `-$${Math.abs(t.pnl).toFixed(2)}`;
    const cls = t.pnl >= 0 ? 'win' : 'loss';
    return `<div class="trade-entry">
      <span>${t.dir}</span>
      <span>$${t.entry.toFixed(2)} â†’ $${t.exit.toFixed(2)}</span>
      <span class="${cls}">${pnlStr}</span>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function updateHUD() {
  if (!candles.length) return;
  const c = candles[visibleCount - 1];
  const range = getViewRange();
  document.getElementById('hudPrice').textContent = `$${c.close.toFixed(2)}`;
  document.getElementById('hudCandle').textContent = `${visibleCount} / ${candles.length}`;
  const volK = (c.volume / 1000).toFixed(0);
  document.getElementById('hudVol').textContent = `${volK}K`;
  const viewEl = document.getElementById('hudView');
  if (viewEl) {
    viewEl.textContent = viewOffset === 0 ? `${range.end - range.start} latest` : `${range.start + 1}-${range.end}`;
  }
  const status = document.getElementById('chartStatus');
  if (status && sourceLabel) status.textContent = `${sourceLabel} | View ${range.start + 1}-${range.end} of ${visibleCount} revealed. Drag to pan; wheel zooms around cursor.`;
}

function renderChart() {
  const svg = document.getElementById('chartSvg');
  const area = document.getElementById('chartArea');
  const W = area.clientWidth || 800;
  const H = area.clientHeight || 500;
  svg.setAttribute('viewBox', `0 0 ${W} ${H}`);

  const range = getViewRange();
  const visible = candles.slice(range.start, range.end);
  const n = visible.length;
  if (!n) return;

  const allHigh = Math.max(...visible.map(c => c.high));
  const allLow = Math.min(...visible.map(c => c.low));
  const priceRange = allHigh - allLow || 1;
  const volMax = Math.max(...visible.map(c => c.volume));

  const padL = 10, padR = 60, padT = 30, padB = 80;
  const chartH = H - padT - padB;
  const chartW = W - padL - padR;
  const volH = 50;
  const mainH = chartH - volH - 10;

  const candleW = Math.max(2, Math.min(16, chartW / n - 2));
  const gap = chartW / n;

  const px = (price) => padT + mainH - ((price - allLow) / priceRange) * mainH;
  const cx = (i) => padL + (i + 0.5) * gap;

  let paths = '';

  // MA line (20 period)
  const maData = visible.map((_, i) => {
    const slice = visible.slice(Math.max(0, i - 19), i + 1);
    return slice.reduce((s, c) => s + c.close, 0) / slice.length;
  });

  const maPoints = maData.map((v, i) => `${cx(i)},${px(v)}`).join(' ');
  paths += `<polyline points="${maPoints}" fill="none" stroke="#ff9800" stroke-width="1.5" opacity="0.8"/>`;

  // Support / Resistance (simple)
  const recentLow = Math.min(...visible.slice(-20).map(c => c.low));
  const recentHigh = Math.max(...visible.slice(-20).map(c => c.high));
  paths += `<line x1="${padL}" y1="${px(recentLow)}" x2="${W-padR}" y2="${px(recentLow)}" stroke="#26de81" stroke-width="1" stroke-dasharray="6,4" opacity="0.5"/>`;
  paths += `<line x1="${padL}" y1="${px(recentHigh)}" x2="${W-padR}" y2="${px(recentHigh)}" stroke="#ff5252" stroke-width="1" stroke-dasharray="6,4" opacity="0.5"/>`;
  paths += `<text x="${W-padR+4}" y="${px(recentLow)+4}" fill="#26de81" font-size="9" font-family="monospace" opacity="0.7">SUP</text>`;
  paths += `<text x="${W-padR+4}" y="${px(recentHigh)+4}" fill="#ff5252" font-size="9" font-family="monospace" opacity="0.7">RES</text>`;

  // Position marker
  if (position) {
    const entryY = px(position.entry);
    paths += `<line x1="${padL}" y1="${entryY}" x2="${W-padR}" y2="${entryY}" stroke="#2979ff" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4,3" opacity="0.8"/>`;
    paths += `<text x="${W-padR+4}" y="${entryY+4}" fill="#2979ff" font-size="9" font-family="monospace">ENTRY</text>`;
  }

  // Candles
  visible.forEach((c, i) => {
    const x = cx(i);
    const openY = px(c.open);
    const closeY = px(c.close);
    const highY = px(c.high);
    const lowY = px(c.low);
    const isBull = c.close >= c.open;
    const color = isBull ? '#26de81' : '#ff5252';
    const bodyTop = Math.min(openY, closeY);
    const bodyH = Math.max(1, Math.abs(openY - closeY));

    // Wick
    paths += `<line x1="${x}" y1="${highY}" x2="${x}" y2="${lowY}" stroke="${color}" stroke-width="1" opacity="0.7"/>`;
    // Body
    paths += `<rect x="${x - candleW/2}" y="${bodyTop}" width="${candleW}" height="${bodyH}" fill="${color}" rx="1"/>`;

    // Volume bar
    const vH = (c.volume / volMax) * volH;
    const vY = H - padB + 5 + (volH - vH);
    paths += `<rect x="${x - Math.max(1,candleW/2-1)}" y="${vY}" width="${Math.max(1,candleW-2)}" height="${vH}" fill="${color}" opacity="0.4" rx="1"/>`;

    // Trade markers from log
    trades.forEach(t => {
      const idx = t.candle - 1 - range.start;
      if (idx === i) {
        const markerY = bodyTop - 8;
        const markerColor = t.dir === 'LONG' ? '#2979ff' : '#ff4d9e';
        paths += `<circle cx="${x}" cy="${markerY}" r="5" fill="${markerColor}" opacity="0.9"/>`;
      }
    });
  });

  // Price axis labels
  const steps = 5;
  for (let i = 0; i <= steps; i++) {
    const price = allLow + (i / steps) * priceRange;
    const y = px(price);
    paths += `<text x="${W-padR+4}" y="${y+4}" fill="#3a4555" font-size="9" font-family="monospace">$${price.toFixed(0)}</text>`;
    paths += `<line x1="${padL}" y1="${y}" x2="${W-padR}" y2="${y}" stroke="#181c25" stroke-width="0.5"/>`;
  }

  // Current price line
  const curr = visible[visible.length-1].close;
  const currY = px(curr);
  paths += `<line x1="${padL}" y1="${currY}" x2="${W-padR}" y2="${currY}" stroke="#b8ff57" stroke-width="0.8" stroke-dasharray="3,3" opacity="0.5"/>`;
  paths += `<rect x="${W-padR}" y="${currY-9}" width="${padR-2}" height="18" fill="#b8ff57" rx="2"/>`;
  paths += `<text x="${W-padR+4}" y="${currY+4}" fill="#040507" font-size="10" font-family="monospace" font-weight="bold">$${curr.toFixed(2)}</text>`;

  svg.innerHTML = paths;
}

function bindChartNavigation() {
  const area = document.getElementById('chartArea');
  if (!area) return;

  area.addEventListener('wheel', (event) => {
    if (!candles.length) return;
    event.preventDefault();
    const rect = area.getBoundingClientRect();
    const padL = 10;
    const padR = 60;
    const ratio = clamp((event.clientX - rect.left - padL) / Math.max(1, rect.width - padL - padR), 0, 1);
    zoomChart(event.deltaY > 0 ? 1 : -1, ratio);
  }, { passive: false });

  area.addEventListener('pointerdown', (event) => {
    if (!candles.length || event.target.closest('.chart-tools')) return;
    event.preventDefault();
    const range = getViewRange();
    const W = area.clientWidth || 800;
    dragState = {
      x: event.clientX,
      offset: viewOffset,
      candlesPerPixel: Math.max(0.04, (range.end - range.start) / Math.max(260, W))
    };
    area.classList.add('dragging');
    area.setPointerCapture(event.pointerId);
    const status = document.getElementById('chartStatus');
    if (status) status.textContent = `${sourceLabel} | Dragging view. Pull right for older candles, left for newer candles.`;
  });

  area.addEventListener('pointermove', (event) => {
    if (!dragState) return;
    const dx = event.clientX - dragState.x;
    viewOffset = dragState.offset + Math.round(dx * dragState.candlesPerPixel);
    clampView();
    renderChart();
    updateHUD();
  });

  function endDrag(event) {
    if (!dragState) return;
    dragState = null;
    area.classList.remove('dragging');
    try { area.releasePointerCapture(event.pointerId); } catch (error) {}
  }

  area.addEventListener('pointerup', endDrag);
  area.addEventListener('pointercancel', endDrag);
  area.addEventListener('pointerleave', endDrag);

  window.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
    if (!candles.length) return;
    const target = event.target?.tagName;
    if (target === 'INPUT' || target === 'SELECT' || target === 'TEXTAREA') return;
    if (event.key === '+' || event.key === '=') zoomChart(-1);
    if (event.key === '-' || event.key === '_') zoomChart(1);
    if (event.key === 'ArrowLeft') panChart(5);
    if (event.key === 'ArrowRight') panChart(-5);
    if (event.key === '0') resetChartView();
  });

  const symbolInput = document.getElementById('symbolInput');
  if (symbolInput) {
    symbolInput.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
      if (event.key === 'Enter') {
        event.preventDefault();
        loadMarketBacktest();
      }
    });
  }
}

// Initialize
bindChartNavigation();
newSession();

// Re-render on resize
window.addEventListener('resize', () => { if (candles.length) renderChart(); });
</script>

    <script>
        const ENGINE_URL = '/api/bot';
        const WATCHLIST_KEY = 'dtoScannerWatchlist';
        const MAX_SYMBOLS = 15;

        // â”€â”€ Watchlist helpers â”€â”€
        function readWatchlist() {
            try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(WATCHLIST_KEY) || '[]'); }
            catch { return []; }
        }

        function writeWatchlist(list) {
            localStorage.setItem(WATCHLIST_KEY, JSON.stringify(list));
        }

        function cleanSymbol(raw) {
            return String(raw || '').trim().toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9.-]/g, '');
        }

        function watchlistSymbols() {
            return readWatchlist().map(item =>
                typeof item === 'string' ? item : (item?.symbol || '')
            ).filter(Boolean);
        }

        function addToWatchlist(rawSymbol) {
            const symbol = cleanSymbol(rawSymbol);
            if (!symbol) return;
            const list = readWatchlist();
            // Check if already exists
            if (list.some(item => (typeof item === 'string' ? item : item?.symbol) === symbol)) return;
            if (list.length >= MAX_SYMBOLS) {
                alert(`Watchlist is capped at ${MAX_SYMBOLS} symbols. Remove one first.`);
                return;
            }
            list.unshift({ symbol, type: 'Watch', level: '', note: '', savedAt: new Date().toISOString() });
            writeWatchlist(list);
            renderWatchlist();
            syncWatchlistToEngine();
        }

        function removeFromWatchlist(symbol) {
            const list = readWatchlist().filter(item =>
                (typeof item === 'string' ? item : item?.symbol) !== symbol
            );
            writeWatchlist(list);
            renderWatchlist();
            syncWatchlistToEngine();
        }

        function clearWatchlist() {
            if (!confirm("Are you sure you want to clear the entire watchlist?")) return;
            writeWatchlist([]);
            renderWatchlist();
            syncWatchlistToEngine();
        }

        function renderWatchlist() {
            const list = readWatchlist();
            const symbols = list.map(item => typeof item === 'string' ? item : item?.symbol).filter(Boolean);
            document.getElementById('watch-cap').textContent = `${symbols.length} / ${MAX_SYMBOLS} symbols`;
            const container = document.getElementById('watch-list');
            
            if (!symbols.length) {
                container.innerHTML = '<div class="watch-empty">No symbols in watchlist.<br>Add tickers above or use Market Desk.</div>';
                return;
            }

            container.innerHTML = symbols.map(sym => {
                const meta = list.find(item => (typeof item === 'string' ? item : item?.symbol) === sym);
                const note = typeof meta === 'object' ? (meta.type || '') : '';
                return `<div class="watch-item">
                    <span class="watch-symbol">${sym}</span>
                    <span class="watch-meta">${note}</span>
                    <a class="watch-signal" href="signal_dashboard.html?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(sym)}">Signal</a>
                    <button class="watch-remove" onclick="removeFromWatchlist('${sym}')" title="Remove">âœ•</button>
                </div>`;
            }).join('');
        }

        async function syncWatchlistToEngine() {
            const symbols = watchlistSymbols();
            if (!symbols.length) return;
            try {
                await fetch(`${ENGINE_URL}/watchlist`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ symbols })
                });
            } catch {
                // Engine offline â€” localStorage is the source of truth
            }
        }

        document.getElementById('watch-form').addEventListener('submit', e => {
            e.preventDefault();
            const input = document.getElementById('watch-input');
            // Support comma-separated input
            const raw = input.value.split(/[,\s]+/).filter(Boolean);
            raw.forEach(sym => addToWatchlist(sym));
            input.value = '';
        });

        // â”€â”€ Bot status â”€â”€
        async function fetchStatus() {
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${ENGINE_URL}/status`);
                if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Engine unreachable');
                const data = await res.json();
                
                document.getElementById('api-error').style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('engine-dot').className = 'engine-status-dot online';
                document.getElementById('connection-text').innerText = 'Engine: Connected';
                
                const isRunning = data.is_running;
                document.getElementById('bot-status').innerText = isRunning ? 'RUNNING' : 'STOPPED';
                document.getElementById('bot-status').style.color = isRunning ? 'var(--dto-green)' : 'var(--dto-red)';
                
                document.getElementById('btn-start').style.display = isRunning ? 'none' : 'block';
                document.getElementById('btn-stop').style.display = isRunning ? 'block' : 'none';
                
                document.getElementById('active-strategies').innerText = data.strategies.join(', ').replace(/_/g, ' ');
                document.getElementById('active-symbols').innerText = data.active_symbols.join(', ');
                
                if (data.alpaca) {
                    const modeSpan = document.getElementById('alpaca-mode');
                    modeSpan.textContent = data.alpaca.mode.toUpperCase();
                    modeSpan.style.color = data.alpaca.mode === 'live' ? 'var(--dto-red)' : 'var(--dto-gold)';
                    
                    document.getElementById('alpaca-bp').textContent = data.alpaca.buying_power ? '$' + data.alpaca.buying_power.toLocaleString('en-US', {minimumFractionDigits:2, maximumFractionDigits:2}) : '$0.00';
                    document.getElementById('alpaca-eq').textContent = data.alpaca.equity ? '$' + data.alpaca.equity.toLocaleString('en-US', {minimumFractionDigits:2, maximumFractionDigits:2}) : '$0.00';
                }
                
            } catch (error) {
                document.getElementById('api-error').style.display = 'block';
                document.getElementById('engine-dot').className = 'engine-status-dot offline';
                document.getElementById('connection-text').innerText = 'Engine: Offline';
                document.getElementById('bot-status').innerText = 'OFFLINE';
            }
        }

        async function toggleConnectionMode() {
            const currentMode = document.getElementById('alpaca-mode').textContent.toLowerCase();
            if (currentMode === '-') return;
            const targetMode = currentMode === 'paper' ? 'live' : 'paper';
            if (targetMode === 'live') {
                if (!confirm("WARNING: Switching to LIVE mode will execute real trades with real money. Proceed?")) return;
            }
            try {
                await fetch(`${ENGINE_URL}/connection`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ mode: targetMode })
                });
                fetchStatus();
            } catch (e) {
                alert("Failed to toggle connection mode.");
            }
        }

        async function fetchTrades() {
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${ENGINE_URL}/trades`);
                if (!res.ok) throw new Error();
                const trades = await res.json();
                
                const tbody = document.getElementById('trades-body');
                tbody.innerHTML = '';
                
                if (trades.length === 0) {
                    tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="7" style="text-align: center; color: var(--dto-muted); padding: 40px;">No trades recorded in database.</td></tr>';
                    return;
                }
                
                trades.forEach(t => {
                    const tr = document.createElement('tr');
                    const sideClass = t.side.toLowerCase() === 'buy' ? 'buy' : 'sell';
                    const date = new Date(t.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString([], {hour: '2-digit', minute:'2-digit', second:'2-digit'});
                    
                    tr.innerHTML = `
                        <td>${date}</td>
                        <td style="color:var(--dto-cyan)">${t.strategy_name.replace(/_/g, ' ')}</td>
                        <td style="font-weight:700">${t.symbol}</td>
                        <td class="${sideClass}">${t.side.toUpperCase()}</td>
                        <td>${t.qty}</td>
                        <td>$${t.price ? t.price.toFixed(2) : '---'}</td>
                        <td style="opacity:0.7; font-size:10px">${t.status.toUpperCase()}</td>
                    `;
                    tbody.appendChild(tr);
                });
            } catch (error) {
                // Background sync failure
            }
        }

        async function toggleBot(start) {
            const endpoint = start ? '/start' : '/stop';
            try {
                await fetch(`${ENGINE_URL}${endpoint}`, { method: 'POST' });
                await fetchStatus();
            } catch (error) {
                alert('Command execution failed. Check backend logs.');
            }
        }

        // Listen for watchlist changes from other pages
        window.addEventListener('storage', event => {
            if (event.key === WATCHLIST_KEY) renderWatchlist();
        });

        // Boot
        renderWatchlist();
        fetchStatus();
        fetchTrades();
        syncWatchlistToEngine();
        setInterval(() => {
            fetchStatus();
            fetchTrades();
        }, 2000);
    </script>
</body>

<script>
let selectedContract = null;

function setConnectionCard(id, state, title, detail) {
  const card = document.getElementById(id);
  if (!card) return;
  card.classList.remove("good", "warn", "bad");
  card.classList.add(state);
  card.querySelector("strong").textContent = title;
  card.querySelector("p").textContent = detail;
}

function writeConnectionOutput(message, data) {
  const output = document.getElementById("connectionOutput");
  if (!output) return;
  output.textContent = data ? `${message}\n\n${JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)}` : message;
}

async function publicApiFetch(path, options = {}) {
  const cleanPath = String(path || "").replace(/^\/+/, "");
  const urls = [`/api/${cleanPath}`, `/.vercel/functions/${cleanPath}`];
  let lastError = null;
  for (const url of urls) {
    try {
      const response = await fetch(url, options);
      const text = await response.text();
      let data = {};
      try {
        data = text ? JSON.parse(text) : {};
      } catch (error) {
        data = { raw: text };
      }
      if (!response.ok) {
        const error = new Error(data.error || data.message || `${url} returned ${response.status}`);
        error.data = data;
        throw error;
      }
      return { url, data };
    } catch (error) {
      lastError = error;
    }
  }
  throw lastError || new Error("Public server route unavailable");
}

async function testPublicFeed() {
  document.getElementById("connectionPill").textContent = "Testing feed";
  writeConnectionOutput("Testing /api/analyze?symbol=AAPL...");
  if (!/^https?:$/.test(location.protocol)) {
    setConnectionCard("feedCard", "warn", "Hosted Needed", "Open the Vercel URL to test the public server feed.");
    writeConnectionOutput("Local file mode cannot call Vercel Functions. Deploy the full folder, then test /api/analyze?symbol=AAPL from the public URL.");
    return;
  }
  try {
    const { url, data } = await publicApiFetch("analyze?symbol=AAPL");
    setConnectionCard("feedCard", "good", "Connected", `${data.symbol || "AAPL"} via ${data.candleSource || data.source || "public API"}.`);
    document.getElementById("connectionPill").textContent = "Feed online";
    writeConnectionOutput(`Public feed is working through ${url}.`, {
      symbol: data.symbol,
      rating: data.rating,
      price: data.price,
      candleSource: data.candleSource,
      source: data.source,
      asOf: data.asOf
    });
  } catch (error) {
    setConnectionCard("feedCard", "bad", "Blocked", error.message);
    document.getElementById("connectionPill").textContent = "Feed blocked";
    writeConnectionOutput("Public feed test failed. Check that the full folder, vercel.toml, and vercel/functions were deployed.", error.data || { error: error.message });
  }
}

async function testOwnerConnection() {
  document.getElementById("connectionPill").textContent = "Testing Alpaca";
  writeConnectionOutput("Testing server-side Alpaca owner account route...");
  if (!/^https?:$/.test(location.protocol)) {
    setConnectionCard("ownerCard", "warn", "Hosted Needed", "Owner account checks run only after deployment.");
    writeConnectionOutput("Open this page from Vercel, then run Test Owner Alpaca. The browser should never receive your Alpaca secret.");
    return;
  }
  try {
    const { url, data } = await publicApiFetch("alpaca-account");
    setConnectionCard("ownerCard", "good", "Connected", `${data.mode || "paper"} account ${data.account?.status || "ready"}.`);
    setConnectionCard("orderCard", "warn", "Preview Only", "Account is reachable; live submit is still locked by design.");
    document.getElementById("connectionPill").textContent = "Alpaca ready";
    writeConnectionOutput(`Owner Alpaca connection is working through ${url}.`, {
      mode: data.mode,
      endpoint: data.endpoint,
      account: data.account,
      requestId: data.requestId
    });
  } catch (error) {
    const missing = /not configured/i.test(error.message);
    setConnectionCard("ownerCard", missing ? "warn" : "bad", missing ? "Needs Keys" : "Failed", error.message);
    document.getElementById("connectionPill").textContent = missing ? "Add keys" : "Alpaca blocked";
    writeConnectionOutput(
      missing
        ? "Alpaca is not connected yet. Add the environment variables in Vercel, redeploy, then test again."
        : "Alpaca owner connection failed. Use the request id/details below when troubleshooting.",
      error.data || { error: error.message }
    );
  }
}

function openSiteStatus() {
  if (/^https?:$/.test(location.protocol)) {
    window.open("/api/site-status", "_blank", "noopener");
  } else {
    writeConnectionOutput("Server status is available after Vercel deployment at /api/site-status.");
  }
}

async function copyEnvChecklist() {
  const text = [
    "ALPACA_API_KEY_ID=your_paper_key_id",
    "ALPACA_API_SECRET_KEY=your_paper_secret_key",
    "ALPACA_TRADING_BASE_URL=https://paper-api.alpaca.markets",
    "ALPACA_DATA_BASE_URL=https://data.alpaca.markets",
    "ALPACA_STOCK_FEED=iex",
    "ALPACA_CRYPTO_LOC=us",
    "ENABLE_ALPACA_ORDER_SUBMIT=false"
  ].join("\n");
  try {
    await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
    writeConnectionOutput("Copied the Vercel environment checklist. Add these in Vercel Site configuration -> Environment variables, then redeploy.", { env: text.split("\n") });
  } catch (error) {
    writeConnectionOutput("Clipboard was blocked. Copy these Vercel environment variables manually:", { env: text.split("\n") });
  }
}

function showAdminConnect() {
  writeConnectionOutput("Alpaca MCP connection path:\n\n1. Clone github.com/alpacahq/alpaca-mcp-server privately.\n2. Configure it with your Alpaca paper keys outside the public website.\n3. Connect it to an MCP-capable assistant for owner/admin workflows.\n4. Keep public site visitors on signup/login and server-side /api routes.");
}

function money(value) {
  const n = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return "$--";
  return "$" + n.toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
}

function cleanNumber(id, fallback = 0) {
  const value = Number(document.getElementById(id).value);
  return Number.isFinite(value) ? value : fallback;
}

function syntheticOption({ strike, underlying, type }) {
  const distance = Math.abs(strike - underlying);
  const intrinsic = type === "call" ? Math.max(0, underlying - strike) : Math.max(0, strike - underlying);
  const timeValue = Math.max(0.18, underlying * 0.006 - distance * 0.03);
  const mid = Math.max(0.05, intrinsic + timeValue);
  const width = Math.max(0.02, Math.min(0.55, mid * 0.08));
  const deltaBase = Math.max(0.08, Math.min(0.92, 0.5 + ((underlying - strike) / Math.max(underlying * 0.08, 1))));
  const delta = type === "call" ? deltaBase : -(1 - deltaBase);
  return { strike, type, bid: Math.max(0.01, mid - width / 2), ask: mid + width / 2, mid, delta };
}

function updateChain() {
  const underlying = cleanNumber("underlying", 500);
  const step = underlying > 100 ? 5 : 1;
  const base = Math.round(underlying / step) * step;
  const strikes = [-2, -1, 0, 1, 2].map(offset => base + offset * step);
  const contracts = strikes.flatMap(strike => [
    syntheticOption({ strike, underlying, type: "call" }),
    syntheticOption({ strike, underlying, type: "put" })
  ]);
  document.getElementById("chainGrid").innerHTML = contracts.map((contract, index) => `
    <button class="chain-card ${selectedContract === index ? "selected" : ""}" type="button" onclick="selectContract(${index}, ${contract.strike}, '${contract.type}', ${contract.bid.toFixed(2)}, ${contract.ask.toFixed(2)}, ${contract.delta.toFixed(2)})">
      <span>${contract.type.toUpperCase()} ${contract.strike}</span>
      <strong>${money(contract.mid)}</strong>
      <div class="fine">Bid ${money(contract.bid)} / Ask ${money(contract.ask)} / Delta ${contract.delta.toFixed(2)}</div>
    </button>
  `).join("");
}

function selectContract(index, strike, type, bid, ask, delta) {
  selectedContract = index;
  document.getElementById("longStrike").value = strike;
  document.getElementById("longAsk").value = ask;
  const strategy = document.getElementById("strategy");
  if (type === "put" && strategy.value === "debit_call") strategy.value = "debit_put";
  if (type === "call" && strategy.value === "debit_put") strategy.value = "debit_call";
  updateChain();
  updatePreview();
}

function strategySide(strategy) {
  return strategy.includes("put") ? "put" : "call";
}

function updatePreview() {
  const strategy = document.getElementById("strategy").value;
  const underlying = cleanNumber("underlying", 500);
  const longStrike = cleanNumber("longStrike", underlying);
  const shortStrike = cleanNumber("shortStrike", underlying);
  const longAsk = cleanNumber("longAsk", 0);
  const shortBid = cleanNumber("shortBid", 0);
  const contracts = Math.max(1, Math.floor(cleanNumber("contracts", 1)));
  const width = Math.abs(shortStrike - longStrike);
  const netDebit = Math.max(0, longAsk - shortBid);
  const netCredit = Math.max(0, shortBid - longAsk);
  const isCredit = strategy.includes("credit");
  const isProtective = strategy.includes("protective");
  const side = strategySide(strategy);
  let maxLoss = 0;
  let maxProfit = 0;
  let breakeven = 0;
  let net = 0;

  if (isProtective) {
    net = longAsk;
    maxLoss = longAsk * 100 * contracts;
    maxProfit = Infinity;
    breakeven = side === "put" ? underlying + longAsk : underlying - longAsk;
  } else if (isCredit) {
    net = netCredit;
    maxProfit = netCredit * 100 * contracts;
    maxLoss = Math.max(0, (width - netCredit) * 100 * contracts);
    breakeven = side === "put" ? shortStrike - netCredit : shortStrike + netCredit;
  } else {
    net = netDebit;
    maxLoss = netDebit * 100 * contracts;
    maxProfit = Math.max(0, (width - netDebit) * 100 * contracts);
    breakeven = side === "put" ? longStrike - netDebit : longStrike + netDebit;
  }

  const widthDollars = Math.abs(longAsk - shortBid);
  const liquidity = widthDollars <= 0.10 ? "Tight" : widthDollars <= 0.35 ? "Okay" : "Wide";
  document.getElementById("netCost").textContent = `${isCredit ? "Credit" : "Debit"} ${money(net * 100 * contracts)}`;
  document.getElementById("maxLoss").textContent = money(maxLoss);
  document.getElementById("maxProfit").textContent = Number.isFinite(maxProfit) ? money(maxProfit) : "Open-ended";
  document.getElementById("breakeven").textContent = money(breakeven);
  document.getElementById("spreadWidth").textContent = money(widthDollars);
  document.getElementById("liquidity").textContent = liquidity;
  const warnings = [];
  if (!isProtective && width <= 0) warnings.push("Spread width must be above zero.");
  if (widthDollars > 0.35) warnings.push("Bid/ask width is wide. Use limit orders and consider skipping if fills are poor.");
  if (!isProtective && maxProfit <= 0) warnings.push("This spread has no positive max-profit estimate with the current inputs.");
  warnings.push("Paper preview only. Use this to plan risk until broker connection, account checks, and final confirmation are live.");
  document.getElementById("previewWarning").textContent = warnings.join(" ");
}

async function savePreview() {
  const preview = {
    symbol: document.getElementById("symbol").value.trim().toUpperCase(),
    strategy: document.getElementById("strategy").value,
    underlying: cleanNumber("underlying", 0),
    longStrike: cleanNumber("longStrike", 0),
    shortStrike: cleanNumber("shortStrike", 0),
    longAsk: cleanNumber("longAsk", 0),
    shortBid: cleanNumber("shortBid", 0),
    contracts: cleanNumber("contracts", 1),
    savedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    liveStatus: "LOCKED"
  };
  localStorage.setItem("dtoBrokerExecutionPreview", JSON.stringify(preview));
  if (!/^https?:$/.test(location.protocol)) {
    document.getElementById("previewWarning").textContent = "Paper preview saved locally. Hosted mode can also test the private preview service.";
    return;
  }
  try {
    const payload = JSON.stringify({
      symbol: preview.symbol,
      side: "buy",
      type: "limit",
      qty: preview.contracts,
      limit_price: preview.longAsk,
      time_in_force: "day"
    });
    const { data } = await publicApiFetch("alpaca-order-preview", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
      body: payload
    });
    localStorage.setItem("dtoBrokerExecutionPreviewResponse", JSON.stringify(data));
    document.getElementById("previewWarning").textContent = data.ok
      ? `Private preview saved. Preview id: ${data.previewId}. Live submit remains locked.`
      : `Private preview warning: ${(data.warnings || [data.error || "preview blocked"]).join(" ")}`;
  } catch (error) {
    document.getElementById("previewWarning").textContent = `Paper preview saved locally. Private preview service did not respond: ${error.message}`;
  }
}

function loadFromSetup() {
  try {
    const setup = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("dtoLastSetup") || "null");
    if (!setup) return;
    if (setup.symbol) document.getElementById("symbol").value = String(setup.symbol).toUpperCase();
    if (setup.entry) document.getElementById("underlying").value = Number(setup.entry).toFixed(2);
  } catch (error) {}
}

function selectAccountType(type) {
  const notes = {
    cash: `<strong style="color:#00e08a">Cash Account Selected</strong><br>
      â€¢ Buying power = settled cash only. Funds from a sale take T+1 to settle.<br>
      â€¢ No margin, no leverage â€” you can only buy with money you have.<br>
      â€¢ No PDT (Pattern Day Trader) rule concern for true cash accounts, but violating "free riding" (selling unsettled purchases) is restricted.<br>
      â€¢ Best for: conservative accounts, smaller balances, swing trading with settled funds.<br>
      â€¢ Alpaca cash accounts: set <code>ALPACA_TRADING_BASE_URL=https://paper-api.alpaca.markets</code> and paper trade first.`,
    margin: `<strong style="color:#00d9ff">Margin Account Selected</strong><br>
      â€¢ Buying power = settled cash + margin. Alpaca typically offers 4:1 intraday / 2:1 overnight leverage.<br>
      â€¢ PDT rule applies: if your account is under $25,000, you are limited to 3 round-trip day trades per rolling 5-business-day period.<br>
      â€¢ Margin calls can force liquidations if equity drops below maintenance margin (~25%).<br>
      â€¢ Best for: active traders, larger balances, strategies that need intraday flexibility.<br>
      â€¢ Requires: enough equity to avoid PDT restrictions or a balance â‰¥ $25,000 for unlimited day trades.`
  };
  const pill = document.getElementById('accountTypePill');
  const note = document.getElementById('accountTypeNote');
  const cashBtn = document.getElementById('cashBtn');
  const marginBtn = document.getElementById('marginBtn');
  if (pill) pill.textContent = type === 'cash' ? 'Cash Account' : 'Margin Account';
  if (note) note.innerHTML = notes[type] || '';
  if (cashBtn) cashBtn.classList.toggle('active', type === 'cash');
  if (marginBtn) marginBtn.classList.toggle('active', type === 'margin');
  try { localStorage.setItem('dtoBrokerAccountType', type); } catch(e) {}
}

loadFromSetup();
updateChain();
updatePreview();

// Restore saved account type selection
try {
  const saved = localStorage.getItem('dtoBrokerAccountType');
  if (saved === 'cash' || saved === 'margin') selectAccountType(saved);
} catch(e) {}
</script>

</html>

        }
