    <script>
        let chart = null;
        let currentVolumeContext = null;

        const CRYPTO_DATA = {
            BTC: "BTCUSDT", BITCOIN: "BTCUSDT", ETH: "ETHUSDT", ETHEREUM: "ETHUSDT",
            SOL: "SOLUSDT", SOLANA: "SOLUSDT", DOGE: "DOGEUSDT", XRP: "XRPUSDT",
            BNB: "BNBUSDT", AVAX: "AVAXUSDT", LINK: "LINKUSDT", SUI: "SUIUSDT",
            PEPE: "PEPEUSDT", SHIB: "SHIBUSDT", ADA: "ADAUSDT", LTC: "LTCUSDT"
        };

        function cleanSymbol(value) {
            return String(value || "").trim().toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9.^-]/g, "") || "AAPL";
        }

        function cryptoPairFor(value) {
            const key = cleanSymbol(value).replace(/[-^]/g, "");
            if (CRYPTO_DATA[key]) return CRYPTO_DATA[key];
            if (/^[A-Z0-9]{2,12}USDT$/.test(key)) return key;
            if (/^[A-Z0-9]{2,12}USD$/.test(key)) return key.replace(/USD$/, "USDT");
            return null;
        }

        function cryptoBaseFor(value) {
            const pair = cryptoPairFor(value);
            return pair ? pair.replace(/USDT$/, "") : null;
        }

        function compactNumber(value) {
            const n = Number(value);
            if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return "--";
            return Intl.NumberFormat("en", { notation: "compact", maximumFractionDigits: 1 }).format(n);
        }

        function money(value) {
            const n = Number(value);
            if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return "$--";
            return "$" + n.toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: n >= 1 ? 2 : 6 });
        }

        function avg(values) {
            const nums = values.filter(Number.isFinite);
            return nums.length ? nums.reduce((sum, value) => sum + value, 0) / nums.length : null;
        }

        function clamp(value, min, max) {
            return Math.max(min, Math.min(max, value));
        }

        async function fetchJson(url, label = "feed") {
            const controller = new AbortController();
            const timeout = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), 8500);
            try {
                const response = await fetch(url, { signal: controller.signal });
                if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`${label} returned ${response.status}`);
                return await response.json();
            } finally {
                clearTimeout(timeout);
            }
        }

        async function fetchPublicApiJson(path, label = "public API") {
            const cleanPath = String(path || "").replace(/^\/+/, "");
            const urls = [`/api/${cleanPath}`, `/.netlify/functions/${cleanPath}`];
            let lastError = null;
            for (const url of urls) {
                try {
                    return await fetchJson(url, label);
                } catch (error) {
                    lastError = error;
                }
            }
            throw lastError || new Error(`${label} unavailable`);
        }

        function publicCandleTime(value) {
            if (!value) return null;
            const numeric = Number(value);
            if (Number.isFinite(numeric)) return new Date(numeric > 100000000000 ? numeric : numeric * 1000);
            const parsed = new Date(value);
            return Number.isNaN(parsed.getTime()) ? null : parsed;
        }

        async function fetchPublicCandles(symbol) {
            if (!/^https?:$/.test(location.protocol)) throw new Error("Public server API requires hosted mode");
            const data = await fetchPublicApiJson(`analyze?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(cleanSymbol(symbol))}`, "public candle feed");
            const candles = (data?.candles || []).map(candle => ({
                time: publicCandleTime(candle.time),
                open: Number(candle.open),
                high: Number(candle.high),
                low: Number(candle.low),
                close: Number(candle.close),
                volume: Number(candle.volume)
            })).filter(candle => Number.isFinite(candle.close) && Number.isFinite(candle.high) && Number.isFinite(candle.low));
            if (!candles.length) throw new Error(data?.error || "Public candle feed returned no candles");
            return { candles, source: data?.candleSource || "Public server candle feed" };
        }

        function marketProxySources(url, label) {
            return [
                { url, label: `${label} direct` },
                { url: `https://api.allorigins.win/raw?url=${encodeURIComponent(url)}`, label: `${label} AllOrigins` },
                { url: `https://corsproxy.io/?${encodeURIComponent(url)}`, label: `${label} CORS proxy` },
                { url: `https://api.codetabs.com/v1/proxy?quest=${encodeURIComponent(url)}`, label: `${label} CodeTabs` }
            ];
        }

        function yahooRangeFor(interval) {
            if (interval === "1m") return "1d";
            if (interval === "5m") return "5d";
            if (interval === "15m") return "5d";
            return "1mo";
        }

        function parseYahooCandles(data) {
            const result = data.chart?.result?.[0];
            const quote = result?.indicators?.quote?.[0];
            if (!quote?.close?.length) throw new Error("No candles returned");
            return quote.close.map((close, index) => ({
                time: result.timestamp?.[index] ? new Date(result.timestamp[index] * 1000) : null,
                open: Number(quote.open?.[index]),
                high: Number(quote.high?.[index]),
                low: Number(quote.low?.[index]),
                close: Number(close),
                volume: Number(quote.volume?.[index])
            })).filter(candle => Number.isFinite(candle.close) && Number.isFinite(candle.high) && Number.isFinite(candle.low));
        }

        async function fetchStockCandles(symbol, interval) {
            const yahooUrl = `https://query1.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/${encodeURIComponent(symbol)}?range=${yahooRangeFor(interval)}&interval=${interval}&includePrePost=true`;
            let lastError = null;
            for (const source of marketProxySources(yahooUrl, "Yahoo candles")) {
                try {
                    const candles = parseYahooCandles(await fetchJson(source.url, source.label));
                    if (candles.length) return { candles, source: source.label };
                } catch (error) {
                    lastError = error;
                }
            }
            throw lastError || new Error("Stock candle feed unavailable");
        }

        async function fetchCryptoCandles(symbol, interval) {
            const pair = cryptoPairFor(symbol);
            const base = cryptoBaseFor(symbol);
            const binanceInterval = interval === "1m" ? "1m" : interval === "15m" ? "15m" : interval === "1h" ? "1h" : "5m";
            const urls = [
                `https://data-api.binance.vision/api/v3/klines?symbol=${pair}&interval=${binanceInterval}&limit=160`,
                `https://api.binance.us/api/v3/klines?symbol=${pair}&interval=${binanceInterval}&limit=160`,
                `https://api.binance.com/api/v3/klines?symbol=${pair}&interval=${binanceInterval}&limit=160`
            ];
            for (const url of urls) {
                try {
                    const rows = await fetchJson(url, "crypto candles");
                    const candles = rows.map(row => ({
                        time: new Date(Number(row[0])),
                        open: Number(row[1]),
                        high: Number(row[2]),
                        low: Number(row[3]),
                        close: Number(row[4]),
                        volume: Number(row[5])
                    })).filter(candle => Number.isFinite(candle.close) && Number.isFinite(candle.high) && Number.isFinite(candle.low));
                    if (candles.length) return { candles, source: "Binance candle feed" };
                } catch (error) {}
            }
            if (base) {
                const granularity = interval === "1m" ? 60 : interval === "15m" ? 900 : interval === "1h" ? 3600 : 300;
                const rows = await fetchJson(`https://api.exchange.coinbase.com/products/${base}-USD/candles?granularity=${granularity}`, "Coinbase candles");
                const candles = rows.map(row => ({
                    time: new Date(Number(row[0]) * 1000),
                    low: Number(row[1]),
                    high: Number(row[2]),
                    open: Number(row[3]),
                    close: Number(row[4]),
                    volume: Number(row[5])
                })).filter(candle => Number.isFinite(candle.close) && Number.isFinite(candle.high) && Number.isFinite(candle.low)).sort((a, b) => a.time - b.time).slice(-160);
                if (candles.length) return { candles, source: "Coinbase candle feed" };
            }
            throw new Error("Crypto candle feed unavailable");
        }

        async function fetchCandles(symbol, interval) {
            const clean = cleanSymbol(symbol);
            try {
                return await fetchPublicCandles(clean);
            } catch (error) {}
            if (cryptoPairFor(clean)) return fetchCryptoCandles(clean, interval);
            return fetchStockCandles(clean, interval);
        }

        function generateMockData(days = 30) {
            let data = [];
            let basePrice = 100 + Math.random() * 100;
            
            for (let i = 0; i < days; i++) {
                const change = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 4;
                const open = basePrice;
                const close = basePrice + change;
                const high = Math.max(open, close) + Math.random() * 2;
                const low = Math.min(open, close) - Math.random() * 2;
                
                data.push({
                    time: new Date(Date.now() - (days - i) * 5 * 60 * 1000),
                    open: parseFloat(open.toFixed(2)),
                    close: parseFloat(close.toFixed(2)),
                    high: parseFloat(high.toFixed(2)),
                    low: parseFloat(low.toFixed(2)),
                    volume: Math.round(800000 + Math.random() * 1800000)
                });
                
                basePrice = close;
            }
            return data;
        }

        function calculateMovingAverage(data, period) {
            return data.map((_, i) => {
                if (i < period - 1) return null;
                const sum = data.slice(i - period + 1, i + 1)
                    .reduce((acc, candle) => acc + candle.close, 0);
                return parseFloat((sum / period).toFixed(2));
            });
        }

        function findSupportResistance(data) {
            const closes = data.map(d => d.close);
            const highs = data.map(d => d.high);
            const lows = data.map(d => d.low);

            const avgHigh = highs.reduce((a, b) => a + b) / highs.length;
            const avgLow = lows.reduce((a, b) => a + b) / lows.length;
            const resistance = Math.max(...highs);
            const support = Math.min(...lows);

            return { support, resistance };
        }

        function calculateVwap(data) {
            const totals = data.reduce((acc, candle) => {
                const volume = Number(candle.volume) || 0;
                const typical = ((Number(candle.high) || candle.close) + (Number(candle.low) || candle.close) + candle.close) / 3;
                acc.priceVolume += typical * volume;
                acc.volume += volume;
                return acc;
            }, { priceVolume: 0, volume: 0 });
            return totals.volume ? totals.priceVolume / totals.volume : null;
        }

        function calculateVolumeIndex(data, ticker, source) {
            const recent = data.slice(-80);
            const last = recent[recent.length - 1];
            const prev = recent[recent.length - 2] || last;
            const volumes = recent.map(c => Number(c.volume)).filter(Number.isFinite);
            const avgVol20 = avg(volumes.slice(-25, -1)) || avg(volumes) || 0;
            const avgVol5 = avg(volumes.slice(-5)) || 0;
            const priorVol20 = avg(volumes.slice(-30, -5)) || avgVol20 || 1;
            const latestVolume = Number(last.volume) || 0;
            const relVolume = avgVol20 ? latestVolume / avgVol20 : 1;
            const volumeTrend = priorVol20 ? avgVol5 / priorVol20 : 1;
            const upVolume = recent.filter(c => c.close >= c.open).reduce((sum, c) => sum + (Number(c.volume) || 0), 0);
            const downVolume = recent.filter(c => c.close < c.open).reduce((sum, c) => sum + (Number(c.volume) || 0), 0);
            const flowRatio = downVolume ? upVolume / downVolume : upVolume ? 3 : 1;
            const vwap = calculateVwap(recent);
            const vwapDistance = vwap ? ((last.close - vwap) / vwap) * 100 : 0;
            const ranges = recent.map(c => Math.abs(c.high - c.low)).filter(Number.isFinite);
            const rangeExpansion = (avg(ranges.slice(-5)) || 0) / (avg(ranges.slice(-30, -5)) || avg(ranges) || 1);
            const priceChange = prev.close ? ((last.close - prev.close) / prev.close) * 100 : 0;

            let score = 42;
            score += clamp((relVolume - 1) * 24, -14, 28);
            score += clamp((volumeTrend - 1) * 18, -10, 18);
            score += clamp((rangeExpansion - 1) * 14, -8, 16);
            score += clamp(Math.abs(vwapDistance) * 1.8, 0, 14);
            score += Math.abs(priceChange) > 0.35 ? 6 : 0;
            score = Math.round(clamp(score, 5, 95));

            const flowBias = vwapDistance > 0.15 && flowRatio > 1.1 ? "Bullish volume pressure" : vwapDistance < -0.15 && flowRatio < 0.9 ? "Bearish volume pressure" : "Mixed / two-way flow";
            const state = score >= 75 ? "Hot volume" : score >= 55 ? "Active" : score >= 35 ? "Normal" : "Quiet";
            const hedgeBias = score >= 70
                ? "Hedge active intraday swings"
                : score >= 50
                    ? "Use conditional hedge triggers"
                    : "Hedge only if level breaks";

            return {
                ticker,
                source,
                price: last.close,
                latestVolume,
                avgVol20,
                relVolume,
                volumeTrend,
                flowRatio,
                flowBias,
                vwap,
                vwapDistance,
                rangeExpansion,
                priceChange,
                score,
                state,
                hedgeBias,
                updatedAt: new Date()
            };
        }

        function renderVolumeIndex(context) {
            currentVolumeContext = context;
            const scoreColor = context.score >= 75 ? "#ff3232" : context.score >= 55 ? "#ff9600" : "#00d4ff";
            document.getElementById("vhiScore").textContent = context.score;
            document.getElementById("vhiState").textContent = context.state;
            document.getElementById("vhiFill").style.width = `${context.score}%`;
            document.getElementById("vhiFill").style.background = scoreColor;
            document.getElementById("relVolume").textContent = `${context.relVolume.toFixed(2)}x avg`;
            document.getElementById("vwapDistance").textContent = `${context.vwapDistance >= 0 ? "+" : ""}${context.vwapDistance.toFixed(2)}%`;
            document.getElementById("flowBias").textContent = context.flowBias;
            document.getElementById("rangeExpansion").textContent = `${context.rangeExpansion.toFixed(2)}x`;
            document.getElementById("latestVolume").textContent = compactNumber(context.latestVolume);
            document.getElementById("volumeTrend").textContent = `${context.volumeTrend.toFixed(2)}x baseline`;
            document.getElementById("vwapLevel").textContent = money(context.vwap);
            document.getElementById("hedgeBias").textContent = context.hedgeBias;
            estimateHedge();
        }

        function estimateHedge() {
            const shares = Number(document.getElementById("hedgeShares")?.value) || 0;
            const hedgePct = clamp(Number(document.getElementById("hedgePct")?.value) || 0, 0, 100);
            const delta = clamp(Math.abs(Number(document.getElementById("optionDelta")?.value) || 0.35), 0.05, 1);
            const side = document.getElementById("hedgeSide")?.value || "long";
            const protectedShares = shares * (hedgePct / 100);
            const contracts = protectedShares ? Math.ceil(protectedShares / (delta * 100)) : 0;
            const hedgeType = side === "long" ? "protective put" : "protective call";
            const deltaCovered = contracts * delta * 100;
            const context = currentVolumeContext;
            const trigger = !context ? "--" : context.score >= 70 ? "Immediate review" : context.score >= 50 ? "Level break" : "Wait";

            document.getElementById("hedgeInstrument").textContent = hedgeType.toUpperCase();
            document.getElementById("hedgeContracts").textContent = contracts ? contracts.toLocaleString() : "--";
            document.getElementById("hedgeDelta").textContent = contracts ? `${Math.round(deltaCovered)} shares` : "--";
            document.getElementById("hedgeTrigger").textContent = trigger;

            if (!context) {
                document.getElementById("hedgePlan").textContent = "Load a ticker to build a volume-aware paper hedge plan.";
                return;
            }

            const directionText = side === "long"
                ? "If you are long the underlying or calls, the paper hedge is downside protection with puts."
                : "If you are short the underlying or holding puts, the paper hedge is upside protection with calls.";
            const pressureText = context.flowBias.includes("Bullish")
                ? "Bullish volume pressure means shorts need faster upside protection, while longs can trail protection below VWAP or support."
                : context.flowBias.includes("Bearish")
                    ? "Bearish volume pressure means longs need faster downside protection, while shorts can trail protection above VWAP or resistance."
                    : "Mixed flow means avoid over-hedging until price accepts above or below VWAP with volume.";

            document.getElementById("hedgePlan").innerHTML =
                `${directionText} For ${shares.toLocaleString()} shares at ${hedgePct}% coverage and ${delta.toFixed(2)} delta, the paper estimate is <strong>${contracts}</strong> ${hedgeType} contract(s), covering roughly <strong>${Math.round(deltaCovered)}</strong> shares of delta.<br><br>` +
                `Volume Hedge Index is <strong>${context.score}/100 (${context.state})</strong>. ${pressureText} Check option spread, implied volatility, expiration, and liquidity manually before using any real-money strategy.`;
        }

        async function loadChart() {
            const ticker = cleanSymbol(document.getElementById('tickerInput').value);
            const interval = document.getElementById('intervalSelect').value;
            
            if (!ticker) {
                showError('Please enter a ticker symbol');
                return;
            }

            showLoading();
            try {
                let data;
                let source;
                try {
                    const result = await fetchCandles(ticker, interval);
                    data = result.candles.slice(-120);
                    source = result.source;
                } catch (error) {
                    data = generateMockData(80);
                    source = "local fallback";
                    showError(`Live candle feed did not respond for ${ticker}; showing fallback structure. Try refresh or a larger ticker.`);
                }

                const ma20 = calculateMovingAverage(data, 20);
                const { support, resistance } = findSupportResistance(data);
                const closes = data.map(d => d.close);
                const returns = [];
                for (let i = 1; i < closes.length; i++) {
                    returns.push((closes[i] - closes[i - 1]) / closes[i - 1] * 100);
                }
                const volatility = Math.sqrt(returns.reduce((sum, r) => sum + r * r, 0) / Math.max(returns.length, 1)).toFixed(2);
                const currentPrice = closes[closes.length - 1];
                const dayHigh = Math.max(...data.slice(-30).map(d => d.high));
                const dayLow = Math.min(...data.slice(-30).map(d => d.low));
                const volumeContext = calculateVolumeIndex(data, ticker, source);

                document.getElementById('tickerDisplay').textContent = ticker;
                document.getElementById('priceDisplay').textContent = money(currentPrice);
                document.getElementById('highDisplay').textContent = money(dayHigh);
                document.getElementById('lowDisplay').textContent = money(dayLow);
                document.getElementById('volatilityDisplay').textContent = `${volatility}%`;

                renderChart(data, ma20, support, resistance, ticker);
                renderVolumeIndex(volumeContext);
                updateChecklist(currentPrice, ma20[ma20.length - 1], support, resistance);
                if (source !== "local fallback") {
                    const statusDiv = document.getElementById('statusMessage');
                    statusDiv.innerHTML = `<div class="info-message">Latest ${interval} candles loaded from ${source}. Volume data is feed-dependent and can be delayed by the provider.</div>`;
                }
            } catch (error) {
                showError(error.message || 'Could not load chart data');
            }
        }

        function renderChart(data, ma20, support, resistance, ticker) {
            const ctx = document.getElementById('chartCanvas').getContext('2d');
            
            const labels = data.map((candle, i) => candle.time ? candle.time.toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit" }) : `Bar ${i + 1}`);
            const closes = data.map(d => d.close);
            const volumes = data.map(d => Number(d.volume) || 0);
            const upColor = "rgba(0, 212, 100, 0.28)";
            const downColor = "rgba(255, 50, 50, 0.28)";

            if (chart) {
                chart.destroy();
            }

            chart = new Chart(ctx, {
                type: 'line',
                data: {
                    labels: labels,
                    datasets: [
                        {
                            label: 'Close Price',
                            data: closes,
                            borderColor: '#00d4ff',
                            backgroundColor: 'rgba(0, 212, 255, 0.1)',
                            borderWidth: 2,
                            fill: true,
                            tension: 0.1,
                            pointRadius: 0,
                            pointHoverRadius: 5
                        },
                        {
                            type: 'bar',
                            label: 'Volume',
                            data: volumes,
                            yAxisID: 'y1',
                            backgroundColor: data.map(candle => candle.close >= candle.open ? upColor : downColor),
                            borderWidth: 0,
                            order: 4
                        },
                        {
                            label: '20-Day MA',
                            data: ma20,
                            borderColor: '#ff9600',
                            borderWidth: 2,
                            fill: false,
                            tension: 0.1,
                            pointRadius: 0
                        },
                        {
                            label: 'Resistance',
                            data: Array(closes.length).fill(resistance),
                            borderColor: '#ff3232',
                            borderDash: [5, 5],
                            borderWidth: 2,
                            fill: false,
                            pointRadius: 0
                        },
                        {
                            label: 'Support',
                            data: Array(closes.length).fill(support),
                            borderColor: '#00d464',
                            borderDash: [5, 5],
                            borderWidth: 2,
                            fill: false,
                            pointRadius: 0
                        }
                    ]
                },
                options: {
                    responsive: true,
                    maintainAspectRatio: true,
                    plugins: {
                        legend: {
                            display: true,
                            labels: {
                                color: '#b3e5ff',
                                font: { family: "'Courier Prime', monospace" }
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    scales: {
                        y: {
                            beginAtZero: false,
                            position: 'left',
                            grid: {
                                color: 'rgba(0, 212, 255, 0.1)'
                            },
                            ticks: {
                                color: '#b3e5ff'
                            }
                        },
                        y1: {
                            beginAtZero: true,
                            position: 'right',
                            grid: {
                                drawOnChartArea: false
                            },
                            ticks: {
                                color: '#8aa6c7',
                                callback: value => compactNumber(value)
                            }
                        },
                        x: {
                            grid: {
                                color: 'rgba(0, 212, 255, 0.05)'
                            },
                            ticks: {
                                color: '#b3e5ff'
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        function updateChecklist(price, ma20, support, resistance) {
            const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.checklist input[type="checkbox"]');
            const checklistItems = document.querySelectorAll('.checklist li');

            // Clear all first
            checklistItems.forEach(li => li.classList.remove('checked'));
            checkboxes.forEach(cb => cb.checked = false);

            // Auto-check based on conditions
            if (price > ma20) {
                checkboxes[0].checked = true;
                checklistItems[0].classList.add('checked');
            }
            
            checkboxes[1].checked = true;
            checklistItems[1].classList.add('checked');
            
            checkboxes[2].checked = true;
            checklistItems[2].classList.add('checked');

            if (currentVolumeContext && currentVolumeContext.relVolume >= 1.15) {
                checkboxes[4].checked = true;
                checklistItems[4].classList.add('checked');
            }

            // Allow manual checking for others
            checkboxes.forEach((cb, i) => {
                cb.onchange = () => {
                    checklistItems[i].classList.toggle('checked');
                    updateSetupStatus();
                };
            });

            updateSetupStatus();
        }

        function updateSetupStatus() {
            const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.checklist input[type="checkbox"]');
            const checked = Array.from(checkboxes).filter(cb => cb.checked).length;
            const total = checkboxes.length;

            const statusDiv = document.getElementById('setupStatus');
            if (checked === total) {
                statusDiv.textContent = 'âœ… READY TO TRADE';
                statusDiv.className = 'status ready';
            } else {
                statusDiv.textContent = `${checked}/${total} conditions met`;
                statusDiv.className = 'status pending';
            }
            statusDiv.style.display = 'block';
        }

        function showLoading() {
            const statusDiv = document.getElementById('statusMessage');
            statusDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="loading"><div class="spinner"></div>Loading latest candle and volume data...</div>';
        }

        function showError(message) {
            const statusDiv = document.getElementById('statusMessage');
            statusDiv.innerHTML = `<div class="error-message">âš ï¸ ${message}</div>`;
        }

        function clearStatus() {
            const statusDiv = document.getElementById('statusMessage');
            statusDiv.innerHTML = '';
        }

        // Allow Enter key to load chart
        document.getElementById('tickerInput').addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') loadChart();
        });
    </script>
<script src="assets/daytrader-os.js?v=20260504-vercel1" defer></script>
</body>

<script>
const $ = id => document.getElementById(id);
const n = id => Number($(id).value);
const money = value => Number.isFinite(Number(value)) ? "$" + Number(value).toFixed(2) : "--";
const clean = value => String(value || "").trim().toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9.-]/g, "");
const isCrypto = sym => /^(BTC|ETH|SOL|DOGE|XRP|BNB|ADA|AVAX|LINK|SUI|PEPE|SHIB|[A-Z0-9]{2,12}(USDT|USD))$/.test(clean(sym));

function riskCalc() {
  const symbol = clean($("symbol").value);
  const crypto = isCrypto(symbol);
  $("assetMode").textContent = crypto ? "Crypto fractional" : "Stock whole shares";
  const account = n("account"), riskPct = n("riskPct") / 100, entry = n("entry"), stop = n("stop"), target = n("target");
  const perUnitRisk = Math.abs(entry - stop);
  const intendedRisk = account * riskPct;
  if (!account || !riskPct || !entry || !stop || !target || perUnitRisk <= 0) {
    $("qtyOut").textContent = "--"; $("riskOut").textContent = "--"; $("notionalOut").textContent = "--"; $("rrOut").textContent = "--";
    $("riskTip").textContent = "Fix setup: entry, stop, target, and account risk must be valid.";
    return;
  }
  const rawQty = intendedRisk / perUnitRisk;
  const qty = crypto ? Number(rawQty.toFixed(8)) : Math.floor(rawQty);
  const actualRisk = qty * perUnitRisk;
  const notional = qty * entry;
  const rr = Math.abs(target - entry) / perUnitRisk;
  $("qtyOut").textContent = crypto ? qty.toLocaleString(undefined, { maximumFractionDigits: 8 }) : qty.toLocaleString();
  $("riskOut").textContent = money(actualRisk);
  $("notionalOut").textContent = `${money(notional)} / ${account ? (notional / account * 100).toFixed(1) : "--"}%`;
  $("rrOut").textContent = `${rr.toFixed(2)}R`;
  const tips = [];
  if (rr < 2) tips.push("R:R is under 2R. Tighten stop, improve target, or skip.");
  if (riskPct > 0.02) tips.push("Risk is above 2%; this is aggressive.");
  if (notional > account) tips.push("Risk size requires leverage or more buying power.");
  if (!crypto && actualRisk < intendedRisk * 0.75) tips.push("Whole-share rounding under-risks this trade.");
  if (crypto) tips.push(`Fractional ${symbol} sizing keeps risk close to intended risk.`);
  $("riskTip").textContent = tips.join(" ") || "Sizing is clean enough to paper trade after chart confirmation.";
  const params = new URLSearchParams({ symbol, side: $("side").value, entry, stop, target });
  $("openRisk").href = `risk_calculator.html?${params}`;
  $("openPaper").href = `paper_trading_simulator.html?${params}`;
}

function spreadCalc() {
  const strategy = $("strategy").value, longStrike = n("longStrike"), shortStrike = n("shortStrike"), contracts = Math.max(1, Math.floor(n("contracts") || 1));
  const longAsk = n("longAsk"), shortBid = n("shortBid"), width = Math.abs(shortStrike - longStrike), isCredit = strategy.includes("credit"), isProtective = strategy.includes("protective"), side = strategy.includes("put") ? "put" : "call";
  const netDebit = Math.max(0, longAsk - shortBid), netCredit = Math.max(0, shortBid - longAsk);
  let net = isCredit ? netCredit : longAsk - shortBid, loss, profit, breakeven;
  if (isProtective) { net = longAsk; loss = longAsk * 100 * contracts; profit = Infinity; breakeven = side === "put" ? longStrike + longAsk : longStrike - longAsk; }
  else if (isCredit) { profit = netCredit * 100 * contracts; loss = Math.max(0, (width - netCredit) * 100 * contracts); breakeven = side === "put" ? shortStrike - netCredit : shortStrike + netCredit; }
  else { loss = netDebit * 100 * contracts; profit = Math.max(0, (width - netDebit) * 100 * contracts); breakeven = side === "put" ? longStrike - netDebit : longStrike + netDebit; }
  $("netOut").textContent = `${isCredit ? "Credit" : "Debit"} ${money(net * 100 * contracts)}`;
  $("lossOut").textContent = money(loss);
  $("profitOut").textContent = Number.isFinite(profit) ? money(profit) : "Open";
  $("beOut").textContent = money(breakeven);
  $("spreadTip").textContent = Math.abs(longAsk - shortBid) > 0.35 ? "Bid/ask width is wide. Use limit orders and consider skipping." : "Spread preview is reasonable for planning. Confirm chain liquidity before acting.";
}

function loadSetup() {
  const setup = window.DTO?.getSetup?.() || {};
  ["symbol","side","entry","stop","target"].forEach(key => { if (setup[key] !== undefined && $(key)) $(key).value = setup[key]; });
  if (setup.entry) { $("longStrike").value = setup.entry; $("shortStrike").value = setup.target || setup.entry; }
  riskCalc(); spreadCalc();
}

async function testStatus() {
  if (!/^https?:$/.test(location.protocol)) { $("brokerNote").textContent = "Deploy to Vercel first, then test /api/site-status."; return; }
  try {
    const res = await fetch("/api/site-status");
    const data = await res.json();
    $("brokerNote").textContent = `Server OK. Data endpoint: ${data.alpaca?.marketDataBaseUrl || "unknown"}. Trading endpoint: ${data.alpaca?.tradingBaseUrl || "unknown"}.`;
  } catch (error) {
    $("brokerNote").textContent = "Server status failed. Check Vercel API functions and environment variables.";
  }
}

document.querySelectorAll("input,select").forEach(el => el.addEventListener("input", () => { riskCalc(); spreadCalc(); }));
$("loadSetup").addEventListener("click", loadSetup);
$("testStatus").addEventListener("click", testStatus);
$("savePreview").addEventListener("click", () => {
  localStorage.setItem("dtoOptionsPreview", JSON.stringify({ strategy: $("strategy").value, longStrike: n("longStrike"), shortStrike: n("shortStrike"), contracts: n("contracts"), savedAt: new Date().toISOString() }));
  $("spreadTip").textContent = "Options preview saved locally.";
});
loadSetup();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script src="assets/daytrader-os.js?v=20260504-vercel1"></script>
<script>
const fields = ["symbol","assetType","side","timeframe","entry","stop","target","rating","support","resistance","confidence","setupType","thesis","catalysts"];
const gates = ["gateLevels","gateRisk","gateCatalyst"];

function el(id) {
  return document.getElementById(id);
}

function val(id) {
  return el(id).value;
}

function num(id) {
  const n = Number(val(id));
  return Number.isFinite(n) ? n : null;
}

function cryptoGuess(symbol) {
  return /^(BTC|ETH|SOL|DOGE|XRP|BNB|ADA|AVAX|LINK|SUI|PEPE|SHIB|LTC|BCH|[A-Z0-9]{2,12}(USDT|USD))$/i.test(String(symbol || "").trim());
}

let lastLiveQuote = null;
let quoteRequestId = 0;
let quoteInputTimer = null;

const cryptoPairs = {
  BTC: "BTCUSDT",
  ETH: "ETHUSDT",
  SOL: "SOLUSDT",
  DOGE: "DOGEUSDT",
  XRP: "XRPUSDT",
  BNB: "BNBUSDT",
  ADA: "ADAUSDT",
  AVAX: "AVAXUSDT",
  LINK: "LINKUSDT",
  SUI: "SUIUSDT",
  PEPE: "PEPEUSDT",
  SHIB: "SHIBUSDT",
  LTC: "LTCUSDT",
  BCH: "BCHUSDT"
};

function cleanSymbol(symbol) {
  return String(symbol || "").trim().toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9.-]/g, "");
}

function fmtPrice(value) {
  const n = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return "--";
  if (n >= 1000) return n.toLocaleString(undefined, { maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
  if (n >= 1) return n.toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
  return n.toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 4, maximumFractionDigits: 8 });
}

function quoteFetch(url, label) {
  const controller = new AbortController();
  const timer = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), 5500);
  return fetch(url, { signal: controller.signal, cache: "no-store" })
    .then(response => {
      clearTimeout(timer);
      if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`${label} HTTP ${response.status}`);
      return response.json();
    });
}

function cryptoPair(symbol) {
  const clean = cleanSymbol(symbol).replace(/[-.]/g, "");
  if (cryptoPairs[clean]) return cryptoPairs[clean];
  if (clean.endsWith("USDT")) return clean;
  if (clean.endsWith("USD")) return `${clean.slice(0, -3)}USDT`;
  return null;
}

async function fetchCryptoQuote(symbol) {
  const pair = cryptoPair(symbol);
  if (!pair) throw new Error("Crypto pair not mapped");
  const urls = [
    `https://api.binance.com/api/v3/ticker/24hr?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(pair)}`,
    `https://data-api.binance.vision/api/v3/ticker/24hr?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(pair)}`
  ];
  let lastError;
  for (const url of urls) {
    try {
      const data = await quoteFetch(url, "Binance");
      return {
        symbol: cleanSymbol(symbol),
        price: Number(data.lastPrice),
        changePct: Number(data.priceChangePercent),
        dayLow: Number(data.lowPrice),
        dayHigh: Number(data.highPrice),
        volume: Number(data.volume),
        source: "Binance 24hr",
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
      };
    } catch (error) {
      lastError = error;
    }
  }
  throw lastError || new Error("Crypto quote unavailable");
}

async function fetchStockQuote(symbol) {
  const clean = cleanSymbol(symbol);
  const url = `https://query1.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/${encodeURIComponent(clean)}?range=1d&interval=1m&includePrePost=true`;
  const data = await quoteFetch(url, "Yahoo chart");
  const result = data?.chart?.result?.[0];
  const meta = result?.meta || {};
  const quote = result?.indicators?.quote?.[0] || {};
  const closes = (quote.close || []).map(Number).filter(Number.isFinite);
  const highs = (quote.high || []).map(Number).filter(Number.isFinite);
  const lows = (quote.low || []).map(Number).filter(Number.isFinite);
  const price = Number(meta.regularMarketPrice) || closes[closes.length - 1];
  const previous = Number(meta.previousClose) || Number(meta.chartPreviousClose);
  if (!Number.isFinite(price)) throw new Error("No stock price returned");
  return {
    symbol: clean,
    price,
    changePct: Number.isFinite(previous) && previous !== 0 ? ((price - previous) / previous) * 100 : null,
    dayLow: lows.length ? Math.min(...lows) : Number(meta.regularMarketDayLow),
    dayHigh: highs.length ? Math.max(...highs) : Number(meta.regularMarketDayHigh),
    volume: Number(meta.regularMarketVolume),
    source: "Yahoo live chart",
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
  };
}

function renderLiveQuote(quote, message = "") {
  const change = Number(quote?.changePct);
  const changeClass = Number.isFinite(change) ? change >= 0 ? "up" : "down" : "";
  el("liveSymbol").textContent = quote?.symbol || "--";
  el("livePrice").textContent = quote?.price ? `$${fmtPrice(quote.price)}` : "--";
  el("liveChange").textContent = Number.isFinite(change) ? `${change >= 0 ? "+" : ""}${change.toFixed(2)}%` : "--";
  el("liveChange").className = changeClass;
  el("liveRange").textContent = quote?.dayLow && quote?.dayHigh ? `$${fmtPrice(quote.dayLow)} - $${fmtPrice(quote.dayHigh)}` : "--";
  el("liveSource").textContent = quote?.source || "--";
  el("liveNote").textContent = message || (quote?.updatedAt ? `Updated ${new Date(quote.updatedAt).toLocaleTimeString()}. Live quote can fill entry/support/resistance, then you still control stop and target.` : "Pick a symbol to pull the latest reachable quote.");
}

function renderQuoteError(symbol, error) {
  lastLiveQuote = null;
  el("liveSymbol").textContent = cleanSymbol(symbol) || "--";
  el("livePrice").textContent = "--";
  el("liveChange").textContent = "--";
  el("liveChange").className = "";
  el("liveRange").textContent = "--";
  el("liveSource").textContent = "Browser/API blocked";
  el("liveNote").textContent = `This local file could not read the quote API directly (${error?.message || "provider/CORS block"}). TradingView can still show the live chart visually, but JavaScript needs a backend proxy to pull stock quotes reliably. Try Refresh Live Price, open Signal Dashboard, or use Yahoo/TradingView for the live entry.`;
}

function applyQuoteToForm(quote, overwrite = false) {
  if (!quote?.price) return;
  if (overwrite || !val("entry")) el("entry").value = Number(quote.price.toFixed(quote.price >= 1 ? 4 : 8));
  if (quote.dayLow && (overwrite || !val("support"))) el("support").value = Number(quote.dayLow.toFixed(quote.dayLow >= 1 ? 4 : 8));
  if (quote.dayHigh && (overwrite || !val("resistance"))) el("resistance").value = Number(quote.dayHigh.toFixed(quote.dayHigh >= 1 ? 4 : 8));
  if (!val("confidence")) el("confidence").value = Number.isFinite(Number(quote.changePct)) ? Math.min(90, Math.max(35, Math.round(55 + Number(quote.changePct) * 2))) : 50;
  if (!val("target") && quote.dayHigh && val("side") === "long") el("target").value = Number(quote.dayHigh.toFixed(quote.dayHigh >= 1 ? 4 : 8));
  if (!val("target") && quote.dayLow && val("side") === "short") el("target").value = Number(quote.dayLow.toFixed(quote.dayLow >= 1 ? 4 : 8));
  if (!val("thesis")) {
    el("thesis").value = `${quote.symbol} live price is $${fmtPrice(quote.price)} from ${quote.source}. Build the trade around current price, day range, trend, volume, catalyst, and a stop that invalidates the setup.`;
  }
  renderGrade();
}

async function refreshLivePrice({ apply = true, overwrite = false } = {}) {
  const symbol = cleanSymbol(val("symbol"));
  if (!symbol) {
    renderQuoteError("", new Error("enter a symbol first"));
    return null;
  }
  const requestId = ++quoteRequestId;
  el("refreshQuoteBtn").textContent = "Loading...";
  renderLiveQuote({ symbol, source: "Loading" }, "Pulling latest reachable quote...");
  try {
    const quote = cryptoGuess(symbol) || val("assetType") === "crypto"
      ? await fetchCryptoQuote(symbol)
      : await fetchStockQuote(symbol);
    if (requestId !== quoteRequestId) return null;
    lastLiveQuote = quote;
    renderLiveQuote(quote);
    if (apply) applyQuoteToForm(quote, overwrite);
    return quote;
  } catch (error) {
    if (requestId === quoteRequestId) renderQuoteError(symbol, error);
    return null;
  } finally {
    if (requestId === quoteRequestId) el("refreshQuoteBtn").textContent = "Refresh Live Price";
  }
}

function setupFromForm() {
  const entry = num("entry");
  const stop = num("stop");
  const target = num("target");
  const rr = entry && stop && target && entry !== stop ? Math.abs(target - entry) / Math.abs(entry - stop) : null;
  return {
    symbol: val("symbol"),
    assetType: val("assetType"),
    side: val("side"),
    timeframe: val("timeframe"),
    entry,
    stop,
    target,
    support: num("support"),
    resistance: num("resistance"),
    confidence: num("confidence"),
    rating: val("rating"),
    rr,
    setupType: val("setupType"),
    thesis: val("thesis"),
    catalysts: val("catalysts").split(/\n|,/).map(item => item.trim()).filter(Boolean),
    riskNotes: gates.filter(id => !el(id).checked).map(id => el(id).closest(".check").innerText.trim()),
    livePrice: lastLiveQuote?.price || null,
    liveSource: lastLiveQuote?.source || "",
    liveUpdatedAt: lastLiveQuote?.updatedAt || "",
    liveDayLow: lastLiveQuote?.dayLow || null,
    liveDayHigh: lastLiveQuote?.dayHigh || null,
    sourcePage: "guided_trade_builder.html",
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString()
  };
}

function gateWarnings() {
  const warnings = [];
  if (!el("gateLevels").checked) warnings.push("Execution gate: levels are not confirmed yet.");
  if (!el("gateRisk").checked) warnings.push("Execution gate: risk/reward is not accepted yet.");
  if (!el("gateCatalyst").checked) warnings.push("Execution gate: catalyst/news context is not confirmed yet.");
  return warnings;
}

function renderGrade() {
  const setup = setupFromForm();
  const grade = DTO.gradeSetup(setup);
  const warnings = [...grade.warnings, ...gateWarnings()];
  const good = warnings.length === 0 && grade.score >= 68;
  el("gradeBox").innerHTML = `
    <div class="score-top">
      <div class="score-ring" style="--score:${grade.score}">
        <div><strong>${grade.score}</strong><span>${DTO.escapeHtml(grade.label)}</span></div>
      </div>
      <div class="score-copy">
        <h3>${good ? "Trade Ready" : grade.label}</h3>
        <p>${DTO.escapeHtml(grade.modeText.beginner)}</p>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="chips">
      <span class="chip">${DTO.escapeHtml(setup.symbol || "No Symbol")}</span>
      <span class="chip">${DTO.escapeHtml(setup.side.toUpperCase())}</span>
      <span class="chip">${setup.rr ? setup.rr.toFixed(2) + "R" : "R:R --"}</span>
      <span class="chip">${DTO.escapeHtml(setup.assetType)}</span>
    </div>
    <div class="blockers">
      ${warnings.length ? warnings.slice(0, 5).map(item => `<div class="blocker">${DTO.escapeHtml(item)}</div>`).join("") : `<div class="blocker good">No major blocker. Still verify live price, liquidity, and your broker feed before acting.</div>`}
    </div>
    <div class="saved-row">
      <div><strong>Packet Preview</strong><small>Entry ${setup.entry || "--"} / Stop ${setup.stop || "--"} / Target ${setup.target || "--"}</small></div>
      <small>${setup.confidence || "--"}/100</small>
    </div>`;
  updateLinks(setup);
}

function updateLinks(rawSetup = setupFromForm()) {
  const setup = DTO.normalizeSetup(rawSetup);
  el("riskLink").href = DTO.workflowUrl("risk_calculator.html", setup);
  el("paperLink").href = DTO.workflowUrl("paper_trading_simulator.html", setup);
  el("strategyLink").href = DTO.workflowUrl("strategy_playbook.html", setup);
  el("backtestLink").href = DTO.workflowUrl("backtest_simulator.html", setup);
  el("journalLink").href = DTO.workflowUrl("trade_journal.html", setup);
}

function saveSetup() {
  const setup = DTO.saveSetup(setupFromForm());
  DTO.renderMissionControl();
  updateLinks(setup);
  el("saveBtn").textContent = `${setup.symbol} Saved`;
  setTimeout(() => { el("saveBtn").textContent = "Save Setup"; }, 1400);
}

function loadSetup() {
  const setup = DTO.getSetup();
  if (!setup) return;
  fields.forEach(id => {
    if (!el(id)) return;
    if (id === "catalysts") el(id).value = Array.isArray(setup.catalysts) ? setup.catalysts.join(", ") : setup.catalysts || "";
    else if (id === "setupType") el(id).value = setup.setupType || "Breakout";
    else if (setup[id] !== null && setup[id] !== undefined) el(id).value = setup[id];
  });
  if (setup.symbol && cryptoGuess(setup.symbol)) el("assetType").value = "crypto";
}

document.querySelectorAll("[data-symbol]").forEach(button => {
  button.addEventListener("click", () => {
    el("symbol").value = button.dataset.symbol;
    el("assetType").value = cryptoGuess(button.dataset.symbol) ? "crypto" : "stock";
    renderGrade();
    refreshLivePrice({ apply: true, overwrite: true });
  });
});

fields.concat(gates).forEach(id => {
  el(id).addEventListener("input", () => {
    if (id === "symbol") {
      if (cryptoGuess(val("symbol"))) el("assetType").value = "crypto";
      clearTimeout(quoteInputTimer);
      const symbol = cleanSymbol(val("symbol"));
      if (symbol.length >= 2) {
        quoteInputTimer = setTimeout(() => refreshLivePrice({ apply: true, overwrite: false }), 750);
      }
    }
    renderGrade();
  });
  el(id).addEventListener("change", renderGrade);
});

el("builderForm").addEventListener("submit", event => {
  event.preventDefault();
  saveSetup();
});
el("saveBtn").addEventListener("click", saveSetup);
el("refreshQuoteBtn").addEventListener("click", () => refreshLivePrice({ apply: true, overwrite: false }));
el("useQuoteBtn").addEventListener("click", () => {
  if (lastLiveQuote) {
    applyQuoteToForm(lastLiveQuote, true);
    renderLiveQuote(lastLiveQuote, `Applied $${fmtPrice(lastLiveQuote.price)} as entry and refreshed the setup grade.`);
  } else {
    refreshLivePrice({ apply: true, overwrite: true });
  }
});

loadSetup();
renderGrade();
DTO.renderMissionControl();
if (val("symbol")) refreshLivePrice({ apply: false, overwrite: false });
</script>
</body>
</html>

  <section id="alpaca-guide" class="dto-tab-content">

      <h2>Alpaca Login Guide</h2>
      <div class="hint">How to connect your broker account to trade on this platform.</div>
    </div>
    <div class="analysis-card" style="margin-top: 16px;">
      <div class="analysis-body">
        <div>
          <h3 style="color: var(--dto-cyan); margin-bottom: 8px;">Bring Your Own Key (User Mode)</h3>
          <p>You can securely connect your own Alpaca account to trade directly from your browser. Your keys are saved locally in your browser and are never sent to our database.</p>
          <ol style="color: var(--dto-muted); font-size: 13px; line-height: 1.6; padding-left: 20px; margin-top: 12px; font-family: 'JetBrains Mono', monospace;">
            <li style="margin-bottom: 8px;">Log in to the <a href="https://app.alpaca.markets/" target="_blank" style="color: var(--dto-cyan);">Alpaca Dashboard</a> and generate your API Keys.</li>
            <li style="margin-bottom: 8px;">Create an account or log in to this site.</li>
            <li style="margin-bottom: 8px;">Click your <strong>Profile</strong> (or the button below).</li>
            <li style="margin-bottom: 8px;">Scroll down to the <strong>Broker Connection (BYOK)</strong> section in the modal.</li>
            <li style="margin-bottom: 8px;">Paste your <strong>Alpaca API Key ID</strong> and <strong>Alpaca API Secret</strong>.</li>
            <li style="margin-bottom: 8px;">Select <strong>Paper Trading</strong> or <strong>Live Trading</strong> from the Trading Mode dropdown, then click <strong>Save Profile</strong>.</li>
            <li>You are now connected! Open the <a href="broker_execution_plan.html" style="color: var(--dto-cyan);">Broker Console</a> to test your connection.</li>
          </ol>
          <div style="margin-top: 20px;">
            <button class="flow-btn primary" type="button" onclick="window.DTO && window.DTO.openAuthModal ? window.DTO.openAuthModal('profile') : alert('Please sign up or log in first!')">Open Profile Settings Now</button>
          </div>
        </div>

<script>
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('.dto-tab-nav button');
    const contents = document.querySelectorAll('.dto-tab-content');
    
    tabs.forEach(tab => {
      tab.addEventListener('click', () => {
        tabs.forEach(t => t.classList.remove('is-active'));
        contents.forEach(c => c.classList.remove('is-active'));
        
        tab.classList.add('is-active');
        const targetId = tab.getAttribute('data-tab-target');
        const targetContent = document.getElementById(targetId);
        if (targetContent) targetContent.classList.add('is-active');
      });
    });
    
    // Handle main nav links to jump to tabs instead of scrolling
    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-links a[href^="#"]').forEach(link => {
      link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        const targetId = link.getAttribute('href').substring(1);
        const tabButton = document.querySelector(`.dto-tab-nav button[data-tab-target="${targetId}"]`);
        if (tabButton) {
          e.preventDefault();
          tabButton.click();
          // Adjust scroll position to account for sticky header if there is one
          const offset = 80;
          const topPos = tabButton.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.scrollY - offset;
          window.scrollTo({ top: topPos, behavior: 'smooth' });
        }
      });
    });
  });
</script>

<script src="assets/daytrader-os.js?v=20260504-vercel1"></script>
<script src="assets/dto-core.js"></script>
<script>

  function renderMarketContext(data) {
    const symbol = data.symbol || "AAPL";
    const context = data.marketContext || marketContextForSymbol(symbol, data.news || []);
    const feeds = context.feeds || {};
    const sourceCards = [feeds.yahoo, feeds.cnbc, feeds.earnings, feeds.sec, feeds.macro, feeds.sector, feeds.groundNews]
      .filter(Boolean)
      .map(feed => `
        <div class="source-card">
          <strong>${escapeHtml(feed.label || "Source Check")}</strong>
          <a href="${escapeHtml(feed.url || "#")}" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Open â†—</a>
        </div>`)
      .join("");
    const headlines = (feeds.headlines || []).slice(0, 5);
    // Only render the summary list once â€” skip if we already have real headlines
    const statusLine = headlines.length
      ? `<p class="context-status">${escapeHtml(`${headlines.length} headline${headlines.length === 1 ? "" : "s"} loaded for ${symbol}.`)}</p>`
      : `<p class="context-status">${escapeHtml((context.summary || [])[0] || `No headlines loaded yet for ${symbol}.`)}</p>`;
    const headlineHtml = headlines.length
      ? `<div class="headline-list">${headlines.map(item => {
          const pub = item.publisher ? `<span class="hl-pub">${escapeHtml(item.publisher)}</span> ` : "";
          return item.url
            ? `<a href="${escapeHtml(item.url)}" target="_blank" rel="noopener">${pub}${escapeHtml(item.title || item)}</a>`
            : `<span>${pub}${escapeHtml(item.title || item)}</span>`;
        }).join("")}</div>`
      : "";
    return `
      ${statusLine}
      ${headlineHtml}
      <div class="source-grid">${sourceCards}</div>`;
  }

  async function fetchAndInjectNews(symbol) {
    if (!symbol || !/^https?:$/.test(location.protocol)) return;
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`/api/news?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(symbol)}&limit=8`);
      const json = await res.json();
      if (!json.ok || !json.articles?.length) return;
      // Convert Alpaca articles to the headline format renderMarketContext expects
      const newsItems = json.articles.map(a => ({
        title: a.headline,
        publisher: a.source,
        url: a.url,
        summary: a.summary,
        createdAt: a.createdAt
      }));
      // Re-render with live articles injected
      if (activeRenderedAnalysis) {
        activeRenderedAnalysis.news = newsItems;
        renderAnalysis(activeRenderedAnalysis);
        renderTradingViewWidgets(activeRenderedAnalysis.symbol, activeRenderedAnalysis.candles || [], activeRenderedAnalysis);
      }
    } catch (e) { /* silently skip if news unavailable */ }
  }



  function yahooRaw(field) {
    if (field == null) return null;
    if (typeof field === "object" && "raw" in field) return field.raw;
    return field;
  }

  function yahooFmt(field) {
    if (field == null) return null;
    if (typeof field === "object" && field.fmt) return field.fmt;
    const raw = yahooRaw(field);
    return raw == null ? null : String(raw);
  }

  function moneyFromYahoo(field) {
    const raw = Number(yahooRaw(field));
    if (Number.isFinite(raw)) return `$${compactNumber(raw)}`;
    return yahooFmt(field);
  }

  function pctFromYahoo(field) {
    const raw = Number(yahooRaw(field));
    if (!Number.isFinite(raw)) return null;
    return `${(raw * 100).toFixed(1)}%`;
  }

  function truncateText(text, max = 520) {
    const clean = String(text || "").replace(/\s+/g, " ").trim();
    if (clean.length <= max) return clean;
    return `${clean.slice(0, max).replace(/\s+\S*$/, "")}...`;
  }

  function parseYahooCompanyProfile(data) {
    const result = data?.quoteSummary?.result?.[0];
    if (!result || data?.quoteSummary?.error) throw new Error("Company profile unavailable");
    const asset = result.assetProfile || {};
    const financial = result.financialData || {};
    const price = result.price || {};
    const summary = result.summaryDetail || {};
    return {
      longName: price.longName || price.shortName || "",
      sector: asset.sector || "",
      industry: asset.industry || "",
      website: asset.website || "",
      summary: asset.longBusinessSummary || "",
      marketCap: moneyFromYahoo(price.marketCap || summary.marketCap),
      beta: yahooFmt(summary.beta),
      revenueGrowth: pctFromYahoo(financial.revenueGrowth),
      grossMargins: pctFromYahoo(financial.grossMargins),
      profitMargins: pctFromYahoo(financial.profitMargins),
      earningsGrowth: pctFromYahoo(financial.earningsGrowth),
      totalCash: moneyFromYahoo(financial.totalCash),
      totalDebt: moneyFromYahoo(financial.totalDebt),
      targetMeanPrice: yahooFmt(financial.targetMeanPrice),
      recommendationKey: financial.recommendationKey ? String(financial.recommendationKey).replace(/_/g, " ") : "",
      analystCount: yahooRaw(financial.numberOfAnalystOpinions),
      source: "Yahoo profile"
    };
  }
