  function buildCompanyRead(rawSymbol, analysis = {}, profile = null) {
    const symbol = cleanSymbol(rawSymbol);
    const builtIn = localCompanyProfiles[symbol] || null;
    const metrics = analysis.metrics || {};
    const rating = analysis.rating || "WAIT";
    const confidence = Number.isFinite(Number(analysis.confidence)) ? `${Math.round(Number(analysis.confidence))}/100` : "--";
    const support = metrics.support || "--";
    const resistance = metrics.resistance || "--";
    const rr = metrics.rr || "--";
    const technicalLine = rating === "LIVE"
      ? `The chart is live; the deeper read improves when candle data and profile data both load.`
      : `Current technical read is ${rating} with confidence ${confidence}; the setup needs price to respect ${support} and make progress through ${resistance}.`;

    if (cryptoDataMap[symbol]) {
      const cryptoBase = String(cryptoDataMap[symbol] || symbol).replace(/USDT$/, "");
      const cryptoProfile = cryptoAssetProfiles[symbol] || cryptoAssetProfiles[cryptoBase] || null;
      const assetName = cryptoProfile?.longName || symbol;
      return {
        title: "Asset / Future Read",
        source: cryptoProfile ? `Built-in ${symbol} crypto profile` : "Crypto asset profile",
        summary: cryptoProfile?.summary || `${assetName} is a crypto asset, not a company. The useful summary is token purpose, network usage, liquidity, supply schedule, exchange access, developer/community activity, and whether BTC/ETH market direction supports risk-taking.`,
        drivers: (cryptoProfile?.drivers || [
          `Adoption and real usage are the biggest future driver; confirm whether the network or token has growing volume, users, fees, or integrations.`,
          `Liquidity matters: stronger BTC/ETH trend and heavier exchange volume usually improve follow-through on crypto setups.`,
          `A clean break above ${resistance} with volume supports upside continuation; failure there can turn the move into a fade.`
        ]).concat([technicalLine]).slice(0, 4),
        risks: (cryptoProfile?.risks || [
          `Loss of ${support} weakens the near-term structure and can trigger fast liquidation-driven downside.`,
          `Token unlocks, exchange delistings, regulatory headlines, bridge/exploit risk, or thin liquidity can override the chart.`,
          `If the move is only social hype without volume confirmation, size should stay small or paper-only.`
        ]).slice(0, 4),
        verify: (cryptoProfile?.verify || [
          `Check tokenomics, unlock calendar, recent protocol updates, exchange volume, and BTC/ETH direction.`,
          `Use Ground News or a trusted crypto news feed for headline bias, then confirm the chart reaction.`,
          `Define entry, stop, target, and max loss before treating the signal as actionable.`
        ]).slice(0, 4)
      };
    }

    const companyName = profile?.longName || builtIn?.longName || symbol;
    const sectorLine = [profile?.sector || builtIn?.sector, profile?.industry || builtIn?.industry].filter(Boolean).join(" / ");
    const summary = profile?.summary
      ? truncateText(profile.summary)
      : builtIn?.summary || `${companyName} is being treated as a stock or ETF candidate. Use the chart levels above for trade timing, then verify the business through filings, earnings, sector trend, liquidity, and same-day news before building a bigger thesis.`;
    const growthLine = profile?.revenueGrowth || profile?.profitMargins || profile?.grossMargins
      ? `Growth/margins snapshot: revenue growth ${profile?.revenueGrowth || "not available"}, gross margin ${profile?.grossMargins || "not available"}, profit margin ${profile?.profitMargins || "not available"}.`
      : `Watch revenue growth, margins, free cash flow, and guidance to see whether the business story supports the chart.`;
    const balanceLine = profile?.totalCash || profile?.totalDebt
      ? `Balance-sheet check: cash ${profile?.totalCash || "not available"} versus debt ${profile?.totalDebt || "not available"}.`
      : `Balance-sheet quality matters if growth slows; check cash, debt, dilution, and financing needs.`;
    const analystLine = profile?.targetMeanPrice
      ? `Analyst mean target in the profile feed is ${profile.targetMeanPrice}${profile.analystCount ? ` from ${profile.analystCount} opinions` : ""}; use it as context, not as an entry trigger.`
      : `Analyst targets and estimate revisions are useful context, but the chart still decides timing.`;
    const hasCompanyProfile = Boolean(profile?.summary || builtIn);

    if (!hasCompanyProfile) {
      const mappedSector = sectorLine || "Company / Sector To Verify";
      return {
        title: "Company / Future Read",
        source: "Live profile needed",
        summary: `${companyName} company summary is not in the built-in offline profile pack yet. In this local static version, treat it as a tradable equity and build the company read around business model, revenue growth, margins, cash flow, balance sheet, management guidance, sector strength, and whether today's move is company-specific or market beta. Sector/industry: ${mappedSector}.`,
        drivers: [
          `${companyName}'s future read should focus on revenue growth, margin trend, free cash flow, balance-sheet strength, management guidance, and whether the company has a durable reason to keep gaining demand.`,
          `For an intraday setup, the business story only matters if it matches price action: buyers need to defend ${support}, push through ${resistance}, and do it with enough volume to prove institutions are involved.`,
          `For a longer hold, compare ${companyName} against direct competitors, sector ETFs, analyst estimate revisions, product cycle headlines, and earnings-call language.`,
          technicalLine
        ],
        risks: [
          `Chart risk: a clean loss of ${support} weakens the thesis; rejection near ${resistance} can turn the idea into a range trade or failed breakout.`,
          `Business risk: earnings misses, guidance cuts, slowing demand, margin compression, dilution, debt pressure, lawsuits, regulation, or weak sector demand can break the story.`,
          `Information risk: if you cannot explain what the company does, what catalyst is moving it, and why the level matters today, keep it paper-only or reduce size.`
        ],
        verify: [
          `Open the latest earnings release, 10-Q/10-K, investor presentation, and same-day company headlines before treating this as more than a chart trade.`,
          `Check sector strength, SPY/QQQ direction, relative volume, short interest if relevant, and whether the move is company-specific or just index flow.`,
          `Use Ground News for headline bias, but use filings, earnings, and the chart reaction to decide whether the story has tradeable confirmation.`
        ]
      };
    }

    return {
      title: "Company / Future Read",
      source: profile?.source || builtIn?.source || "Local company read",
      summary: sectorLine ? `${summary} Sector/industry: ${sectorLine}.` : summary,
      drivers: (builtIn?.drivers || [
        sectorLine ? `${companyName}'s future depends on execution in ${sectorLine}, including demand, pricing power, competition, and product cycle strength.` : `${companyName}'s future read needs company filings, earnings calls, guidance, and sector trend confirmation.`,
        growthLine,
        analystLine,
        technicalLine
      ]).concat(builtIn ? [technicalLine] : []).slice(0, 4),
      risks: (builtIn?.risks || [
        balanceLine,
        `Chart risk: a clean loss of ${support} weakens the thesis; rejection near ${resistance} can turn the setup into a range trade.`,
        `Business risk: earnings misses, guidance cuts, dilution, lawsuits, regulation, or weaker sector demand can break the story even if the chart looked strong.`
      ]).concat(builtIn ? [`Chart risk: a clean loss of ${support} weakens the thesis; rejection near ${resistance} can turn the setup into a range trade.`] : []).slice(0, 4),
      verify: (builtIn?.verify || [
        `Read the latest earnings release, 10-Q/10-K, guidance, and any same-day company news before making a bigger decision.`,
        `Compare the ticker against its sector and nearest competitors so you know whether the move is company-specific or just market beta.`,
        `For trades, use the stop/target/R:R here. For investing, build a separate multi-month thesis instead of relying on one signal.`
      ]).slice(0, 4)
    };
  }

  async function fetchCompanyRead(rawSymbol, analysis = {}) {
    const symbol = cleanSymbol(rawSymbol);
    if (cryptoDataMap[symbol]) return buildCompanyRead(symbol, analysis);
    const modules = "assetProfile,financialData,defaultKeyStatistics,summaryDetail,recommendationTrend,earningsTrend,price";
    const url = `https://query1.finance.yahoo.com/v10/finance/quoteSummary/${encodeURIComponent(symbol)}?modules=${modules}`;
    const data = await fetchJsonWithFallback(url, "Yahoo profile");
    return buildCompanyRead(symbol, analysis, parseYahooCompanyProfile(data));
  }

  function resetElement(el) {
    el.innerHTML = "";
    return el;
  }

  function injectTradingViewScript(container, src, config) {
    const script = document.createElement("script");
    script.type = "text/javascript";
    script.src = src;
    script.async = true;
    script.innerHTML = JSON.stringify(config, null, 2);
    container.appendChild(script);
  }

  function renderTradingViewWidgets(rawSymbol, candles = [], data = null) {
    const symbol = tradingViewSymbol(rawSymbol);
    document.querySelectorAll(".tvSymbolLabel").forEach(el => el.textContent = symbol);
    document.querySelectorAll(".tvOverview").forEach(el => {
      renderNativeChart(resetElement(el), rawSymbol, candles, data);
    });
    document.querySelectorAll(".tvTechnical").forEach(el => {
      renderNativeTechnical(resetElement(el), data);
    });
  }

  function chartPath(candles, width = 680, height = 230) {
    if (!candles.length) return { line: "", area: "", min: 0, max: 0 };
    const closes = candles.map(c => Number(c.close)).filter(Number.isFinite);
    const min = Math.min(...closes);
    const max = Math.max(...closes);
    const span = max - min || Math.max(max * 0.01, 1);
    const pad = 14;
    const points = closes.map((close, index) => {
      const x = pad + (index / Math.max(closes.length - 1, 1)) * (width - pad * 2);
      const y = pad + (1 - ((close - min) / span)) * (height - pad * 2);
      return [x, y];
    });
    const line = points.map(([x, y]) => `${x.toFixed(1)},${y.toFixed(1)}`).join(" ");
    const area = `M${points[0][0].toFixed(1)},${height - pad} L${points.map(([x, y]) => `${x.toFixed(1)},${y.toFixed(1)}`).join(" L")} L${points[points.length - 1][0].toFixed(1)},${height - pad} Z`;
    return { line, area, min, max };
  }

  function renderNativeChart(container, rawSymbol, candles = [], data = null) {
    const recent = candles.slice(-90);
    const tvFrame = `<iframe class="tradingview-frame tv-live-frame" src="${tradingViewEmbedUrl(rawSymbol)}" title="TradingView live chart for ${escapeHtml(rawSymbol)}"></iframe>`;
    const sources = `${sourceDeckHtml(rawSymbol)}<p class="source-note">TradingView is embedded directly in this HTML. Yahoo/Binance candles power the local chart when the browser allows them; Yahoo Finance, CNBC, MarketWatch, Nasdaq, and Ground News open as verification sources.</p>`;
    if (!recent.length) {
      container.innerHTML = `<div class="native-widget" style="min-height:0;padding-bottom:0">
        ${sources}
      </div>
      ${tvFrame}
      <div class="native-empty" style="min-height:74px;padding:10px 14px">TradingView is the primary live visual. Candle-analysis numbers will fill in when Yahoo/proxy or crypto candle data is reachable.</div>`;
      return;
    }
    const chart = chartPath(recent);
    const last = recent[recent.length - 1]?.close;
    const first = recent[0]?.close || last;
    const move = first ? ((last - first) / first) * 100 : 0;
    const color = move >= 0 ? "var(--dto-green)" : "var(--dto-red)";
    container.innerHTML = `<div class="native-widget">
      <svg class="native-chart" viewBox="0 0 680 230" preserveAspectRatio="none" role="img" aria-label="Local candle close chart for ${rawSymbol}">
        <path d="${chart.area}" fill="${move >= 0 ? "rgba(0,224,138,0.12)" : "rgba(255,61,113,0.12)"}"></path>
        <polyline points="${chart.line}" fill="none" stroke="${color}" stroke-width="3" vector-effect="non-scaling-stroke"></polyline>
        <line x1="0" x2="680" y1="115" y2="115" stroke="rgba(220,231,245,0.12)" stroke-dasharray="4 6"></line>
      </svg>
      <div class="chart-stats">
        <div class="chart-stat"><span>Last</span><strong>${fmtPrice(last)}</strong></div>
        <div class="chart-stat"><span>Range High</span><strong>${fmtPrice(chart.max)}</strong></div>
        <div class="chart-stat"><span>Range Move</span><strong style="color:${color}">${move >= 0 ? "+" : ""}${move.toFixed(2)}%</strong></div>
      </div>
      ${sources}
    </div>
    ${tvFrame}`;
  }

  function renderNativeTechnical(container, data = null) {
    const score = Number(data?.confidence ?? 50);
    const rating = data?.rating || "WAIT";
    const metrics = data?.metrics || {};
    const rrNum = numberFromDisplay(metrics.rr);
    const rsiNum = numberFromDisplay(metrics.rsi);
    const support = metrics.support || "--";
    const resistance = metrics.resistance || "--";
    const price = metrics.price || "--";
    const ringColor = rating === "BUY" ? "var(--dto-green)" : rating === "SELL" ? "var(--dto-red)" : "var(--dto-gold)";
    const ratingRead = rating === "BUY"
      ? `Bias is bullish, but the better entry is still near support or after a clean break above ${resistance}.`
      : rating === "SELL"
        ? `Bias is bearish, so failed reclaims and rejection near resistance matter more than chasing lows.`
        : `Bias is neutral/check. Wait for a decisive move through ${resistance} or a reclaim/failure around ${support}.`;
    const rrRead = rrNum === null
      ? `R:R is not available yet because one of entry, stop, or target is missing.`
      : rrNum >= 2
        ? `${rrNum.toFixed(2)}R clears the planning bar. Now confirm volume and catalyst before sizing.`
        : `${rrNum.toFixed(2)}R is below the 2R planning bar, so the trade needs a tighter stop, better target, or no entry.`;
    const rsiRead = rsiNum === null
      ? `RSI is not loaded yet. Use the chart slope, candle closes, and volume to judge momentum.`
      : rsiNum >= 70
        ? `RSI near ${Math.round(rsiNum)} is stretched. Momentum can continue, but late entries are easier to trap.`
        : rsiNum <= 35
          ? `RSI near ${Math.round(rsiNum)} is washed out. Look for reversal proof before shorting lows or buying too early.`
          : `RSI near ${Math.round(rsiNum)} is balanced enough to let levels and volume decide.`;
    const planRead = `Trade map: current price ${price}; support ${support}; resistance ${resistance}. A good plan defines the invalidation first, then only takes the setup if reward justifies the risk.`;
    container.innerHTML = `<div class="native-widget rating-dial">
      <div class="rating-main">
        <div>
          <div class="label">Native Technical Rating</div>
          <strong style="color:${ringColor}">${rating}</strong>
        </div>
        <div class="score-ring" style="--score:${score}%;--dto-cyan:${ringColor}"><span>${Number.isFinite(score) ? Math.round(score) : "--"}</span></div>
      </div>
      <div class="tech-grid">
        <div class="tech-stat"><span>Support</span><strong>${metrics.support || "--"}</strong></div>
        <div class="tech-stat"><span>Resistance</span><strong>${metrics.resistance || "--"}</strong></div>
        <div class="tech-stat"><span>R:R</span><strong>${metrics.rr || "--"}</strong></div>
      </div>
      <div class="tech-line"><label><span>Trend score</span><span>${Number.isFinite(score) ? Math.round(score) + "/100" : "--"}</span></label><div class="tech-track"><div class="tech-fill" style="width:${Number.isFinite(score) ? score : 50}%;background:${ringColor}"></div></div></div>
      <div class="tech-line"><label><span>RSI</span><span>${metrics.rsi || "--"}</span></label><div class="tech-track"><div class="tech-fill" style="width:${Math.max(5, Math.min(95, Number(metrics.rsi) || 50))}%;background:var(--dto-gold)"></div></div></div>
      <div class="tech-analysis">
        <div class="tech-read"><span>Directional Read</span><p>${escapeHtml(ratingRead)}</p></div>
        <div class="tech-read"><span>Risk / Reward</span><p>${escapeHtml(rrRead)}</p></div>
        <div class="tech-read"><span>Momentum</span><p>${escapeHtml(rsiRead)}</p></div>
        <div class="tech-read"><span>Execution Map</span><p>${escapeHtml(planRead)}</p></div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }

  function setText(id, value) {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (el) el.textContent = value;
    return el;
  }

  function localActiveUser() {
    const users = readJson("dtoUsers", []);
    const activeId = localStorage.getItem("dtoActiveUser");
    return users.find(user => user.id === activeId) || null;
  }

  function compactMeta(value, fallback = "--") {
    if (value === null || value === undefined || value === "") return fallback;
    const numberValue = Number(value);
    if (Number.isFinite(numberValue)) return Math.abs(numberValue) >= 10 ? numberValue.toFixed(0) : numberValue.toFixed(2);
    return String(value);
  }

  const MARKET_PULSE_BASE_SYMBOLS = ["NVDA", "TSLA", "AMD", "AAPL", "MSFT", "META", "AMZN", "GOOGL", "INTC", "COIN", "MSTR", "SPY", "QQQ", "BTC", "ETH", "SOL"];

  function pulseSymbols() {
    const setup = readJson("dtoLastSetup", null) || readJson("dtoSetupPacket", null);
    const saved = readJson("dtoSetupPackets", []);
    const watchlist = readJson("watchlist", []);
    const scanner = readJson("dtoScannerWatchlist", []);
    const raw = [
      setup?.symbol,
      ...saved.slice(0, 6).map(item => item?.symbol),
      ...watchlist.slice(0, 8).map(item => typeof item === "string" ? item : item?.symbol || item?.ticker || item?.name),
      ...scanner.slice(0, 8).map(item => typeof item === "string" ? item : item?.symbol),
      ...MARKET_PULSE_BASE_SYMBOLS
    ];
    return [...new Set(raw.map(cleanSymbol).filter(Boolean))].slice(0, 18);
  }

  function pulseFromCandles(symbol, candles) {
    const clean = cleanSymbol(symbol);
    const recent = candles.slice(-24);
    if (recent.length < 2) throw new Error("Not enough candles");
    const first = recent[0];
    const last = recent[recent.length - 1];
    const high = Math.max(...recent.map(candle => Number(candle.high)).filter(Number.isFinite));
    const low = Math.min(...recent.map(candle => Number(candle.low)).filter(Number.isFinite));
    const move = first.close ? ((last.close - first.close) / first.close) * 100 : 0;
    const volatility = last.close ? ((high - low) / last.close) * 100 : 0;
    const direction = move >= 0 ? "up" : "down";
    return {
      symbol: clean,
      price: last.close,
      move,
      volatility,
      direction,
      source: candles.source || "candles",
      delayed: Boolean(candles.delayed)
    };
  }

  function renderPulseCard(id, item, label) {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (!el) return;
    if (!item) {
      el.href = "market_workbench.html";
      el.innerHTML = `<span>${escapeHtml(label)}</span><strong>--</strong><small>No candle result yet</small>`;
      return;
    }
    const moveText = `${item.move >= 0 ? "+" : ""}${item.move.toFixed(2)}%`;
    const volText = `${item.volatility.toFixed(2)}% range`;
    const cls = item.move >= 0 ? "pulse-up" : "pulse-down";
    el.href = signalDashboardUrl({ symbol: item.symbol });
    el.innerHTML = `<span>${escapeHtml(label)}</span><strong>${escapeHtml(item.symbol)}</strong><small><b class="${cls}">${moveText}</b> / ${volText}</small>`;
  }

  function renderMarketPulse(results, statusText = "") {
    const usable = (results || []).filter(item => item && Number.isFinite(item.move) && Number.isFinite(item.volatility));
    const status = document.getElementById("pulseStatus");
    if (status) {
      const delayedCount = usable.filter(item => item.delayed).length;
      status.textContent = statusText || (usable.length
        ? `${usable.length} symbols scanned${delayedCount ? ` / ${delayedCount} delayed fallback` : ""}.`
        : "No mover feed reached yet. Try refresh after deploy/backend is live.");
    }
    const best = usable.length ? [...usable].sort((a, b) => b.move - a.move)[0] : null;
    const worst = usable.length ? [...usable].sort((a, b) => a.move - b.move)[0] : null;
    const volatile = usable.length ? [...usable].sort((a, b) => b.volatility - a.volatility)[0] : null;
    renderPulseCard("pulseBest", best, "Best Performer");
    renderPulseCard("pulseWorst", worst, "Worst Performer");
    renderPulseCard("pulseVolatile", volatile, "Highest Volatility");
    const strip = document.getElementById("pulseStrip");
    if (strip) {
      strip.innerHTML = usable.length
        ? [...usable].sort((a, b) => Math.abs(b.move) - Math.abs(a.move)).slice(0, 10).map(item => {
            const cls = item.move >= 0 ? "pulse-up" : "pulse-down";
            return `<a class="pulse-chip" href="${escapeHtml(signalDashboardUrl({ symbol: item.symbol }))}">${escapeHtml(item.symbol)} <span class="${cls}">${item.move >= 0 ? "+" : ""}${item.move.toFixed(1)}%</span></a>`;
          }).join("")
        : `<span class="pulse-chip">Feed waiting</span><span class="pulse-chip">Deploy backend for best coverage</span>`;
    }
  }

  async function mapLimit(items, limit, worker) {
    const results = [];
    let index = 0;
    async function run() {
      while (index < items.length) {
        const currentIndex = index;
        index += 1;
        try {
          results[currentIndex] = await worker(items[currentIndex], currentIndex);
        } catch (error) {
          results[currentIndex] = null;
        }
      }
    }
    await Promise.all(Array.from({ length: Math.min(limit, items.length) }, run));
    return results;
  }

  async function refreshMarketPulse(force = false) {
    const cached = readJson("dtoMarketPulse", null);
    const cacheAge = cached?.createdAt ? Date.now() - new Date(cached.createdAt).getTime() : Infinity;
    if (cached?.results?.length) renderMarketPulse(cached.results, force ? "Refreshing market pulse..." : "");
    if (!force && cached?.results?.length && cacheAge < 8 * 60 * 1000) return;
    const symbols = pulseSymbols();
    renderMarketPulse(cached?.results || [], `Scanning ${symbols.length} liquid names...`);
    const results = (await mapLimit(symbols, 4, async symbol => pulseFromCandles(symbol, await fetchCandles(symbol)))).filter(Boolean);
    if (results.length) {
      localStorage.setItem("dtoMarketPulse", JSON.stringify({ createdAt: new Date().toISOString(), results }));
      renderMarketPulse(results);
    } else {
      renderMarketPulse(cached?.results || [], "Market pulse feed is blocked in this browser session.");
    }
  }

  function updateHeroWorkflow({ setup, watchlist, paper, grade }) {
    const positions = Array.isArray(paper?.positions) ? paper.positions : [];
    const hasSetup = Boolean(setup?.symbol);
    const hasLevels = Boolean(Number(setup?.entry) && Number(setup?.stop) && Number(setup?.target));
    const hasPlan = hasSetup && (Number(setup?.rr) >= 2 || String(setup?.thesis || "").length > 80 || grade?.score >= 68);
    const hasPaper = positions.length > 0 || (Array.isArray(paper?.log) && paper.log.length > 0);
    const steps = [
      { key: "scan", label: "Scan", href: "market_workbench.html", done: watchlist.length > 0 || hasSetup, active: !hasSetup },
      { key: "analyze", label: "Analyze", done: hasSetup, active: hasSetup && !hasLevels },
      { key: "plan", label: "Plan", href: "trade_planner.html", done: hasPlan, active: hasLevels && !hasPlan },
      { key: "size", label: "Size", href: "execution_workbench.html", done: hasLevels && Number(setup?.rr) >= 2, active: hasPlan && Number(setup?.rr) < 2 },
      { key: "paper", label: "Paper", href: "practice_workbench.html", done: hasPaper, active: hasPlan && Number(setup?.rr) >= 2 && !hasPaper }
    ];
    const flow = document.getElementById("heroWorkflow");
    if (!flow) return;
    flow.innerHTML = steps.map(step => {
      const cls = step.done ? "is-done" : step.active ? "is-active" : "";
      if (step.key === "analyze") {
        return `<button class="command-step ${cls}" type="button" data-flow-step="analyze">${escapeHtml(step.label)}</button>`;
      }
      const href = setup?.symbol ? workflowUrl(step.href, setup) : step.href;
      return `<a class="command-step ${cls}" href="${escapeHtml(href)}" data-flow-step="${escapeHtml(step.key)}">${escapeHtml(step.label)}</a>`;
    }).join("");
  }

  function updateSnapshot() {
    const trades = readJson("trades", []);
    const watchlist = readJson("watchlist", []);
    const stats = window.DTO?.missionStats ? window.DTO.missionStats() : {};
    const setup = stats.setup || readJson("dtoSetupPacket", null) || readJson("dtoLastSetup", null);
    const grade = stats.grade || (setup && window.DTO?.gradeSetup ? window.DTO.gradeSetup(setup) : null);
    const savedSetups = stats.savedSetups || readJson("dtoSetupPackets", []);
    const paper = stats.paper || readJson("dtoPaperTradingAccount", { startingCash: 100000, cash: 100000, positions: [], log: [], realized: 0, quotes: {} });
    const positions = Array.isArray(paper.positions) ? paper.positions : [];
    const history = stats.history || window.DTO?.tradeHistory?.() || trades;
    const pnl = trades.reduce((sum, trade) => sum + Number(trade.pnl || 0), 0);
    const closed = history.filter(trade => Number.isFinite(Number(trade.pnl)));
    const wins = closed.filter(trade => Number(trade.pnl) > 0).length;
    const winRate = closed.length ? Math.round((wins / closed.length) * 100) : 0;
    const paperOpenPnl = Number(stats.openPnl || 0);
    const paperRealized = Number(paper.realized || 0);
    const paperTotal = paperOpenPnl + paperRealized;
    setText("tradeCount", trades.length);
    setText("watchCount", watchlist.length);
    const pnlEl = document.getElementById("netPnl");
    if (pnlEl) {
      pnlEl.textContent = formatMoney(pnl);
      pnlEl.style.color = pnl < 0 ? "var(--dto-red)" : "var(--dto-green)";
    }
    const user = window.DTO?.activeUser ? window.DTO.activeUser() : localActiveUser();
    const mode = window.DTO?.profileMode ? window.DTO.profileMode(user) : String(user?.experience || "beginner");
    const displayUser = user ? (user.username || user.name || "Trader") : "Guest";
    setText("heroProfileMode", `${displayUser} / ${String(mode || "beginner").toUpperCase()}`);
    if (setup?.symbol) {
      const rrText = Number.isFinite(Number(setup.rr)) ? `${Number(setup.rr).toFixed(2)}R` : "R:R --";
      setText("heroActiveSetup", cleanSymbol(setup.symbol));
      setText("heroSetupMeta", `${String(setup.rating || "CHECK").toUpperCase()} / ${rrText} / ${String(setup.assetType || "asset").toUpperCase()}`);
      if (!Number(setup.entry) || !Number(setup.stop) || !Number(setup.target)) {
        setText("heroNextAction", `${cleanSymbol(setup.symbol)}: mark entry, stop, target, support, and resistance.`);
        setText("heroCommandNote", "Open Trade Builder or the chart, tighten the levels, then save the setup packet again.");
      } else if (Number(setup.rr) < 2) {
        setText("heroNextAction", `${cleanSymbol(setup.symbol)}: improve the setup before sizing risk.`);
        setText("heroCommandNote", `Current reward/risk is ${Number(setup.rr).toFixed(2)}R. Build a cleaner target, tighter invalidation, or keep it paper-only.`);
      } else if (String(setup.rating || "").toUpperCase().match(/HOLD|CHECK|WAIT/)) {
        setText("heroNextAction", `${cleanSymbol(setup.symbol)}: confirm catalyst and chart direction.`);
        setText("heroCommandNote", "The packet has levels, but the rating still needs confirmation before any serious sizing.");
      } else {
        setText("heroNextAction", `${cleanSymbol(setup.symbol)} is ready to size and paper trade.`);
        setText("heroCommandNote", "Use Open in Risk to verify position size, then paper trade and journal the outcome.");
      }
    } else {
      setText("heroActiveSetup", "None");
      setText("heroSetupMeta", "Analyze a symbol to create the shared setup packet.");
      setText("heroNextAction", "Analyze a symbol to start the workflow.");
      setText("heroCommandNote", "Use the signal box on the right, then save the setup packet so every tool stays linked.");
    }
    setText("heroSavedSetups", savedSetups.length);
    setText("heroSavedMeta", savedSetups.length ? `${cleanSymbol(savedSetups[0]?.symbol || "")} is the latest saved plan.` : "Practice plans stored in this browser.");
    const paperEl = setText("heroPaperPnl", formatMoney(paperTotal));
    if (paperEl) paperEl.style.color = paperTotal < 0 ? "var(--dto-red)" : "var(--dto-green)";
    setText("heroPaperMeta", `${positions.length} open / realized ${formatMoney(paperRealized)}.`);
    setText("heroJournalEdge", `${winRate}%`);
    setText("heroJournalMeta", closed.length ? `${closed.length} closed trades / net ${formatMoney(stats.net || pnl)}.` : "No closed trades logged yet.");
    updateHeroWorkflow({ setup, watchlist, paper, grade });
  }

  function updateClock() {
    const et = new Date(new Date().toLocaleString("en-US", { timeZone: "America/New_York" }));
    const pad = value => String(value).padStart(2, "0");
    const mins = et.getHours() * 60 + et.getMinutes();
    const day = et.getDay();
    document.getElementById("clock").textContent = `${pad(et.getHours())}:${pad(et.getMinutes())} ET`;
    let state = "Closed";
    if (day > 0 && day < 6 && mins >= 240 && mins < 570) state = "Pre-market";
    if (day > 0 && day < 6 && mins >= 570 && mins < 960) state = "Market open";
    if (day > 0 && day < 6 && mins >= 960 && mins < 1200) state = "After-hours";
    document.getElementById("marketState").textContent = state;
  }

  function widgetOnlyAnalysis(rawSymbol) {
    const symbol = cleanSymbol(rawSymbol);
    const fallback = {
      symbol,
      name: "TradingView chart is live. Static hosts can show the chart immediately; automatic candle calculations need a reachable data feed.",
      rating: "CHECK",
      confidence: 50,
      price: null,
      changePercent: null,
      volume: null,
      metrics: {
        price: "Chart",
        support: "Set Level",
        resistance: "Set Level",
        stop: "Builder",
        target: "Builder",
        top: "Set Level",
        bottom: "Set Level",
        rr: "--",
        rsi: "--",
        news: "Ground News",
        risk: "Use Calculator"
      },
      rationale: [
        "TradingView loads the visual chart even when Yahoo/proxy candle data is blocked by the browser or unavailable on static hosting.",
        "Use the chart to mark support, resistance, stop, and target, then send the setup into Trade Builder or Risk Calculator.",
        "Automatic levels appear when a browser candle feed or private backend is reachable; otherwise this stays in chart-first planning mode."
      ],
      news: ["Use Ground News to compare coverage before reacting to market-moving headlines."],
      groundNews: {
        query: `${symbol} market news`,
        url: "https://ground.news/search"
      },
      source: "TradingView live widgets"
    };
    fallback.company = buildCompanyRead(symbol, fallback);
    return fallback;
  }

  let activeRenderedAnalysis = null;

  function numberFromDisplay(value) {
    const n = Number(String(value ?? "").replace(/[^0-9.-]/g, ""));
    return Number.isFinite(n) ? n : null;
  }

  function roundSetupNumber(value) {
    const n = Number(value);
    if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return null;
    return Number(n.toFixed(n >= 1 ? 4 : 8));
  }

  function setupFromAnalysis(data) {
    const metrics = data?.metrics || {};
    const raw = data?.raw || {};
    const entry = roundSetupNumber(raw.price ?? numberFromDisplay(metrics.price));
    const stop = roundSetupNumber(raw.stop ?? numberFromDisplay(metrics.stop || metrics.bottom));
    const target = roundSetupNumber(raw.target ?? numberFromDisplay(metrics.target || metrics.top));
    const support = roundSetupNumber(raw.support ?? numberFromDisplay(metrics.support));
    const resistance = roundSetupNumber(raw.resistance ?? numberFromDisplay(metrics.resistance));
    const rating = data?.rating || "WAIT";
    const side = rating.includes("SELL") || (entry && stop && stop > entry) ? "short" : "long";
    const thesisParts = [
      data?.name,
      ...(data?.rationale || []).slice(0, 3),
      data?.company?.summary
    ].filter(Boolean);
    return {
      symbol: cleanSymbol(data?.symbol || "AAPL"),
      assetType: cryptoDataMap[cleanSymbol(data?.symbol || "AAPL")] ? "crypto" : "stock",
      side,
      rating,
      confidence: data?.confidence ?? null,
      timeframe: "intraday",
      entry,
      stop,
      target,
      support,
      resistance,
      rr: raw.rr ?? numberFromDisplay(metrics.rr),
      rsi: raw.rsi ?? numberFromDisplay(metrics.rsi),
      catalysts: data?.news?.slice?.(0, 3)?.map(item => typeof item === "string" ? item : item.title) || [],
      riskNotes: data?.company?.risks?.slice?.(0, 3) || [],
      sourcePage: "index.html",
      source: data?.source || "Command Center",
      thesis: thesisParts.join(" "),
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
    };
  }

  function localSetupGrade(setup) {
    const n = value => {
      const parsed = Number(value);
      return Number.isFinite(parsed) ? parsed : null;
    };
    const rr = n(setup.rr);
    const conf = n(setup.confidence);
    const entry = n(setup.entry);
    const stop = n(setup.stop);
    const target = n(setup.target);
    const support = n(setup.support);
    const resistance = n(setup.resistance);
    const side = String(setup.side || "long").toLowerCase();
    const rating = String(setup.rating || "CHECK").toUpperCase();
    const notes = [];
    const warnings = [];
    let score = 45;

    if (rating.includes("BUY") || rating.includes("SELL")) {
      score += 12;
      notes.push(`${rating} signal is directional, so it is ready to plan but not auto-enter.`);
    } else {
      score -= 4;
      warnings.push(`${rating} rating needs extra confirmation before execution.`);
    }

    if (rr !== null && rr >= 2) {
      score += 20;
      notes.push(`Reward/risk is ${rr.toFixed(2)}R, which clears the 2R planning bar.`);
    } else if (rr !== null) {
      score -= 18;
      warnings.push(`Reward/risk is only ${rr.toFixed(2)}R. Improve target, tighten stop, or skip.`);
    } else {
      warnings.push("Reward/risk is missing until entry, stop, and target are clear.");
    }

    if (entry !== null && stop !== null && target !== null && entry !== stop && entry !== target) {
      score += 14;
      const targetWrongWay = side === "long" ? target <= entry : target >= entry;
      const stopWrongWay = side === "long" ? stop >= entry : stop <= entry;
      if (targetWrongWay) {
        score -= 18;
        warnings.push("Target is on the wrong side of entry for this trade direction.");
      }
      if (stopWrongWay) {
        score -= 18;
        warnings.push("Stop is on the wrong side of entry for this trade direction.");
      }
    } else {
      score -= 12;
      warnings.push("Entry, stop, or target is missing, so the setup is not execution-ready.");
    }

    if (support !== null && resistance !== null && entry !== null) {
      score += 8;
      const nearResistance = resistance > 0 && Math.abs(resistance - entry) / Math.max(Math.abs(entry), 1) < 0.007;
      const nearSupport = support > 0 && Math.abs(entry - support) / Math.max(Math.abs(entry), 1) < 0.007;
      if (side === "long" && nearResistance) warnings.push("Long setup is close to resistance, so breakout proof matters.");
      if (side === "short" && nearSupport) warnings.push("Short setup is close to support, so downside may be crowded.");
      if (nearSupport || nearResistance) score -= 4;
    } else {
      warnings.push("Support/resistance map is incomplete.");
    }

    if (conf !== null && conf >= 70) score += 9;
    if (conf !== null && conf < 55) {
      score -= 8;
      warnings.push("Confidence is below 55, so keep it paper-only until structure improves.");
    }
    if ((setup.thesis || "").length > 100) score += 5;
    if ((setup.catalysts || []).length) score += 4;
    else warnings.push("No catalyst is attached yet; check news, earnings, macro, and sector/crypto beta.");

    score = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Math.round(score)));
    const label = score >= 80 ? "A Setup" : score >= 68 ? "B Setup" : score >= 55 ? "C Setup" : "Paper Only";
    const primary = warnings[0] || notes[0] || "Review trend, levels, risk/reward, catalyst quality, and liquidity before sizing.";
    return {
      score,
      label,
      notes,
      warnings,
      setup,
      modeText: {
        beginner: `${label}: ${primary}`,
        pro: `${label}. RR ${rr === null ? "--" : rr.toFixed(2)}R, confidence ${conf === null ? "--" : Math.round(conf)}, asset ${setup.assetType || "asset"}.`,
        expert: `Score ${score}/100 from rating, RR, levels, catalyst, and risk structure.`
      }
    };
  }

  function safeGradeAnalysis(data) {
    let setup;
    try {
      setup = setupFromAnalysis(data);
      const dtoGrade = window.DTO?.gradeSetup?.(setup);
      if (dtoGrade && Number.isFinite(Number(dtoGrade.score))) return dtoGrade;
    } catch (error) {
      if (!setup) setup = {
        symbol: cleanSymbol(data?.symbol || "AAPL"),
        assetType: cryptoDataMap[cleanSymbol(data?.symbol || "AAPL")] ? "crypto" : "stock",
        rating: data?.rating || "CHECK"
      };
    }
    return localSetupGrade(setup || setupFromAnalysis(data));
  }

  function writeLastSetup(setup) {
    if (window.DTO) setup = window.DTO.saveSetup(setup);
    else localStorage.setItem("dtoLastSetup", JSON.stringify(setup));
    renderProductionPath(setup);
    if (window.DTO) window.DTO.renderMissionControl();
    try { updateSnapshot(); } catch (error) {}
    refreshSignalLinks(setup);
    return setup;
  }

  function saveVisibleSetup() {
    const setup = writeLastSetup(setupFromAnalysis(activeRenderedAnalysis || widgetOnlyAnalysis(document.getElementById("assetInput").value)));
    const note = document.getElementById("liveStatus");
    if (note) note.textContent = `${setup.symbol} setup saved into the Production Path.`;
    return setup;
  }

  function setupUrlParams(setup) {
    const params = new URLSearchParams();
    ["symbol", "side", "rating", "entry", "stop", "target", "support", "resistance", "rr"].forEach(key => {
      if (setup[key] !== null && setup[key] !== undefined && setup[key] !== "--") params.set(key, setup[key]);
    });
    if (setup.thesis) params.set("thesis", setup.thesis.slice(0, 700));
    return params.toString();
  }

  function workflowUrl(page, setup = readJson("dtoLastSetup", null)) {
    if (!setup) setup = saveVisibleSetup();
    return `${page}?${setupUrlParams(setup)}`;
  }

  function signalDashboardUrl(setup = readJson("dtoLastSetup", null)) {
    if (!setup && activeRenderedAnalysis) setup = setupFromAnalysis(activeRenderedAnalysis);
    const inputSymbol = cleanSymbol(document.getElementById("assetInput")?.value || "");
    if ((!setup || !setup.symbol) && inputSymbol) setup = { symbol: inputSymbol };
    return setup?.symbol ? `signal_dashboard.html?${setupUrlParams(setup)}` : "signal_dashboard.html";
  }

  function refreshSignalLinks(setup = readJson("dtoLastSetup", null)) {
    const url = signalDashboardUrl(setup);
    document.querySelectorAll("[data-signal-link]").forEach(link => {
      link.href = url;
    });
  }

  function openWorkflow(page) {
    const setup = saveVisibleSetup();
    location.href = workflowUrl(page, setup);
  }

  function renderProductionPath(setup = readJson("dtoLastSetup", null)) {
    const el = document.getElementById("productionPath");
    if (!el) return;
    const hasSetup = setup && setup.symbol;
    const symbol = hasSetup ? escapeHtml(setup.symbol) : "No setup";
    const rating = hasSetup ? escapeHtml(setup.rating || "WAIT") : "Search first";
    const entry = hasSetup && setup.entry ? fmtPrice(setup.entry) : "--";
    const stop = hasSetup && setup.stop ? fmtPrice(setup.stop) : "--";
    const target = hasSetup && setup.target ? fmtPrice(setup.target) : "--";
    const rr = hasSetup && setup.rr ? `${Number(setup.rr).toFixed(2)}R` : "--";
    const marketUrl = hasSetup ? workflowUrl("market_workbench.html", setup) : "market_workbench.html";
    const riskUrl = hasSetup ? workflowUrl("execution_workbench.html", setup) : "execution_workbench.html";
    const strategyUrl = hasSetup ? workflowUrl("trade_planner.html", setup) : "trade_planner.html";
    const paperUrl = hasSetup ? workflowUrl("practice_workbench.html", setup) : "practice_workbench.html";
    const reviewUrl = hasSetup ? workflowUrl("review_workbench.html", setup) : "review_workbench.html";
    const signalUrl = hasSetup ? signalDashboardUrl(setup) : "signal_dashboard.html";
    el.innerHTML = `
      <div class="op">
        <strong>1. Market Intelligence</strong>
        <span>Scan watchlists, context, catalysts, and alerts before choosing the setup.</span>
        <div class="op-data">${symbol} / ${rating}</div>
        <div class="op-actions"><a href="${escapeHtml(marketUrl)}">Open Market Desk</a><a data-signal-link href="${escapeHtml(signalUrl)}">Signals</a></div>
      </div>
      <div class="op">
        <strong>2. Trade Planner</strong>
        <span>Load the setup into guided strategy thinking before forcing a trade.</span>
        <div class="op-data">Entry ${escapeHtml(entry)} / R:R ${escapeHtml(rr)}</div>
        <div class="op-actions"><a href="${escapeHtml(strategyUrl)}">Plan Trade</a><button type="button" onclick="saveVisibleSetup()">Save Current</button></div>
      </div>
      <div class="op">
        <strong>3. Execution Desk</strong>
        <span>Prefill entry, stop, target, side, and symbol for risk sizing and hedge planning.</span>
        <div class="op-data">Stop ${escapeHtml(stop)} / Target ${escapeHtml(target)}</div>
        <div class="op-actions"><a href="${escapeHtml(riskUrl)}">Size Risk</a><a href="broker_execution_plan.html">Broker Plan</a></div>
      </div>
      <div class="op">
        <strong>4. Practice + Review</strong>
        <span>Paper trade, replay, journal, and improve, or connect directly to Alpaca for live execution.</span>
        <div class="op-data">${hasSetup ? escapeHtml(setup.side || "long").toUpperCase() : "Paper only"}</div>
        <div class="op-actions"><a href="${escapeHtml(paperUrl)}">Practice</a><a href="${escapeHtml(reviewUrl)}">Review</a></div>
      </div>`;
  }

  function renderAnalysis(data) {
    activeRenderedAnalysis = data;
    try { refreshSignalLinks(setupFromAnalysis(data)); } catch (error) {}
    const ratingClass = data.rating === "BUY" || data.rating === "LIVE" ? "buy" : data.rating === "SELL" ? "sell" : "";
    const metrics = data.metrics || {};
    const company = data.company || buildCompanyRead(data.symbol || "AAPL", data);
    const grade = safeGradeAnalysis(data);
    const companyList = items => (items || []).slice(0, 4).map(item => `<li>${escapeHtml(item)}</li>`).join("");
    const gradeWarnings = grade?.warnings?.slice(0, 3) || [];
    const gradeNotes = grade?.notes?.slice(0, 2) || [];
    const primaryGradeRead = gradeWarnings[0] || gradeNotes[0] || "Review trend, levels, risk/reward, catalyst quality, and liquidity before sizing.";
    const gradeNoteHtml = gradeWarnings.length || gradeNotes.length
      ? [
          ...gradeWarnings.map(item => `<div class="signal-grade-note">${escapeHtml(item)}</div>`),
          ...gradeNotes.map(item => `<div class="signal-grade-note good">${escapeHtml(item)}</div>`)
        ].slice(0, 4).join("")
      : `<div class="signal-grade-note">Save the setup to preserve this grade and send it into Risk, Paper Trading, and Journal.</div>`;
    const feedNoteHtml = data.feedNote
      ? `<div class="signal-grade-note ${data.feedDelayed ? "" : "good"}">${escapeHtml(data.feedNote)}</div>`
      : "";
    document.getElementById("analysisResult").innerHTML = `
      <div class="result-top">
        <div>
          <div class="symbol">${escapeHtml(data.symbol || "--")}</div>
          <div class="name">${escapeHtml(data.name || data.source || "Latest available market analysis")}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="rating ${ratingClass}">${escapeHtml(data.rating || "WAIT")}</div>
      </div>
      ${feedNoteHtml}
      <div class="metrics">
        <div class="metric"><div class="label">Price</div><strong>${escapeHtml(metrics.price || "--")}</strong></div>
        <div class="metric"><div class="label">Support</div><strong>${escapeHtml(metrics.support || "--")}</strong></div>
        <div class="metric"><div class="label">Resistance</div><strong>${escapeHtml(metrics.resistance || "--")}</strong></div>
        <div class="metric"><div class="label">Stop</div><strong>${escapeHtml(metrics.stop || metrics.bottom || "--")}</strong></div>
        <div class="metric"><div class="label">Target</div><strong>${escapeHtml(metrics.target || metrics.top || "--")}</strong></div>
        <div class="metric"><div class="label">R:R / RSI</div><strong>${escapeHtml(metrics.rr || "--")} / ${escapeHtml(metrics.rsi || "--")}</strong></div>
      </div>
      <div class="signal-grade">
        <div class="signal-grade-head">
          <h3>Setup Grader</h3>
          <span class="company-source">${grade ? `${grade.score}/100 ${grade.label}` : "No Grade"}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="signal-grade-grid">
          <div class="signal-grade-card">
            <h4>Score</h4>
            <strong>${grade ? `${grade.score}/100` : "--"}</strong>
            <p>${escapeHtml(grade?.modeText?.expert || "No setup score yet.")}</p>
          </div>
          <div class="signal-grade-card">
            <h4>Quality</h4>
            <strong>${escapeHtml(grade?.label || "No Grade")}</strong>
            <p>${escapeHtml(`${grade?.setup?.assetType || "asset"} / ${grade?.setup?.side || "side"} / ${data.rating || "WAIT"}`)}</p>
          </div>
          <div class="signal-grade-card">
            <h4>Main Read</h4>
            <p>${escapeHtml(grade?.modeText?.beginner || primaryGradeRead)}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="signal-grade-list">${gradeNoteHtml}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="company-read">
        <div class="company-read-head">
          <h3>${escapeHtml(company.title || "Company / Future Read")}</h3>
          <span class="company-source">${escapeHtml(company.source || "Local read")}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="company-grid">
          <div class="company-card">
            <h4>What It Is</h4>
            <p>${escapeHtml(company.summary || "Company context is loading.")}</p>
          </div>
          <div class="company-card">
            <h4>Future Drivers</h4>
            <ul>${companyList(company.drivers)}</ul>
          </div>
          <div class="company-card">
            <h4>What Can Break It</h4>
            <ul>${companyList(company.risks)}</ul>
          </div>
          <div class="company-card">
            <h4>Verify First</h4>
            <ul>${companyList(company.verify)}</ul>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="workflow-actions" aria-label="Trade workflow actions">
        <button class="flow-btn primary" type="button" onclick="saveVisibleSetup()">Save Setup</button>
        <button class="flow-btn" type="button" onclick="addAnalyzedToWatchlist()">+ Watchlist</button>
        <button class="flow-btn" type="button" onclick="openWorkflow('trade_planner.html')">Plan Strategy</button>
        <button class="flow-btn" type="button" onclick="openWorkflow('execution_workbench.html')">Size Risk</button>
        <button class="flow-btn gold" type="button" onclick="openWorkflow('practice_workbench.html')">Paper Trade</button>
      </div>
      <div class="live-widgets">
        <div class="widget-box">
          <div class="widget-label"><span>Live Quote / Chart</span><span class="tvSymbolLabel">${escapeHtml(tradingViewSymbol(data.symbol || "AAPL"))}</span></div>
          <div class="tvOverview"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="widget-box technical">
          <div class="widget-label"><span>Technical Rating</span><span>Native</span></div>
          <div class="tvTechnical"></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="analysis-body">
        <div>
          <h3>Signal Logic</h3>
          <ul>${(data.rationale || []).slice(0, 7).map(item => `<li>${escapeHtml(item)}</li>`).join("")}</ul>
        </div>
        <div>
          <h3>Market Context</h3>
          ${renderMarketContext(data)}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="status-note" id="liveStatus">Live chart, technical rating, and company read refreshed. Review the setup before planning risk.</div>`;
  }

  let activeAnalysisToken = 0;

  function updateCompanyRead(symbol, analysis, candles, token) {
    fetchCompanyRead(symbol, analysis)
      .then(company => {
        if (token !== activeAnalysisToken) return;
        analysis.company = company;
        renderAnalysis(analysis);
        renderTradingViewWidgets(symbol, candles, analysis);
        writeLastSetup(setupFromAnalysis(analysis));
        const note = document.getElementById("liveStatus");
        if (note) note.textContent = `${company.title} updated from ${company.source}. Use this as context, not a prediction.`;
      })
      .catch(() => {});
  }

  async function analyzeAsset(symbol) {
    const requestedSymbol = cleanSymbol(symbol);
    const token = ++activeAnalysisToken;
    const state = document.getElementById("feedState");
    state.textContent = "Loading";
    const loadingAnalysis = widgetOnlyAnalysis(requestedSymbol);
    loadingAnalysis.candles = [];
    renderAnalysis(loadingAnalysis);
    renderTradingViewWidgets(requestedSymbol, [], loadingAnalysis);
    try {
      const candles = await fetchCandles(requestedSymbol);
      if (token !== activeAnalysisToken) return;
      const analysis = analyzeCandles(requestedSymbol, candles);
      analysis.candles = candles;
      analysis.source = candles.source || analysis.source;
      analysis.feedDelayed = Boolean(candles.delayed);
      analysis.feedNote = candles.delayed
        ? `${requestedSymbol} is using delayed fallback candles in this browser. Deploy on Vercel with Alpaca env vars for live intraday candles on every supported ticker.`
        : `${requestedSymbol} candle analysis loaded from ${candles.source || "the live/backend feed"}.`;
      analysis.company = buildCompanyRead(requestedSymbol, analysis);
      renderAnalysis(analysis);
      renderTradingViewWidgets(requestedSymbol, candles, analysis);
      state.textContent = candles.delayed ? "Delayed" : "Live";
      if (candles.delayed) {
        analysis.rationale = [
          "Local browser could not reach the live intraday candle feed, so this analysis is using delayed daily fallback candles.",
          ...(analysis.rationale || [])
        ].slice(0, 6);
        renderAnalysis(analysis);
        renderTradingViewWidgets(requestedSymbol, candles, analysis);
      }
      try { writeLastSetup(setupFromAnalysis(analysis)); } catch (setupError) {}
      updateCompanyRead(requestedSymbol, analysis, candles, token);
      fetchAndInjectNews(requestedSymbol);
    } catch (error) {
      if (token !== activeAnalysisToken) return;
      const fallback = widgetOnlyAnalysis(requestedSymbol);
      fallback.rating = "CHECK";
      fallback.name = "TradingView chart is available. Automatic candle levels are blocked in this browser session.";
      fallback.rationale = [
        "The chart panel pulls through TradingView immediately for the live visual.",
        "The Yahoo/proxy candle request did not return, so this result is chart-only instead of stale or fake.",
        "Open Trade Builder to manually mark entry, stop, target, support, and resistance from the chart."
      ];
      fallback.company = buildCompanyRead(requestedSymbol, fallback);
      state.textContent = "Chart Only";
      renderAnalysis(fallback);
      renderTradingViewWidgets(requestedSymbol, [], fallback);
      try { writeLastSetup(setupFromAnalysis(fallback)); } catch (setupError) {}
      updateCompanyRead(requestedSymbol, fallback, [], token);
    } finally {
      const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString([], {hour: '2-digit', minute:'2-digit', second:'2-digit'});
      if (token === activeAnalysisToken && state.textContent === "Loading") state.textContent = `Chart Only (${time})`;
      else if (token === activeAnalysisToken) state.textContent += ` (${time})`;
    }
  }

  window.commandCenterSubmit = function commandCenterSubmit(event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    const input = document.getElementById("assetInput");
    analyzeAsset(input?.value || "AAPL");
    return false;
  };

  const analysisForm = document.getElementById("analysisForm");
  if (analysisForm) analysisForm.addEventListener("submit", window.commandCenterSubmit);
  
  // Ctrl+Enter to trigger analysis
  document.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
    if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'Enter') {
      const input = document.getElementById('assetInput');
      if (input && input.value) {
        e.preventDefault();
        analyzeAsset(input.value);
        document.querySelector('.analysis-card')?.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'center'});
      }
    }
  });
  document.getElementById("assetInput")?.addEventListener("input", () => refreshSignalLinks());
  document.getElementById("refreshPulse")?.addEventListener("click", () => refreshMarketPulse(true));
  document.getElementById("heroWorkflow")?.addEventListener("click", event => {
    const control = event.target.closest("[data-flow-step]");
    if (!control) return;
    if (control.dataset.flowStep !== "analyze") return;
    event.preventDefault();
    const card = document.querySelector(".analysis-card");
    const input = document.getElementById("assetInput");
    card?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth", block: "center" });
    window.setTimeout(() => {
      input?.focus();
      input?.select();
    }, 260);
  });
  window.addEventListener("dto:user-changed", () => updateSnapshot());
  window.addEventListener("dto:setup-saved", () => updateSnapshot());
  window.addEventListener("dto:trade-recorded", () => updateSnapshot());
  window.addEventListener("storage", event => {
    if (["dtoLastSetup", "dtoSetupPacket", "dtoSetupPackets", "dtoPaperTradingAccount", "dtoUsers", "dtoActiveUser", "trades"].includes(event.key)) updateSnapshot();
  });

  function bootCommandCenter() {
    if (!localStorage.getItem("dtoScannerWatchlist")) {
       localStorage.setItem("dtoScannerWatchlist", JSON.stringify([
         {symbol: 'SPY', type: 'Watch', level: '', note: 'Pre-populated'},
         {symbol: 'QQQ', type: 'Watch', level: '', note: 'Pre-populated'},
         {symbol: 'AAPL', type: 'Watch', level: '', note: 'Pre-populated'}
       ]));
    }
    try { updateSnapshot(); } catch (error) {}
    try { updateClock(); } catch (error) {}
    try {
      const bootAnalysis = widgetOnlyAnalysis(document.getElementById("assetInput")?.value || "AAPL");
      renderAnalysis(bootAnalysis);
      renderTradingViewWidgets(bootAnalysis.symbol || "AAPL", [], bootAnalysis);
    } catch (error) {
      const status = document.getElementById("liveStatus");
      if (status) status.textContent = "Command Center recovered from a startup render issue. Enter a ticker and analyze again.";
    }
    try { renderProductionPath(); } catch (error) {}
    try { refreshSignalLinks(); } catch (error) {}
    try {
      const cachedPulse = readJson("dtoMarketPulse", null);
      if (cachedPulse?.results?.length) renderMarketPulse(cachedPulse.results);
      window.setTimeout(() => refreshMarketPulse(false), 300);
    } catch (error) {}
  }

  // â”€â”€ Watchlist Ratings â”€â”€
  const WATCHLIST_KEY = 'dtoScannerWatchlist';
  const MAX_WATCHLIST = 15;

  function readWatchlistSymbols() {
    try {
      const list = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(WATCHLIST_KEY) || '[]');
      return list.map(item => typeof item === 'string' ? item : item?.symbol).filter(Boolean);
    } catch { return []; }
  }

  function addAnalyzedToWatchlist() {
    const data = activeRenderedAnalysis;
    const symbol = cleanSymbol(data?.symbol || document.getElementById('assetInput')?.value);
    if (!symbol) return;
    try {
      const list = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(WATCHLIST_KEY) || '[]');
      if (list.some(item => (typeof item === 'string' ? item : item?.symbol) === symbol)) {
        const note = document.getElementById('liveStatus');
        if (note) note.textContent = `${symbol} is already in your watchlist.`;
        return;
      }
      if (list.length >= MAX_WATCHLIST) {
        const note = document.getElementById('liveStatus');
        if (note) note.textContent = `Watchlist is full (${MAX_WATCHLIST} max). Remove a symbol first.`;
        return;
      }
      const entry = {
        symbol,
        type: data?.rating || 'Watch',
        level: data?.metrics?.support || '',
        note: `Added from Command Center at ${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}`,
        savedAt: new Date().toISOString()
      };
      list.unshift(entry);
      localStorage.setItem(WATCHLIST_KEY, JSON.stringify(list));
      renderWatchlistRatings();
      const note = document.getElementById('liveStatus');
      if (note) note.textContent = `${symbol} added to shared watchlist.`;
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Watchlist save error:', err);
    }
  }

  const watchlistCache = {};
  
  async function renderWatchlistRatings() {
    const grid = document.getElementById('wlGrid');
    if (!grid) return;
    const symbols = readWatchlistSymbols();
    if (!symbols.length) {
      grid.innerHTML = '<div class="wl-empty">No symbols in your watchlist yet.<br>Analyze a ticker above and click "+ Watchlist", or add from Market Desk or Bot Engine.</div>';
      return;
    }
    
    const now = Date.now();
    grid.innerHTML = symbols.map(sym => {
      const cached = watchlistCache[sym];
      if (cached && (now - cached.timestamp < 60000)) {
        return renderWatchlistCard(sym, cached.data);
      }
      return `<div class="wl-card" id="wl-card-${sym}">
        <div class="wl-top">
          <span class="wl-sym">${escapeHtml(sym)}</span>
          <span class="wl-badge wait">...</span>
        </div>
        <div class="wl-meta">
          <span class="wl-move">Loading</span>
          <span>--</span>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');

    const toFetch = symbols.filter(sym => !watchlistCache[sym] || (now - watchlistCache[sym].timestamp >= 60000));
    
    if (toFetch.length) {
      await Promise.allSettled(toFetch.map(async sym => {
        try {
          const candles = await fetchCandles(sym, '1h', 160);
          const analysis = analyzeCandles(sym, candles);
          watchlistCache[sym] = { timestamp: Date.now(), data: analysis };
        } catch (e) {
          watchlistCache[sym] = { timestamp: Date.now(), data: null };
        }
      }));
    }

    const ratingOrder = { 'BUY': 1, 'HOLD': 2, 'SELL': 3, 'WAIT': 4, 'CHECK': 5 };
    let sortedSymbols = [...symbols].sort((a, b) => {
      const aData = watchlistCache[a]?.data;
      const bData = watchlistCache[b]?.data;
      const aRating = aData ? (aData.rating || 'HOLD') : 'CHECK';
      const bRating = bData ? (bData.rating || 'HOLD') : 'CHECK';
      const aScore = ratingOrder[aRating] || 5;
      const bScore = ratingOrder[bRating] || 5;
      if (aScore !== bScore) return aScore - bScore;
      const aMove = aData?.metrics?.move || 0;
      const bMove = bData?.metrics?.move || 0;
      return bMove - aMove;
    });

    grid.innerHTML = sortedSymbols.map(sym => renderWatchlistCard(sym, watchlistCache[sym]?.data)).join('');
  }

  function renderWatchlistCard(sym, analysis) {
    if (!analysis) {
      return `<div class="wl-card" onclick="event.preventDefault(); document.getElementById('assetInput').value='${sym}'; analyzeAsset('${sym}'); document.querySelector('.analysis-card')?.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'center'});">
        <div class="wl-top">
          <span class="wl-sym">${escapeHtml(sym)}</span>
          <span class="wl-badge wait">CHECK</span>
        </div>
        <div class="wl-meta">
          <span class="wl-move">No data</span>
          <span>--</span>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    }

    let badge = 'wait';
    let label = analysis.rating || 'HOLD';
    if (label === 'BUY') badge = 'buy';
    else if (label === 'SELL') badge = 'sell';
    else if (label === 'HOLD') badge = 'hold';

    const price = analysis.metrics?.close || 0;
    const move = analysis.metrics?.move || 0;
    const moveText = `${move >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${move.toFixed(2)}%`;
    const moveClass = move >= 0 ? 'up' : 'dn';
    const conf = safeGradeAnalysis(analysis)?.score || '--';

    return `<a class="wl-card" href="signal_dashboard.html?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(sym)}" onclick="event.preventDefault(); document.getElementById('assetInput').value='${sym}'; analyzeAsset('${sym}'); document.querySelector('.analysis-card')?.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'center'});">
        <div class="wl-top">
          <span class="wl-sym">${escapeHtml(sym)}</span>
          <span class="wl-badge ${badge}">${label}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="wl-meta">
          <span class="wl-move ${moveClass}">${price ? '$'+price.toFixed(2) : '--'} (${moveText})</span>
          <span>Score: ${conf}</span>
        </div>
      </a>`;
  }

  // Listen for watchlist changes from other tabs/pages
  window.addEventListener('storage', event => {
    if (event.key === WATCHLIST_KEY) renderWatchlistRatings();
  });

  bootCommandCenter();
  renderWatchlistRatings();
  setInterval(updateClock, 30000);
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script src="assets/daytrader-os.js?v=20260504-vercel1"></script>
<script>
const ASSETS = [
  { symbol:"SPY", label:"S&P 500", role:"Broad market direction" },
  { symbol:"QQQ", label:"Nasdaq", role:"Growth / tech risk appetite" },
  { symbol:"IWM", label:"Small Caps", role:"Breadth / speculation" },
  { symbol:"VIX", label:"Volatility", role:"Risk and stop-width pressure" },
  { symbol:"BTC", label:"Bitcoin", role:"Crypto market direction" },
  { symbol:"ETH", label:"Ethereum", role:"Altcoin liquidity tone" },
  { symbol:"DXY", label:"Dollar", role:"Macro pressure check" },
  { symbol:"GLD", label:"Gold", role:"Safety / inflation tone" }
];
const STORAGE_KEY = "dtoMarketContexts";
const fieldIds = ["earnings","macro","headlineRisk","headlineNotes","sessionMode","ruleTrend","ruleVix","ruleCatalyst","ruleLevels","ruleCrypto","ruleSize"];

function readJson(key, fallback) {
  try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || JSON.stringify(fallback)); }
  catch (error) { return fallback; }
}
function writeJson(key, value) {
  localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(value));
  return value;
}
function dto() {
  return window.DTO || {
    escapeHtml: value => String(value ?? "").replace(/[&<>"']/g, ch => ({ "&":"&amp;", "<":"&lt;", ">":"&gt;", '"':"&quot;", "'":"&#39;" }[ch])),
    getSetup: () => readJson("dtoSetupPacket", null),
    saveSetup: setup => (localStorage.setItem("dtoSetupPacket", JSON.stringify(setup)), setup),
    renderMissionControl: () => {}
  };
}
function assetId(symbol, suffix) { return `${symbol}_${suffix}`; }
function renderAssets() {
  const saved = readJson("dtoMarketContextDraft", {});
  document.getElementById("assetGrid").innerHTML = ASSETS.map(asset => `
    <article class="asset-card">
      <div class="asset-top"><strong>${asset.symbol}</strong><span>${asset.label}</span></div>
      <select id="${assetId(asset.symbol,"bias")}">
        <option value="neutral">Neutral / unclear</option>
        <option value="bullish">Bullish</option>
        <option value="bearish">Bearish</option>
        <option value="riskOff">Risk-off warning</option>
      </select>
      <input id="${assetId(asset.symbol,"level")}" placeholder="Key level / note">
      <small>${asset.role}</small>
    </article>`).join("");
  ASSETS.forEach(asset => {
    const bias = document.getElementById(assetId(asset.symbol,"bias"));
    const level = document.getElementById(assetId(asset.symbol,"level"));
    if (saved.assets?.[asset.symbol]?.bias) bias.value = saved.assets[asset.symbol].bias;
    if (saved.assets?.[asset.symbol]?.level) level.value = saved.assets[asset.symbol].level;
    bias.addEventListener("change", renderScore);
    level.addEventListener("input", renderScore);
  });
}
function currentContext() {
  const assets = {};
  ASSETS.forEach(asset => {
    assets[asset.symbol] = {
      bias: document.getElementById(assetId(asset.symbol,"bias")).value,
      level: document.getElementById(assetId(asset.symbol,"level")).value.trim()
    };
  });
  return {
    id: `context-${Date.now()}`,
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    assets,
    earnings: document.getElementById("earnings").value,
    macro: document.getElementById("macro").value,
    headlineRisk: document.getElementById("headlineRisk").value,
    headlineNotes: document.getElementById("headlineNotes").value.trim(),
    sessionMode: document.getElementById("sessionMode").value,
    rules: {
      trend: ruleTrend.checked,
      vix: ruleVix.checked,
      catalyst: ruleCatalyst.checked,
      levels: ruleLevels.checked,
      crypto: ruleCrypto.checked,
      size: ruleSize.checked
    }
  };
}
function scoreContext(ctx = currentContext()) {
  let score = 50;
  const rules = [];
  const spy = ctx.assets.SPY.bias;
  const qqq = ctx.assets.QQQ.bias;
  const iwm = ctx.assets.IWM.bias;
  const vix = ctx.assets.VIX.bias;
  const btc = ctx.assets.BTC.bias;
  const eth = ctx.assets.ETH.bias;
  const bullishCount = [spy, qqq, iwm].filter(v => v === "bullish").length;
  const bearishCount = [spy, qqq, iwm].filter(v => v === "bearish" || v === "riskOff").length;

  if (bullishCount >= 2) { score += 15; rules.push({ good:true, text:"Index alignment supports selective long setups." }); }
  if (bearishCount >= 2) { score -= 14; rules.push({ text:"Index alignment is weak. Favor smaller size, shorts, or paper trades." }); }
  if (vix === "riskOff" || vix === "bullish") { score -= 12; rules.push({ text:"Volatility is elevated. Widen stops or reduce size." }); }
  if (btc === "bullish" && eth === "bullish") { score += 8; rules.push({ good:true, text:"BTC/ETH tone supports crypto risk appetite." }); }
  if (btc === "bearish" || btc === "riskOff" || eth === "bearish" || eth === "riskOff") { score -= 8; rules.push({ text:"Crypto tone is weak. Altcoin momentum needs extra confirmation." }); }
  if (ctx.earnings === "major") { score -= 7; rules.push({ text:"Major earnings risk is active. Avoid holding through surprise reports." }); }
  if (ctx.macro === "high") { score -= 10; rules.push({ text:"High macro risk. Wait for data/Fed reaction before pressing size." }); }
  if (ctx.headlineRisk === "extreme") { score -= 10; rules.push({ text:"Extreme headline risk. Paper-only or A+ setups." }); }
  if (ctx.sessionMode === "half") { score -= 4; rules.push({ text:"Session mode is half size. Respect reduced exposure." }); }
  if (ctx.sessionMode === "paper" || ctx.sessionMode === "noTrade") { score -= 15; rules.push({ text:"Session mode blocks normal live risk." }); }
  const checked = Object.values(ctx.rules).filter(Boolean).length;
  score += checked * 3;
  if (checked < 4) rules.push({ text:"Execution checklist is incomplete. Finish rules before trading." });
  if (ctx.headlineNotes.length > 20) { score += 4; rules.push({ good:true, text:"Headline/catalyst notes are specific enough to review later." }); }

  score = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Math.round(score)));
  const bias = score >= 72 ? "Risk-On" : score >= 55 ? "Selective" : score >= 40 ? "Defensive" : "Paper Only";
  return { score, bias, rules };
}
function renderScore() {
  const ctx = currentContext();
  writeJson("dtoMarketContextDraft", ctx);
  const result = scoreContext(ctx);
  document.getElementById("scoreBox").innerHTML = `
    <div class="score-ring" style="--score:${result.score}"><div><strong>${result.score}</strong><span>${result.bias}</span></div></div>
    <div class="bias">${result.bias}</div>
    <p class="readout">${summaryLine(ctx, result)}</p>
    <div class="rule-list">${result.rules.slice(0, 7).map(rule => `<div class="rule ${rule.good ? "good" : ""}">${escapeText(rule.text)}</div>`).join("")}</div>`;
}
function summaryLine(ctx, result) {
  if (result.bias === "Risk-On") return "Market context supports planned trades, but each setup still needs levels, catalyst, and R:R.";
  if (result.bias === "Selective") return "There is enough context to trade selectively. Avoid forcing weak setups.";
  if (result.bias === "Defensive") return "Risk is mixed or elevated. Reduce size and demand cleaner confirmation.";
  return "This context is not friendly for live risk. Paper trade, observe, or wait for clarity.";
}
function escapeText(value) {
  return dto().escapeHtml ? dto().escapeHtml(value) : String(value ?? "");
}
function saveContext() {
  const ctx = currentContext();
  const result = scoreContext(ctx);
  const saved = [{ ...ctx, score: result.score, bias: result.bias }, ...readJson(STORAGE_KEY, [])].slice(0, 20);
  writeJson(STORAGE_KEY, saved);
  renderSaved();
  renderScore();
}
function renderSaved() {
  const list = readJson(STORAGE_KEY, []);
  document.getElementById("savedContexts").innerHTML = list.length ? list.slice(0, 8).map(item => `
    <div class="saved-row">
      <strong>${new Date(item.createdAt).toLocaleString()} / ${escapeText(item.bias)} / ${item.score}/100</strong>
      <span>SPY ${escapeText(item.assets?.SPY?.bias || "--")} / QQQ ${escapeText(item.assets?.QQQ?.bias || "--")} / VIX ${escapeText(item.assets?.VIX?.bias || "--")} / BTC ${escapeText(item.assets?.BTC?.bias || "--")}</span>
      <span>${escapeText(item.headlineNotes || "No catalyst notes saved.")}</span>
    </div>`).join("") : `<p class="readout">No saved market reads yet. Build the context above and save it before trading.</p>`;
}
function attachToSetup() {
  const api = dto();
  const setup = api.getSetup?.() || {};
  const ctx = currentContext();
  const result = scoreContext(ctx);
  const note = `Market context: ${result.bias} ${result.score}/100. ${summaryLine(ctx, result)} Headlines: ${ctx.headlineNotes || "none logged"}`;
  api.saveSetup({ ...setup, riskNotes: [...(setup.riskNotes || []), note], catalysts: [...(setup.catalysts || []), ctx.headlineNotes].filter(Boolean), sourcePage:"market_context.html" });
  api.renderMissionControl?.();
}
function restoreDraft() {
  const draft = readJson("dtoMarketContextDraft", null);
  if (!draft) return;
  ["earnings","macro","headlineRisk","headlineNotes","sessionMode"].forEach(id => {
    if (draft[id] !== undefined) document.getElementById(id).value = draft[id];
  });
  if (draft.rules) {
    ruleTrend.checked = !!draft.rules.trend;
    ruleVix.checked = !!draft.rules.vix;
    ruleCatalyst.checked = !!draft.rules.catalyst;
    ruleLevels.checked = !!draft.rules.levels;
    ruleCrypto.checked = !!draft.rules.crypto;
    ruleSize.checked = !!draft.rules.size;
  }
}
renderAssets();
restoreDraft();
fieldIds.forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).addEventListener("input", renderScore));
fieldIds.forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).addEventListener("change", renderScore));
document.getElementById("saveContext").addEventListener("click", saveContext);
document.getElementById("copyToSetup").addEventListener("click", attachToSetup);
renderScore();
renderSaved();
dto().renderMissionControl?.();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<style>

<script>
// â”€â”€ Clock â”€â”€
function tickClock() {
  document.getElementById('clock').textContent =
    new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en-US',{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit',second:'2-digit'});
}
tickClock();
setInterval(tickClock, 1000);

function escHtml(s) {
  return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;');
}
function fmtNum(n) {
  if (!n && n !== 0) return 'â€”';
  if (n >= 1e9) return `${(n/1e9).toFixed(1)}B`;
  if (n >= 1e6) return `${(n/1e6).toFixed(1)}M`;
  if (n >= 1e3) return `${(n/1e3).toFixed(0)}K`;
  return String(n);
}
function fmtPremium(n) {
  if (!n) return 'â€”';
  if (n >= 1e6) return `$${(n/1e6).toFixed(2)}M`;
  if (n >= 1e3) return `$${(n/1e3).toFixed(0)}K`;
  return `$${n}`;
}

// â”€â”€ Section toggle â”€â”€
function toggleSection(id) {
  const body = document.getElementById(`body-${id}`);
  const tog  = document.getElementById(`toggle-${id}`);
  const isHidden = body.hasAttribute('hidden');
  if (isHidden) { body.removeAttribute('hidden'); tog.classList.add('open'); }
  else          { body.setAttribute('hidden',''); tog.classList.remove('open'); }
}

// â”€â”€ Badge helper â”€â”€
function setBadge(id, count, hasData) {
  const el = document.getElementById(`badge-${id}`);
  if (!el) return;
  el.textContent = hasData ? String(count) : '!';
}

// â”€â”€ Show more â”€â”€
const showMoreState = { insider: 8, sweeps: 8 };
const allData = { insider: [], sweeps: [] };

function showMore(key) {
  showMoreState[key] += 10;
  if (key === 'insider') renderInsiderRows();
  if (key === 'sweeps')  renderSweeps();
}

// â”€â”€ Symbol Pools â”€â”€
const STOCK_POOL = [
  'SPY','QQQ','AAPL','TSLA','NVDA','AMD','META','MSFT','AMZN','GOOGL',
  'NFLX','CRM','ORCL','AVGO','QCOM','MU','INTC','TXN','NOW','SNOW',
  'JPM','GS','BAC','MS','V','MA','PYPL','COIN','HOOD','PLTR',
];
const CRYPTO_POOL_SYMBOLS = ['BTC','ETH','SOL','DOGE','XRP','BNB','AVAX','LINK','ADA','MATIC'];
const CRYPTO_PAIRS = {
  BTC:'BTCUSDT', ETH:'ETHUSDT', SOL:'SOLUSDT', DOGE:'DOGEUSDT', XRP:'XRPUSDT',
  BNB:'BNBUSDT', AVAX:'AVAXUSDT', LINK:'LINKUSDT', ADA:'ADAUSDT', MATIC:'MATICUSDT',
};
let sweepBatchIdx = 0;
let zoneBatchIdx  = 0;

function getRotatingBatch(pool, size, idx) {
  const doubled = [...pool, ...pool];
  const start = (idx * size) % pool.length;
  return doubled.slice(start, start + size);
}

// â”€â”€ 1. HALT SCANNER â”€â”€
async function loadHalts() {
  const tbody = document.getElementById('rows-halts');
  tbody.innerHTML = '<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="6"><span class="spinner"></span>Fetching haltsâ€¦</td></tr>';
  try {
    const resp = await fetch('/api/halts');
    const data = await resp.json();
    if (!data.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'API error');
    setBadge('halts', data.halts.length, true);

    const lgEl = document.getElementById('haltCountLg');
    if (data.halts.length > 0) {
      lgEl.textContent = data.halts.length;
      lgEl.removeAttribute('hidden');
    } else {
      lgEl.setAttribute('hidden','');
    }

    if (!data.halts.length) {
      tbody.innerHTML = '<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="6" style="color:var(--green)">âœ“ No active trading halts</td></tr>';
      return;
    }
    tbody.innerHTML = data.halts.map(h => `
      <tr>
        <td class="c-bright" style="font-weight:700">${escHtml(h.symbol)}</td>
        <td class="c-muted">${escHtml(h.market)}</td>
        <td class="halt-${h.reasonCode}">${escHtml(h.reasonCode)}</td>
        <td class="${'halt-'+h.reasonCode}">${escHtml(h.reason)}</td>
        <td>${escHtml(h.haltDate)} ${escHtml(h.haltTime)}</td>
        <td>${h.resumeTime ? `${escHtml(h.resumeDate)} ${escHtml(h.resumeTime)}` : '<span class="c-muted">Pending</span>'}</td>
      </tr>`).join('');
  } catch(e) {
    setBadge('halts', 0, false);
    tbody.innerHTML = `<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="6">âš  ${escHtml(e.message)}</td></tr>`;
  }
}

    </tr>`).join('');
