}

async function loadInsider() {
  const tbody = document.getElementById('rows-insider');
  tbody.innerHTML = '<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="5"><span class="spinner"></span>Fetching Form 4 filingsâ€¦</td></tr>';
  try {
    const resp = await fetch('/api/insider?limit=60');
    const data = await resp.json();
    if (!data.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'API error');
    allData.insider = data.filings;
    setBadge('insider', data.count, true);
    if (!data.filings.length) {
      tbody.innerHTML = '<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="5">No Form 4 filings found in the last 48 hours.</td></tr>';
      return;
    }
    showMoreState.insider = 8;
    renderInsiderRows();
  } catch(e) {
    setBadge('insider', 0, false);
    tbody.innerHTML = `<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="5">âš  ${escHtml(e.message)}</td></tr>`;
  }
}

// â”€â”€ 3. EARNINGS â”€â”€
let earningsSymbols = [];

async function loadEarnings() {
  const tbody = document.getElementById('rows-earnings');
  tbody.innerHTML = '<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="5"><span class="spinner"></span>Loading earnings calendarâ€¦</td></tr>';
  try {
    const symParam = earningsSymbols.length ? `?symbols=${earningsSymbols.join(',')}` : '';
    const resp = await fetch(`/api/earnings${symParam}`);
    const data = await resp.json();
    if (!data.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'API error');
    setBadge('earnings', data.count, true);
    if (!data.earnings.length) {
      tbody.innerHTML = '<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="5">No earnings reports found in the next 7 days for tracked symbols.</td></tr>';
      return;
    }
    tbody.innerHTML = data.earnings.map(e => `
      <tr>
        <td class="c-bright" style="font-weight:700">${escHtml(e.dayName)}</td>
        <td class="c-gold" style="font-weight:700">${escHtml(e.symbol)}</td>
        <td><span class="badge-pill badge-${e.when}">${e.when === 'bmo' ? 'Pre-Market' : 'After-Market'}</span></td>
        <td>${e.epsEstimate !== null ? `<span class="c-green">$${Number(e.epsEstimate).toFixed(2)}</span>` : '<span class="c-muted">â€”</span>'}</td>
        <td class="c-muted">${escHtml(e.date)}</td>
      </tr>`).join('');
  } catch(e) {
    setBadge('earnings', 0, false);
    tbody.innerHTML = `<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="5">âš  ${escHtml(e.message)}</td></tr>`;
  }
}

function addEarningsSymbol() {
  const input = document.getElementById('earningsSymInput');
  const val = input.value.trim().toUpperCase();
  if (!val) return;
  const syms = val.split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);
  earningsSymbols = [...new Set([...earningsSymbols, ...syms])];
  input.value = '';
  loadEarnings();
}
document.getElementById('earningsSymInput').addEventListener('keydown', e => {
  if (e.key === 'Enter') addEarningsSymbol();
});

// â”€â”€ 4. GOLDEN SWEEPS (rotating batches) â”€â”€
let sweepFilter = 'all';
let rawSweeps   = [];

function setSweepFilter(f) {
  sweepFilter = f;
  ['all','call','put'].forEach(k => {
    document.getElementById(`filter-${k}`)?.classList.toggle('active', k === f);
  });
  showMoreState.sweeps = 8;
  renderSweeps();
}

function renderSweeps() {
  const tbody = document.getElementById('rows-sweeps');
  const moreBtn = document.getElementById('more-sweeps');
  const sortKey = document.getElementById('sweepSort')?.value || 'premium';

  let rows = rawSweeps;
  if (sweepFilter !== 'all') rows = rows.filter(s => s.type === sweepFilter);
  rows = [...rows].sort((a, b) => {
    if (sortKey === 'vol') return b.volume - a.volume;
    if (sortKey === 'ratio') return b.volOiRatio - a.volOiRatio;
    return b.premiumEst - a.premiumEst;
  });

  // Featured top sweep
  let fsEl = document.querySelector('#body-sweeps .featured-sweep');
  if (fsEl) fsEl.remove();
  if (rows.length) {
    const top = rows[0];
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.className = 'featured-sweep';
    div.innerHTML = `<span class="fs-label">TOP SWEEP</span>
      <span class="fs-sym">${escHtml(top.symbol)}</span>
      <span class="badge-pill badge-${top.type}" style="margin:0 4px">${top.type.toUpperCase()}</span>
      <span class="fs-info">$${top.strike} Â· ${escHtml(top.expiry)}</span>
      <span class="fs-premium">${fmtPremium(top.premiumEst)}</span>`;
    const table = document.querySelector('#body-sweeps table');
    if (table) document.getElementById('body-sweeps').insertBefore(div, table);
  }

  const limit = showMoreState.sweeps;
  const visible = rows.slice(0, limit);
  tbody.innerHTML = visible.map(s => `
    <tr>
      <td class="c-bright" style="font-weight:700">${escHtml(s.symbol)}</td>
      <td><span class="badge-pill badge-${s.type}">${s.type.toUpperCase()}</span></td>
      <td class="c-bright">$${s.strike}</td>
      <td class="c-muted">${escHtml(s.expiry)}</td>
      <td class="${s.type==='call'?'c-green':'c-red'}" style="font-weight:700">${fmtNum(s.volume)}</td>
      <td class="c-muted">${fmtNum(s.openInterest)}</td>
      <td class="c-gold" style="font-weight:700">${s.volOiRatio}x</td>
      <td class="${s.type==='call'?'c-green':'c-red'}" style="font-weight:700">${fmtPremium(s.premiumEst)}</td>
      <td class="c-muted">${s.impliedVolatility ? s.impliedVolatility+'%' : 'â€”'}</td>
    </tr>`).join('');

  if (rows.length > limit) moreBtn.removeAttribute('hidden');
  else moreBtn.setAttribute('hidden','');
}

async function loadSweeps() {
  const tbody = document.getElementById('rows-sweeps');
  tbody.innerHTML = '<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="9"><span class="spinner"></span>Scanning options flowâ€¦</td></tr>';
  try {
    const batch = getRotatingBatch(STOCK_POOL, 10, sweepBatchIdx);
    sweepBatchIdx++;
    const batchNum = sweepBatchIdx;
    const totalBatches = Math.ceil(STOCK_POOL.length / 10);
    document.getElementById('sweeps-meta').textContent =
      `Options Flow Â· batch ${((batchNum - 1) % totalBatches) + 1}/${totalBatches} Â· Vol/OI â‰¥ 2.5x`;

    const resp = await fetch(`/api/options-flow?symbols=${batch.join(',')}`);
    const data = await resp.json();
    if (!data.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'API error');
    rawSweeps = data.sweeps;
    setBadge('sweeps', data.count, true);
    if (!data.sweeps.length) {
      tbody.innerHTML = '<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="9">No unusual options activity detected in this batch.</td></tr>';
      // Still update featured sweep removal
      const fsEl = document.querySelector('#body-sweeps .featured-sweep');
      if (fsEl) fsEl.remove();
      return;
    }
    showMoreState.sweeps = 8;
    renderSweeps();
  } catch(e) {
    setBadge('sweeps', 0, false);
    tbody.innerHTML = `<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="9">âš  ${escHtml(e.message)}</td></tr>`;
  }
}

// â”€â”€ 5. DARK POOL (FINRA ATS via client-side fetch) â”€â”€
async function loadDarkPool() {
  const tbody = document.getElementById('rows-darkpool');
  tbody.innerHTML = '<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="5"><span class="spinner"></span>Fetching FINRA ATS dataâ€¦</td></tr>';
  try {
    const filesResp = await fetch('https://api.finra.org/data/group/otcMarket/name/weeklyDownloadFiles', {
      headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json' }
    });
    if (!filesResp.ok) throw new Error('FINRA API unavailable');
    const filesList = await filesResp.json();

    const consolidated = (filesList || []).find(f =>
      f.label && f.label.toLowerCase().includes('consolidated') ||
      f.fileName && f.fileName.toLowerCase().includes('consolidated')
    ) || filesList?.[0];

    if (!consolidated) throw new Error('No ATS file found');
    const fileUrl = consolidated.downloadURL || consolidated.url || '';
    if (!fileUrl) throw new Error('No download URL');

    const csvResp = await fetch(fileUrl);
    const csv = await csvResp.text();
    const lines = csv.split(/\r?\n/).filter(Boolean);

    const symTotals = {};
    const symDark   = {};

    for (let i = 1; i < lines.length; i++) {
      const parts = lines[i].split(',').map(p => p.replace(/"/g,'').trim());
      const sym = parts[1] || '';
      const darkVol  = parseFloat(parts[2]) || 0;
      const totalVol = parseFloat(parts[3]) || 0;
      if (!sym || sym.length > 6) continue;
      symDark[sym]   = (symDark[sym]  || 0) + darkVol;
      symTotals[sym] = (symTotals[sym]|| 0) + totalVol;
    }

    const sorted = Object.keys(symTotals)
      .filter(s => symTotals[s] > 0)
      .map(s => ({
        symbol:   s,
        darkVol:  symDark[s] || 0,
        totalVol: symTotals[s],
        darkPct:  symTotals[s] > 0 ? (symDark[s] / symTotals[s]) * 100 : 0,
      }))
      .sort((a, b) => b.darkPct - a.darkPct)
      .slice(0, 25);

    setBadge('darkpool', sorted.length, true);
    if (!sorted.length) throw new Error('No ATS data parsed');

    tbody.innerHTML = sorted.map(r => {
      const pct = r.darkPct.toFixed(1);
      const signal = r.darkPct >= 50 ? '<span class="c-red">VERY HIGH</span>'
                   : r.darkPct >= 40 ? '<span class="c-orange">HIGH</span>'
                   : r.darkPct >= 30 ? '<span class="c-gold">MODERATE</span>'
                   : '<span class="c-muted">LOW</span>';
      return `
        <tr>
          <td class="c-bright" style="font-weight:700">${escHtml(r.symbol)}</td>
          <td class="c-blue">${fmtNum(r.darkVol)}</td>
          <td class="c-muted">${fmtNum(r.totalVol)}</td>
          <td class="c-blue" style="font-weight:700">${pct}%</td>
          <td>${signal}</td>
        </tr>`;
    }).join('');

  } catch(e) {
    setBadge('darkpool', 0, false);
    tbody.innerHTML = `<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="5">âš  FINRA ATS unavailable: ${escHtml(e.message)}</td></tr>`;
  }
}

// â”€â”€ 6. DEMAND ZONES & LIQUIDITY (rotating batches) â”€â”€
async function computeDemandZones(symbol) {
  const resp = await fetch(`/api/candles?symbol=${symbol}&interval=1d&limit=200`);
  const data = await resp.json();
  if (!data.ok || !data.candles || data.candles.length < 30) return null;

  const candles = data.candles;
  const vols = candles.map(c => c.volume || 0);
  const avgVol = vols.reduce((a,b) => a+b, 0) / vols.length;

  const zones = [];
  for (let i = 5; i < candles.length - 5; i++) {
    const c = candles[i];
    const body = Math.abs(c.close - c.open);
    const isGreen = c.close >= c.open;
    if (!isGreen) continue;
    if ((c.volume || 0) < avgVol * 1.3) continue;

    const futureHigh = Math.max(...candles.slice(i+1, i+6).map(x => x.close));
    const rally = (futureHigh - c.close) / c.close;
    if (rally < 0.04) continue;

    const prior = candles.slice(Math.max(0,i-10), i);
    const wasDepressed = prior.some(p => p.low <= c.low * 1.01);
    if (!wasDepressed) continue;

    const zoneHigh = c.open + body * 0.5;
    const zoneLow  = c.low;
    const daysAgo  = candles.length - 1 - i;
    const strength = rally > 0.08 ? 'STRONG' : rally > 0.04 ? 'MODERATE' : 'WEAK';
    zones.push({ symbol, zoneLow, zoneHigh, strength, daysAgo, type: 'Demand' });
  }

  return zones.length ? zones[zones.length - 1] : null;
}

async function fetchBinanceLiqWall(symbol, pair) {
  const resp = await fetch(`https://api.binance.com/api/v3/depth?symbol=${pair}&limit=20`);
  const data = await resp.json();
  if (!data.bids || !data.asks) return null;

  const sumNotional = (arr) => arr.reduce((a, [p, q]) => a + parseFloat(p) * parseFloat(q), 0);

  let bestBid = { notional: 0, price: 0 };
  for (let i = 0; i < data.bids.length - 3; i++) {
    const slice = data.bids.slice(i, i + 4);
    const notional = sumNotional(slice);
    if (notional > bestBid.notional) bestBid = { notional, price: parseFloat(data.bids[i][0]) };
  }

  let bestAsk = { notional: 0, price: 0 };
  for (let i = 0; i < data.asks.length - 3; i++) {
    const slice = data.asks.slice(i, i + 4);
    const notional = sumNotional(slice);
    if (notional > bestAsk.notional) bestAsk = { notional, price: parseFloat(data.asks[i][0]) };
  }

  const results = [];
  if (bestBid.notional >= 100000) {
    results.push({
      symbol, zoneLow: bestBid.price * 0.9995, zoneHigh: bestBid.price,
      strength: bestBid.notional >= 1e6 ? 'STRONG' : 'MODERATE',
      type: `Bid Wall ($${bestBid.notional >= 1e6 ? (bestBid.notional/1e6).toFixed(1)+'M' : (bestBid.notional/1e3).toFixed(0)+'K'})`,
      daysAgo: null,
    });
  }
  if (bestAsk.notional >= 100000) {
    results.push({
      symbol, zoneLow: bestAsk.price, zoneHigh: bestAsk.price * 1.0005,
      strength: bestAsk.notional >= 1e6 ? 'STRONG' : 'MODERATE',
      type: `Ask Wall ($${bestAsk.notional >= 1e6 ? (bestAsk.notional/1e6).toFixed(1)+'M' : (bestAsk.notional/1e3).toFixed(0)+'K'})`,
      daysAgo: null,
    });
  }
  return results;
}

async function loadZones() {
  const tbody = document.getElementById('rows-zones');
  tbody.innerHTML = '<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="5"><span class="spinner"></span>Computing zonesâ€¦</td></tr>';
  try {
    const stockBatch  = getRotatingBatch(STOCK_POOL, 8, zoneBatchIdx);
    const cryptoBatch = getRotatingBatch(CRYPTO_POOL_SYMBOLS, 3, zoneBatchIdx);
    zoneBatchIdx++;

    document.getElementById('zones-meta').textContent =
      `Candle analysis + Binance depth Â· ${stockBatch.join(', ')} + ${cryptoBatch.join(', ')}`;

    const results = [];

    const stockResults = await Promise.allSettled(
      stockBatch.map(s => computeDemandZones(s))
    );
    stockResults.forEach(r => {
      if (r.status === 'fulfilled' && r.value) results.push(r.value);
    });

    const cryptoResults = await Promise.allSettled(
      cryptoBatch
        .filter(s => CRYPTO_PAIRS[s])
        .map(s => fetchBinanceLiqWall(s, CRYPTO_PAIRS[s]).then(arr => arr || []))
    );
    cryptoResults.forEach(r => {
      if (r.status === 'fulfilled') results.push(...r.value);
    });

    setBadge('zones', results.length, true);
    if (!results.length) {
      tbody.innerHTML = '<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="5">No significant demand zones detected in current data.</td></tr>';
      return;
    }

    tbody.innerHTML = results.map(z => {
      const hi = z.zoneHigh >= 100 ? z.zoneHigh.toFixed(2) : z.zoneHigh.toFixed(4);
      const lo = z.zoneLow  >= 100 ? z.zoneLow.toFixed(2)  : z.zoneLow.toFixed(4);
      const strengthColor = z.strength === 'STRONG' ? 'c-green' : z.strength === 'MODERATE' ? 'c-gold' : 'c-muted';
      const lastTest = z.daysAgo !== null ? (z.daysAgo === 0 ? 'Today' : `${z.daysAgo}d ago`) : 'Live';
      return `
        <tr>
          <td class="c-bright" style="font-weight:700">${escHtml(z.symbol)}</td>
          <td class="c-purple">$${escHtml(lo)} â€“ $${escHtml(hi)}</td>
          <td class="${strengthColor}" style="font-weight:700">${escHtml(z.strength)}</td>
          <td class="c-muted">${escHtml(z.type)}</td>
          <td class="c-muted">${escHtml(lastTest)}</td>
        </tr>`;
    }).join('');
  } catch(e) {
    setBadge('zones', 0, false);
    tbody.innerHTML = `<tr class="state-row"><td colspan="5">âš  ${escHtml(e.message)}</td></tr>`;
  }
}

// â”€â”€ Ticker Strip â”€â”€
async function loadTicker() {
  const track = document.getElementById('tickerTrack');
  const TICKER_STOCKS  = ['SPY','QQQ','AAPL','TSLA','NVDA','MSFT'];
  const TICKER_CRYPTOS = ['BTCUSDT','ETHUSDT','SOLUSDT'];

  const stockResults = await Promise.allSettled(
    TICKER_STOCKS.map(sym =>
      fetch(`/api/candles?symbol=${sym}&interval=1d&limit=2`).then(r => r.json())
    )
  );
  const cryptoResults = await Promise.allSettled(
    TICKER_CRYPTOS.map(pair =>
      fetch(`https://api.binance.com/api/v3/ticker/24hr?symbol=${pair}`).then(r => r.json())
    )
  );

  const items = [];

  TICKER_STOCKS.forEach((sym, i) => {
    const r = stockResults[i];
    if (r.status !== 'fulfilled' || !r.value.ok || !r.value.candles?.length) return;
    const candles = r.value.candles;
    if (candles.length < 2) return;
    const prev  = candles[candles.length - 2].close;
    const last  = candles[candles.length - 1].close;
    const pct   = ((last - prev) / prev * 100).toFixed(2);
    const cls   = pct > 0 ? 't-up' : pct < 0 ? 't-down' : 't-flat';
    const sign  = pct > 0 ? '+' : '';
    const price = last >= 1000 ? last.toFixed(0) : last >= 100 ? last.toFixed(2) : last.toFixed(2);
    items.push(`<span class="ticker-item"><span class="t-sym">${sym}</span><span class="t-price">$${price}</span><span class="${cls}">${sign}${pct}%</span></span>`);
  });

  const cryptoLabels = ['BTC','ETH','SOL'];
  TICKER_CRYPTOS.forEach((pair, i) => {
    const r = cryptoResults[i];
    if (r.status !== 'fulfilled' || r.value.code) return;
    const d    = r.value;
    const last = parseFloat(d.lastPrice);
    const pct  = parseFloat(d.priceChangePercent).toFixed(2);
    const cls  = pct > 0 ? 't-up' : pct < 0 ? 't-down' : 't-flat';
    const sign = pct > 0 ? '+' : '';
    const price = last >= 10000 ? last.toFixed(0) : last >= 100 ? last.toFixed(2) : last.toFixed(4);
    items.push(`<span class="ticker-item"><span class="t-sym">${cryptoLabels[i]}</span><span class="t-price">$${price}</span><span class="${cls}">${sign}${pct}%</span></span>`);
  });

  if (!items.length) return;

  const sep = '<span class="ticker-sep">Â·</span>';
  const content = items.join(sep);
  track.innerHTML = content + sep + content; // duplicate for seamless loop
}

// â”€â”€ Sync All â”€â”€
function syncAll() {
  loadHalts();
  loadInsider();
  loadEarnings();
  loadSweeps();
  loadDarkPool();
  loadZones();
  loadTicker();
  const now = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en-US',{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'});
  document.getElementById('lastSync').textContent = `Last sync: ${now}`;
}

document.getElementById('syncAllBtn').addEventListener('click', syncAll);

// â”€â”€ Auto-refresh intervals â”€â”€
setInterval(loadHalts,    60000);
setInterval(loadSweeps,   90000);
setInterval(loadInsider,  300000);

<script src="assets/daytrader-os.js?v=20260504-vercel1"></script>
<script>
const $ = id => document.getElementById(id);
const read = (key, fallback) => { try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || JSON.stringify(fallback)); } catch { return fallback; } };
const write = (key, value) => { localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(value)); return value; };
const clean = value => String(value || "").trim().toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9.-]/g, "");
const money = value => Number.isFinite(Number(value)) ? "$" + Number(value).toFixed(Number(value) >= 100 ? 2 : 4).replace(/\.?0+$/, "") : "--";

async function api(path) {
  const cleanPath = String(path).replace(/^\/+/, "");
  const urls = [`/api/${cleanPath}`, `/.netlify/functions/${cleanPath}`];
  let last;
  for (const url of urls) {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(url);
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || res.status);
      return data;
    } catch (error) { last = error; }
  }
  throw last || new Error("API unavailable");
}

function renderWatch() {
  const list = read("dtoScannerWatchlist", []);
  $("watchList").innerHTML = list.length ? list.map(item => `
    <div class="row"><div><strong>${item.symbol}</strong><span>${item.type} / ${item.level || "no level"} / ${item.note || "no note"}</span></div><a class="btn" href="signal_dashboard.html?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(item.symbol)}">Signal</a></div>
  `).join("") : `<div class="note">No watchlist names yet. Add 3-5 high-conviction ideas only.</div>`;
}

function renderAlerts() {
  const list = read("dtoAlerts", []);
  $("alertList").innerHTML = list.length ? list.slice(0, 6).map(item => `
    <div class="row"><div><strong>${item.symbol}</strong><span>${item.trigger} ${item.level ? "near " + item.level : ""}. ${item.note || ""}</span></div><span>${item.priority || "Plan"}</span></div>
  `).join("") : `<div class="note">No alert plans saved yet.</div>`;
}

function renderContext() {
  const checks = [
    "SPY/QQQ trend agrees with trade direction",
    "VIX is not warning of sudden risk-off tape",
    "Earnings and macro calendar checked",
    "Sector or crypto beta supports the setup",
    "Ground News/catalyst bias checked before reacting",
    "Plan includes no-trade condition"
  ];
  const saved = read("dtoMarketGate", {});
  $("contextChecks").innerHTML = checks.map((text, index) => `
    <label class="row" style="grid-template-columns:auto 1fr"><input type="checkbox" data-check="${index}" ${saved[index] ? "checked" : ""}><span>${text}</span></label>
  `).join("");
  document.querySelectorAll("[data-check]").forEach(input => input.addEventListener("change", () => {
    const next = read("dtoMarketGate", {});
    next[input.dataset.check] = input.checked;
    write("dtoMarketGate", next);
  }));
}

async function analyze(symbol) {
  const sym = clean(symbol || $("quickSymbol").value || "AAPL");
  $("quickSymbol").value = sym;
  $("openSignal").href = `signal_dashboard.html?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(sym)}`;
  $("quickNote").textContent = "Checking public server feed...";
  if (!/^https?:$/.test(location.protocol)) {
    $("quickNote").textContent = "Local file mode cannot call hosted API functions. Use Open Signal or deploy to Vercel to test the public feed.";
    return;
  }
  try {
    const data = await api(`analyze?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(sym)}`);
    $("quickPrice").textContent = money(data.price);
    $("quickRating").textContent = data.rating || "CHECK";
    $("quickSource").textContent = (data.candleSource || data.source || "API").replace(/^Alpaca /, "Alpaca ");
    $("quickTime").textContent = new Date(data.asOf || Date.now()).toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit" });
    $("quickNote").textContent = `${data.name || data.symbol || sym}: ${(data.rationale || []).slice(0, 2).join(" ") || "Review chart, levels, and catalyst before planning."}`;
  } catch (error) {
    $("quickPrice").textContent = "--";
    $("quickRating").textContent = "CHECK";
    $("quickSource").textContent = "Blocked";
    $("quickNote").textContent = error.message || "Public feed unavailable.";
  }
}

$("quickForm").addEventListener("submit", event => { event.preventDefault(); analyze(); });
$("watchForm").addEventListener("submit", event => {
  event.preventDefault();
  const item = { symbol: clean($("watchSymbol").value), type: $("watchType").value, level: $("watchLevel").value, note: $("watchNote").value, savedAt: new Date().toISOString() };
  if (!item.symbol) return;
  write("dtoScannerWatchlist", [item, ...read("dtoScannerWatchlist", []).filter(old => old.symbol !== item.symbol)].slice(0, 30));
  renderWatch();
});
$("alertForm").addEventListener("submit", event => {
  event.preventDefault();
  const item = { symbol: clean($("alertSymbol").value), trigger: $("alertTrigger").value, level: $("alertLevel").value, note: $("alertNote").value, savedAt: new Date().toISOString() };
  if (!item.symbol) return;
  write("dtoAlerts", [item, ...read("dtoAlerts", [])].slice(0, 40));
  renderAlerts();
});
$("savePrep").addEventListener("click", () => {
  write("dtoPrepWorkbench", { bias: $("biasNotes").value, plan: $("gamePlan").value, savedAt: new Date().toISOString() });
  $("savePrep").textContent = "Saved";
  setTimeout(() => $("savePrep").textContent = "Save Prep", 900);
});
["AAPL","TSLA","NVDA","SPY","QQQ","BTC","ETH","SOL","INTC","AMD"].forEach(sym => {
  const btn = document.createElement("button");
  btn.type = "button";
  btn.textContent = sym;
  btn.addEventListener("click", () => { $("quickSymbol").value = sym; $("watchSymbol").value = sym; analyze(sym); });
  $("quickChips").appendChild(btn);
});
const prep = read("dtoPrepWorkbench", {});
$("biasNotes").value = prep.bias || "";
$("gamePlan").value = prep.plan || "";
renderWatch();
renderAlerts();
renderContext();
analyze("AAPL");
</script>
</body>
</html>

function calc(){const c=Math.max(1,Number(contracts.value||1)), ls=Number(longStrike.value), ss=Number(shortStrike.value), ask=Number(longAsk.value), bid=Number(shortBid.value), width=Math.abs(ss-ls), isCredit=strategy.value==="credit", isProt=strategy.value==="protective";const net=isCredit?Math.max(0,bid-ask):ask;const maxLoss=isProt?ask*100*c:isCredit?Math.max(0,(width-(bid-ask))*100*c):net*100*c;const maxProfit=isProt?Infinity:isCredit?Math.max(0,(bid-ask)*100*c):Math.max(0,(width-net)*100*c);const breakeven=Number(underlying.value||0)+(strategy.value==="credit"?bid-ask:net);const spread=Math.abs(ask-bid);result.innerHTML=[["Net",DTO.money(net*100*c)],["Max Loss",DTO.money(maxLoss)],["Max Profit",Number.isFinite(maxProfit)?DTO.money(maxProfit):"Open-ended"],["Bid/Ask Width",DTO.money(spread)]].map(x=>`<div class="dto-mission-panel"><div class="dto-panel-kicker">${x[0]}</div><h3>${x[1]}</h3></div>`).join("")+`<div class="dto-warning dto-span-4">Breakeven estimate ${DTO.money(breakeven)}. ${spread>.35?"Wide spread: use limit orders and avoid thin contracts.":"Liquidity width is reasonable for planning."} Live execution remains locked.</div>`;}
hedgeForm.addEventListener("submit",e=>{e.preventDefault();calc();});const s=DTO.getSetup();if(s){symbol.value=s.symbol||"";underlying.value=s.entry||"";}calc();
</script></body></html>

<script>
const STORAGE_KEY = "dtoPaperTradingAccount";
const CRYPTO_DATA = {
  BTC:"BTCUSDT", XBT:"BTCUSDT", BITCOIN:"BTCUSDT", ETH:"ETHUSDT", ETHEREUM:"ETHUSDT",
  SOL:"SOLUSDT", SOLANA:"SOLUSDT", DOGE:"DOGEUSDT", XRP:"XRPUSDT", ADA:"ADAUSDT",
  BNB:"BNBUSDT", AVAX:"AVAXUSDT", LINK:"LINKUSDT", LTC:"LTCUSDT", BCH:"BCHUSDT",
  DOT:"DOTUSDT", MATIC:"MATICUSDT", POL:"POLUSDT", UNI:"UNIUSDT", AAVE:"AAVEUSDT",
  ATOM:"ATOMUSDT", NEAR:"NEARUSDT", OP:"OPUSDT", ARB:"ARBUSDT", FIL:"FILUSDT",
  ETC:"ETCUSDT", TRX:"TRXUSDT", XLM:"XLMUSDT", HBAR:"HBARUSDT", ICP:"ICPUSDT",
  INJ:"INJUSDT", SUI:"SUIUSDT", APT:"APTUSDT", PEPE:"PEPEUSDT", SHIB:"SHIBUSDT",
  WIF:"WIFUSDT", BONK:"BONKUSDT", FET:"FETUSDT", RENDER:"RENDERUSDT", RNDR:"RENDERUSDT", TAO:"TAOUSDT"
};
let account = loadAccount();
let side = "long";
let gameMode = true;
let tickTimer = null;
let liveTimer = null;
const WATCH_SYMBOLS = ["BTC","ETH","SOL","DOGE","AAPL","TSLA"];

function defaultAccount(){
  return { startingCash: 100000, cash: 100000, positions: [], log: [], realized: 0, quotes: {} };
}
function loadAccount(){
  try {
    const saved = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY));
    return { ...defaultAccount(), ...(saved || {}), quotes: saved?.quotes || {}, positions: saved?.positions || [], log: saved?.log || [] };
  }
  catch(e) { return defaultAccount(); }
}
function saveAccount(){ localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(account)); }
function cleanSymbol(value){ return String(value || "").trim().toUpperCase().replace(/^BINANCE:/,"").replace(/[^A-Z0-9.\-/_\s]/g,"").replace(/[-/_\s]/g,""); }
function cryptoPairFor(value){
  const key = cleanSymbol(value);
  if (CRYPTO_DATA[key]) return CRYPTO_DATA[key];
  if (/^[A-Z0-9]{2,12}USDT$/.test(key)) return key;
  if (/^[A-Z0-9]{2,12}USD$/.test(key)) return key.replace(/USD$/,"USDT");
  return null;
}
function cryptoBaseFor(value){
  const pair = cryptoPairFor(value);
  return pair ? pair.replace(/USDT$/,"") : null;
}
function money(value){
  const n = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return "$--";
  return "$" + n.toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: n >= 1 ? 2 : 6 });
}
function qtyFmt(value){
  const n = Number(value);
  return Number.isFinite(n) ? n.toLocaleString(undefined, { maximumFractionDigits: 6 }) : "--";
}
function setStatus(text){ document.getElementById("quoteState").textContent = text; }
function setSide(next){
  side = next;
  document.getElementById("longBtn").className = next === "long" ? "active long" : "";
  document.getElementById("shortBtn").className = next === "short" ? "active short" : "";
}
async function fetchJson(url){
  const response = await fetch(url);
  if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`${response.status} ${response.statusText}`.trim());
  return response.json();
}
async function fetchPublicApiJson(path){
  const cleanPath = String(path || "").replace(/^\/+/, "");
  const urls = [`/api/${cleanPath}`, `/.netlify/functions/${cleanPath}`];
  let lastError = null;
  for (const url of urls) {
    try {
      return await fetchJson(url);
    } catch (error) {
      lastError = error;
    }
  }
  throw lastError || new Error("Public API unavailable");
}
async function fetchPublicCandles(symbol){
  if (!/^https?:$/.test(location.protocol)) throw new Error("Public server API requires hosted mode");
  const data = await fetchPublicApiJson(`analyze?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(cleanSymbol(symbol))}`);
  const candles = (data?.candles || []).map(candle => ({
    high: Number(candle.high),
    low: Number(candle.low),
    close: Number(candle.close),
    volume: Number(candle.volume)
  })).filter(c => Number.isFinite(c.close) && Number.isFinite(c.high) && Number.isFinite(c.low));
  if (!candles.length) throw new Error(data?.error || "Public candle feed returned no candles");
  return candles;
}
async function fetchCryptoCandles(symbol, limit = 120){
  const pair = cryptoPairFor(symbol);
  const base = cryptoBaseFor(symbol);
  if (!pair) return null;
  const binanceUrls = [
    `https://data-api.binance.vision/api/v3/klines?symbol=${pair}&interval=1h&limit=${limit}`,
    `https://api.binance.us/api/v3/klines?symbol=${pair}&interval=1h&limit=${limit}`,
    `https://api.binance.com/api/v3/klines?symbol=${pair}&interval=1h&limit=${limit}`
  ];
  for (const url of binanceUrls) {
    try {
      const rows = await fetchJson(url);
      const candles = rows.map(row => ({ high:+row[2], low:+row[3], close:+row[4], volume:+row[5] })).filter(c => Number.isFinite(c.close) && Number.isFinite(c.high) && Number.isFinite(c.low));
      if (candles.length) return candles;
    } catch(e) {}
  }
  if (base) {
    try {
      const rows = await fetchJson(`https://api.exchange.coinbase.com/products/${base}-USD/candles?granularity=3600`);
      const candles = rows
        .map(row => ({ time:+row[0], low:+row[1], high:+row[2], close:+row[4], volume:+row[5] }))
        .filter(c => Number.isFinite(c.close) && Number.isFinite(c.high) && Number.isFinite(c.low))
        .sort((a,b) => a.time - b.time)
        .slice(-limit);
      if (candles.length) return candles;
    } catch(e) {}
  }
  throw new Error("Crypto candle feed unavailable after trying Binance market data, Binance.US, and Coinbase");
}
async function fetchCandles(symbol){
  const sym = cleanSymbol(symbol);
  try {
    return await fetchPublicCandles(sym);
  } catch(e) {}
  const pair = cryptoPairFor(sym);
  if (pair) {
    return fetchCryptoCandles(sym, 120);
  }
  const yahooUrl = `https://query1.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/${encodeURIComponent(sym)}?range=5d&interval=15m&includePrePost=true`;
  try {
    const response = await fetch(yahooUrl);
    if (!response.ok) throw new Error("Direct quote blocked");
    const data = await response.json();
    return yahooCandles(data);
  } catch(e) {
    const proxy = await fetch(`https://api.allorigins.win/raw?url=${encodeURIComponent(yahooUrl)}`);
    if (!proxy.ok) throw new Error("Stock candle feed unavailable");
    return yahooCandles(await proxy.json());
  }
}
function yahooCandles(data){
  const quote = data.chart?.result?.[0]?.indicators?.quote?.[0];
  if (!quote?.close?.length) throw new Error("No candles returned");
  return quote.close.map((close, index) => ({
    high:+quote.high?.[index],
    low:+quote.low?.[index],
    close:+close,
    volume:+quote.volume?.[index]
  })).filter(c => Number.isFinite(c.close));
}
async function fetchLastPrice(symbol){
  const candles = await fetchCandles(symbol);
  const last = candles[candles.length - 1];
  if (!last) throw new Error("No latest candle");
  const sym = cleanSymbol(symbol);
  const old = account.quotes[sym];
  account.quotes[sym] = { price: last.close, prev: old?.price || last.close, high: last.high, low: last.low, time: new Date().toISOString(), source: "live" };
  saveAccount();
  return account.quotes[sym];
}
async function fetchQuoteForTicket(){
  const sym = cleanSymbol(document.getElementById("symbol").value);
  if (!sym) return;
  setStatus("Fetching");
  try {
    const quote = await fetchLastPrice(sym);
    document.getElementById("price").value = quote.price;
    setStatus("Live");
    render();
  } catch(e) {
    setStatus("Manual");
    alert("Could not fetch live candles for " + sym + ". You can still type a manual paper price.");
  }
}
function sizeByRisk(){
  const entry = Number(document.getElementById("price").value);
  const stop = Number(document.getElementById("stop").value);
  const maxRisk = Number(document.getElementById("maxRisk").value);
  if (!entry || !stop || !maxRisk || entry === stop) {
    alert("Add entry price, stop, and max risk first.");
    return;
  }
  const riskPerShare = Math.abs(entry - stop);
  document.getElementById("qty").value = Math.max(0, maxRisk / riskPerShare).toFixed(6).replace(/\.?0+$/,"");
}
function placePaperTrade(){
  const sym = cleanSymbol(document.getElementById("symbol").value);
  const qty = Number(document.getElementById("qty").value);
  const entry = Number(document.getElementById("price").value);
  const stop = Number(document.getElementById("stop").value) || null;
  const target = Number(document.getElementById("target").value) || null;
  const thesis = document.getElementById("thesis").value.trim();
  if (!sym || !qty || !entry) {
    alert("Add symbol, quantity, and price before placing a paper trade.");
    return;
  }
  const notional = qty * entry;
  if (side === "long" && notional > account.cash) {
    alert("Not enough paper cash for this long position.");
    return;
  }
  if (side === "long") account.cash -= notional;
  account.quotes[sym] = account.quotes[sym] || { price: entry, prev: entry, high: entry, low: entry, time: new Date().toISOString(), source: "manual" };
  account.positions.push({
    id: crypto.randomUUID ? crypto.randomUUID() : String(Date.now()),
    symbol: sym,
    side,
    qty,
    entry,
    stop,
    target,
    thesis,
    openedAt: new Date().toISOString()
  });
  account.log.unshift({ time:new Date().toISOString(), symbol:sym, action:"OPEN " + side.toUpperCase(), qty, price:entry, pnl:null });
  if (window.DTO) DTO.saveSetup({ symbol:sym, side, entry, stop, target, thesis, rating:"PAPER", sourcePage:"paper_trading_simulator.html" });
  document.getElementById("thesis").value = "";
  saveAccount();
  startLiveLoop();
  render();
}
function positionLast(position){
  return account.quotes[position.symbol]?.price || position.entry;
}
function positionPnl(position){
  const last = positionLast(position);
  const direction = position.side === "long" ? 1 : -1;
  return (last - position.entry) * position.qty * direction;
}
function positionRisk(position){
  if (!position.stop) return null;
  return Math.abs(position.entry - position.stop) * position.qty;
}
function closePosition(id){
  const index = account.positions.findIndex(p => p.id === id);
  if (index < 0) return;
  const position = account.positions[index];
  const last = positionLast(position);
  const pnl = positionPnl(position);
  if (position.side === "long") account.cash += position.qty * last;
  account.realized += pnl;
  account.log.unshift({ time:new Date().toISOString(), symbol:position.symbol, action:"CLOSE " + position.side.toUpperCase(), qty:position.qty, price:last, pnl });
  if (window.DTO) DTO.recordTrade({
    source:"paper",
    symbol:position.symbol,
    side:position.side,
    qty:position.qty,
    entry:position.entry,
    exit:last,
    pnl,
    setupType:"Paper trade",
    notes:position.thesis || "",
    closedAt:new Date().toISOString()
  });
  account.positions.splice(index, 1);
  saveAccount();
  render();
}
async function refreshAllQuotes(){
  const symbols = [...new Set([...WATCH_SYMBOLS, ...account.positions.map(p => p.symbol)])];
  if (!symbols.length) return;
  setStatus("Refreshing");
  await Promise.allSettled(symbols.map(fetchLastPrice));
  setStatus("Live");
  render();
}
function paperTick(){
  if (!gameMode) return;
  const symbols = [...new Set([...WATCH_SYMBOLS, ...account.positions.map(p => p.symbol)])];
  symbols.forEach(symbol => {
    const quote = account.quotes[symbol];
    if (!quote?.price) return;
    const volatility = cryptoPairFor(symbol) ? 0.0018 : 0.0009;
    const drift = account.positions.some(p => p.symbol === symbol && p.side === "long") ? 0.00008 : 0;
    const move = ((Math.random() - 0.5) * volatility) + drift;
    const next = Math.max(0.000001, quote.price * (1 + move));
    account.quotes[symbol] = {
      ...quote,
      prev: quote.price,
      price: next,
      high: Math.max(quote.high || next, next),
      low: Math.min(quote.low || next, next),
      time: new Date().toISOString(),
      source: "paper tick"
    };
  });
  render();
}
function startLiveLoop(){
  if (!tickTimer) tickTimer = setInterval(paperTick, 1000);
  if (!liveTimer) liveTimer = setInterval(refreshAllQuotes, 30000);
}
function toggleGameMode(){
  gameMode = !gameMode;
  const btn = document.getElementById("gameToggle");
  btn.textContent = gameMode ? "Pause Ticks" : "Resume Ticks";
  btn.className = gameMode ? "toggle" : "toggle paused";
  document.getElementById("gameModeText").textContent = gameMode ? "Live paper mode is running." : "Paper ticks are paused.";
}
function totals(){
  const openPnl = account.positions.reduce((sum, p) => sum + positionPnl(p), 0);
  const longValue = account.positions.filter(p => p.side === "long").reduce((sum, p) => sum + p.qty * positionLast(p), 0);
  const shortPnl = account.positions.filter(p => p.side === "short").reduce((sum, p) => sum + positionPnl(p), 0);
  return { openPnl, equity: account.cash + longValue + shortPnl };
}
function render(){
  const t = totals();
  document.getElementById("equity").textContent = money(t.equity);
  document.getElementById("cash").textContent = money(account.cash);
  document.getElementById("openPnl").textContent = money(t.openPnl);
  document.getElementById("openPnl").className = "value " + (t.openPnl >= 0 ? "green" : "red");
  document.getElementById("realizedPnl").textContent = money(account.realized);
  document.getElementById("realizedPnl").className = "value " + (account.realized >= 0 ? "green" : "red");
  renderMarketWatch();
  renderPositionArena();
  const positionsBody = document.getElementById("positionsBody");
  positionsBody.innerHTML = account.positions.length ? account.positions.map(position => {
    const pnl = positionPnl(position);
    const risk = positionRisk(position);
    return `<tr>
      <td><strong>${position.symbol}</strong><br><span class="label">${position.thesis ? position.thesis.slice(0, 44) : "No thesis"}</span></td>
      <td class="${position.side === "long" ? "green" : "red"}">${position.side.toUpperCase()}</td>
      <td>${qtyFmt(position.qty)}</td>
      <td>${money(position.entry)}</td>
      <td>${money(positionLast(position))}</td>
      <td class="${pnl >= 0 ? "green" : "red"}">${money(pnl)}</td>
      <td>${risk === null ? "--" : money(risk)}<br><span class="label">S ${position.stop ? money(position.stop) : "--"} / T ${position.target ? money(position.target) : "--"}</span></td>
      <td><button class="secondary danger-action" onclick="closePosition('${position.id}')">Close</button></td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join("") : `<tr><td colspan="8" class="empty">No open paper positions yet. Build a setup, fetch a candle price, then place a fake-money trade.</td></tr>`;
  const logBody = document.getElementById("logBody");
  logBody.innerHTML = account.log.length ? account.log.slice(0, 20).map(item => `
    <tr>
      <td>${new Date(item.time).toLocaleString()}</td>
      <td><strong>${item.symbol}</strong></td>
      <td>${item.action}</td>
      <td>${qtyFmt(item.qty)}</td>
      <td>${money(item.price)}</td>
      <td class="${(item.pnl || 0) >= 0 ? "green" : "red"}">${item.pnl === null ? "--" : money(item.pnl)}</td>
    </tr>`).join("") : `<tr><td colspan="6" class="empty">Closed trades will appear here and can be exported.</td></tr>`;
}
function quoteChange(symbol){
  const q = account.quotes[symbol];
  if (!q?.price || !q?.prev) return 0;
  return ((q.price - q.prev) / q.prev) * 100;
}
function renderMarketWatch(){
  const el = document.getElementById("marketWatch");
  if (!el) return;
  const symbols = [...new Set([...WATCH_SYMBOLS, ...account.positions.map(p => p.symbol)])];
  el.innerHTML = symbols.map(symbol => {
    const q = account.quotes[symbol];
    const change = quoteChange(symbol);
    const cls = change >= 0 ? "green" : "red";
    const flash = change > 0 ? "flash-up" : change < 0 ? "flash-down" : "";
    return `<div class="watch-card ${flash}">
      <div class="card-line"><strong>${symbol}</strong><span class="${cls}">${change ? change.toFixed(2) + "%" : "--"}</span></div>
      <div class="value" style="font-size:25px">${q?.price ? money(q.price) : "--"}</div>
      <div class="micro">${q?.source || "not loaded"}${q?.time ? " / " + new Date(q.time).toLocaleTimeString() : ""}</div>
      <button class="secondary" onclick="document.getElementById('symbol').value='${symbol}'; if(account.quotes['${symbol}']) document.getElementById('price').value=account.quotes['${symbol}'].price;">Trade</button>
    </div>`;
  }).join("");
}
function renderPositionArena(){
  const el = document.getElementById("positionArena");
  if (!el) return;
  el.innerHTML = account.positions.length ? account.positions.map(position => {
    const pnl = positionPnl(position);
    const last = positionLast(position);
    const risk = positionRisk(position);
    const progress = risk ? Math.max(0, Math.min(100, 50 + (pnl / risk) * 50)) : Math.max(0, Math.min(100, 50 + ((last - position.entry) / position.entry) * 900));
    const cls = pnl >= 0 ? "hot" : "cold";
    return `<article class="trade-card ${cls}">
      <div class="card-line">
        <div><div class="symbol-big">${position.symbol}</div><div class="micro">${position.side.toUpperCase()} / ${qtyFmt(position.qty)} @ ${money(position.entry)}</div></div>
        <div class="pnl-big ${pnl >= 0 ? "green" : "red"}">${money(pnl)}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="meter"><span style="width:${progress}%;background:${pnl >= 0 ? "var(--green)" : "var(--red)"}"></span></div>
      <div class="micro">Last ${money(last)} / Stop ${position.stop ? money(position.stop) : "--"} / Target ${position.target ? money(position.target) : "--"}</div>
    </article>`;
  }).join("") : `<article class="trade-card"><div class="symbol-big">No Trades</div><div class="micro">Open a paper trade and this becomes the live P&L arena.</div></article>`;
}
function resetAccount(){
  if (!confirm("Reset the fake-money paper account? This clears local simulator positions and logs.")) return;
  account = defaultAccount();
  saveAccount();
  render();
}
function exportLog(){
  const rows = [["time","symbol","action","qty","price","pnl"], ...account.log.map(item => [item.time,item.symbol,item.action,item.qty,item.price,item.pnl ?? ""])];
  const csv = rows.map(row => row.map(cell => `"${String(cell).replace(/"/g,'""')}"`).join(",")).join("\n");
  const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: "text/csv" });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement("a");
  a.href = url;
  a.download = "paper-trade-log.csv";
  a.click();
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
}
function loadQuerySetup(){
  const params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
  const symbol = cleanSymbol(params.get("symbol"));
  const price = Number(params.get("price") || params.get("entry"));
  const stop = Number(params.get("stop"));
  const target = Number(params.get("target"));
  const nextSide = String(params.get("side") || "").toLowerCase();
  const thesis = params.get("thesis");
  if (symbol) document.getElementById("symbol").value = symbol;
  if (Number.isFinite(price) && price > 0) document.getElementById("price").value = price;
  if (Number.isFinite(stop) && stop > 0) document.getElementById("stop").value = stop;
  if (Number.isFinite(target) && target > 0) document.getElementById("target").value = target;
  if (nextSide === "short" || nextSide === "long") setSide(nextSide);
  if (thesis) document.getElementById("thesis").value = thesis;
}
loadQuerySetup();
render();
startLiveLoop();
refreshAllQuotes();
</script>
</body>
</html>

function renderCandlePatterns(filter) {
  const grid = document.getElementById('patternGrid');
  const filtered = filter === 'all' ? candlePatterns : candlePatterns.filter(p => p.cat === filter);
  grid.innerHTML = filtered.map(p => `
    <div class="pattern-card ${p.cat}">
      <div class="chart-area">${p.svg}</div>
      <div class="pattern-info">
        <div class="pattern-name">${p.name}</div>
        <div class="pattern-signal sig-${p.signal}">
          ${p.signal === 'bull' ? 'â–²' : p.signal === 'bear' ? 'â–¼' : 'â—'} ${p.signal.toUpperCase()} SIGNAL
        </div>
        <div class="reliability">
          ${[1,2,3,4,5].map(i => `<div class="rel-dot ${i <= p.reliability ? 'filled' : ''}"></div>`).join('')}
          <span class="rel-label">Reliability ${p.reliability}/5</span>
        </div>
        <div class="pattern-desc">${p.desc}</div>
        <div class="pattern-rules">
          ${p.rules.map(r => `<div class="rule"><span class="icon">${r[0]}</span><span>${r.slice(1)}</span></div>`).join('')}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  `).join('');
}

function renderChartPatterns() {
  const grid = document.getElementById('chartGrid');
  grid.innerHTML = chartPatterns.map(p => `
    <div class="cp-card">
      <div class="cp-name">${p.name}</div>
      <div class="cp-type">${p.type}</div>
      <div class="cp-svg">${p.svg}</div>
      <div class="cp-desc">${p.desc}</div>
      <div class="how-to-trade">${p.how.split('\n').map(l => `${l}<br>`).join('')}</div>
    </div>
  `).join('');
}

function showCat(cat, btn) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  btn.classList.add('active');

  const candles = document.getElementById('cat-candles');
  const charts = document.getElementById('cat-chart');

  if (cat === 'chart') {
    candles.style.display = 'none';
    charts.style.display = 'block';
    renderChartPatterns();
  } else {
    candles.style.display = 'block';
    charts.style.display = 'none';
    renderCandlePatterns(cat === 'all' ? 'all' : cat === 'neutral' ? 'neutral' : cat === 'bull' ? 'bull' : 'bear');
  }
}

renderCandlePatterns('all');
</script>

<script>
const PINS_KEY = 'dtoPolyPins';
let currentMarkets = [];
let activeCategory = '';
let currentQuery = '';
let searchTimeout = null;
let pinRefreshInterval = null;
let activeOrderMarket = null;
let refreshCountdown = 30;

// â”€â”€ Helpers â”€â”€
function readPins() {
  try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(PINS_KEY) || '[]'); }
  catch { return []; }
}
function savePins(pins) { localStorage.setItem(PINS_KEY, JSON.stringify(pins)); }

function fmtVol(n) {
  if (!n) return '$0';
  if (n >= 1e6) return `$${(n/1e6).toFixed(1)}M`;
  if (n >= 1e3) return `$${(n/1e3).toFixed(0)}K`;
  return `$${n.toFixed(0)}`;
}
function fmtDate(d) {
  if (!d) return 'â€”';
  const dt = new Date(d);
  return isNaN(dt) ? 'â€”' : dt.toLocaleDateString('en-US',{month:'short',day:'numeric'});
}
function catLabel(c) {
  const m = {economics:'macro',crypto:'crypto',politics:'politics',business:'earnings'};
  return m[c] || (c||'general');
}
function escHtml(s) {
  return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;');
}

function polyHeaders() {
  try {
    const raw = localStorage.getItem('dtoActiveUser');
    const uid = raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : null;
    const users = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('dtoUsers') || '[]');
    const u = users.find(x => x.id === uid);
    if (!u || !u.polyApiKey) return {};
    return {
      'x-poly-key':        u.polyApiKey || '',
      'x-poly-secret':     u.polyApiSecret || '',
      'x-poly-passphrase': u.polyPassphrase || '',
      'x-poly-funder':     u.polyFunderAddress || '',
    };
  } catch { return {}; }
}

function hasPolyKeys() {
  const h = polyHeaders();
  return !!(h['x-poly-key'] && h['x-poly-secret'] && h['x-poly-passphrase'] && h['x-poly-funder']);
}

// â”€â”€ AI technical probability â”€â”€
const CRYPTO_MAP = {
  BTC:'BTC', BITCOIN:'BTC', ETH:'ETH', ETHEREUM:'ETH',
  SOL:'SOL', SOLANA:'SOL', DOGE:'DOGE', DOGECOIN:'DOGE',
  XRP:'XRP', BNB:'BNB', AVAX:'AVAX', LINK:'LINK',
  ADA:'ADA', MATIC:'MATIC', DOT:'DOT', SUI:'SUI',
  PEPE:'PEPE', WIF:'WIF', SHIB:'SHIB',
};

function parsePriceTarget(question) {
  const q = question.toUpperCase();
  let symbol = null;
  for (const [key, val] of Object.entries(CRYPTO_MAP)) {
    if (q.includes(key)) { symbol = val; break; }
  }
  if (!symbol) return null;

  const priceMatch = q.match(/\$([0-9,]+(?:\.[0-9]+)?)\s*(?:K|M)?/i);
  if (!priceMatch) return null;
  let raw = priceMatch[1].replace(/,/g,'');
  let targetPrice = parseFloat(raw);
  if (/K/i.test(priceMatch[0])) targetPrice *= 1000;
  if (/M/i.test(priceMatch[0])) targetPrice *= 1e6;
  if (!targetPrice || isNaN(targetPrice)) return null;

  const direction = /FALL|DROP|BELOW|UNDER|LESS/i.test(q) ? 'below' : 'above';
  return { symbol, targetPrice, direction };
}

function sigmoid(x) { return 1 / (1 + Math.exp(-x)); }

async function computeTechProb(symbol, targetPrice, direction, endDate) {
  try {
    const resp = await fetch(`/api/candles?symbol=${symbol}&interval=1d&limit=30`);
    const data = await resp.json();
    if (!data.ok || !data.candles || data.candles.length < 5) return null;

    const candles = data.candles;
    const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);
    const current = closes[closes.length - 1];

    const sma = (arr, n) => arr.slice(-n).reduce((a,b) => a+b, 0) / Math.min(n, arr.length);
    const sma7 = sma(closes, 7);
    const sma14 = sma(closes, 14);
    const trend = (sma7 - sma14) / sma14;

    const old = closes[Math.max(0, closes.length - 15)];
    const momentum = (current - old) / old;

    const dist = (targetPrice - current) / current;
    const daysLeft = endDate
      ? Math.max(1, (new Date(endDate) - Date.now()) / 86400000)
      : 60;
    const timeBonus = Math.log(Math.max(daysLeft, 1)) / 10;

    let score = -dist * 4 + trend * 3 + momentum * 2 + timeBonus;
    if (direction === 'below') score = -score;
    const prob = Math.max(0.05, Math.min(0.95, sigmoid(score)));

    const pct = Math.round(prob * 100);
    const trendTxt = trend > 0.01 ? 'bullish trend' : trend < -0.01 ? 'bearish trend' : 'neutral';
    const basis = `${symbol} $${current.toFixed(current < 10 ? 4 : 0)} â†’ $${targetPrice.toLocaleString()} target Â· ${Math.round(momentum*100)}% 14d Â· ${trendTxt}`;
    return { prob, pct, basis };
  } catch { return null; }
}

const aiCache = new Map();

async function attachAiProb(market) {
  if (aiCache.has(market.id)) {
    const cached = aiCache.get(market.id);
    if (cached) injectAiRow(market.id, cached);
    return;
  }
  const parsed = parsePriceTarget(market.question);
  if (!parsed) { aiCache.set(market.id, null); return; }

  const result = await computeTechProb(parsed.symbol, parsed.targetPrice, parsed.direction, market.endDate);
  aiCache.set(market.id, result);
  if (result) injectAiRow(market.id, result);
}

function injectAiRow(marketId, result) {
  const container = document.getElementById(`ai-slot-${marketId}`);
  if (!container) return;
  container.innerHTML = `
    <div class="outcomes-divider"></div>
    <div class="outcome-row">
      <span class="outcome-label ai">AI</span>
      <div class="bar-track"><div class="bar-fill ai" style="width:${result.pct}%"></div></div>
      <span class="outcome-pct ai">${result.pct}%</span>
      <span class="outcome-price" style="color:var(--purple);font-size:0.55em;width:auto">TECH</span>
    </div>
    <div class="ai-basis">${escHtml(result.basis)}</div>`;
}

// â”€â”€ Fetch markets â”€â”€
async function fetchMarkets(category, q) {
  const params = new URLSearchParams({ action: 'markets', limit: '25' });
  if (category) params.set('category', category);
  if (q)        params.set('q', q);
  const resp = await fetch(`/api/polymarket?${params}`);
  const data = await resp.json();
  return data.markets || [];
}

// â”€â”€ Build card HTML â”€â”€
function buildCard(m) {
  const outcomes = m.outcomes || ['Yes','No'];
  const prices   = m.outcomePrices || ['0.5','0.5'];
  const yesPrice = parseFloat(prices[0]) || 0.5;
  const noPrice  = parseFloat(prices[1]) || 0.5;
  const yesPct   = Math.round(yesPrice * 100);
  const noPct    = Math.round(noPrice  * 100);
  const cat      = catLabel(m.category);
  const isPinned = readPins().some(p => p.id === m.id);
  const tokens   = m.clobTokenIds || [];

  const tierClass = m.volume >= 1_000_000 ? 'card-mega'
                  : m.volume >= 500_000   ? 'card-prominent'
                  : '';

  const yesBold = yesPct >= 70 ? 'font-weight:900' : '';
  const noBold  = noPct  >= 70 ? 'font-weight:900' : '';

  return `
    <div class="market-card ${tierClass}" id="card-${m.id}" data-id="${m.id}">
      <div class="card-top">
        <div class="card-question">${escHtml(m.question)}</div>
        <div class="card-meta">
          <span class="cat-badge ${cat}">${cat.toUpperCase()}</span>
          <span class="vol-label">${fmtVol(m.volume)} vol</span>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="outcomes">
        <div class="outcome-row">
          <span class="outcome-label yes">${escHtml(outcomes[0]||'YES')}</span>
          <div class="bar-track"><div class="bar-fill yes" style="width:${yesPct}%"></div></div>
          <span class="outcome-pct yes" style="${yesBold}">${yesPct}%</span>
          <span class="outcome-price">$${yesPrice.toFixed(2)}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="outcome-row">
          <span class="outcome-label no">${escHtml(outcomes[1]||'NO')}</span>
          <div class="bar-track"><div class="bar-fill no" style="width:${noPct}%"></div></div>
          <span class="outcome-pct no" style="${noBold}">${noPct}%</span>
          <span class="outcome-price">$${noPrice.toFixed(2)}</span>
        </div>
        <div id="ai-slot-${m.id}"></div>
      </div>
      <div class="card-footer">
        <div class="card-stats">
          <span>Ends ${fmtDate(m.endDate)}</span>
          <span>${fmtVol(m.liquidity)} liq</span>
          <span>${fmtVol(m.volume24hr)} 24h vol</span>
        </div>
        <div class="card-actions">
          <button class="card-btn ${isPinned?'pinned':''}" onclick="togglePin(${JSON.stringify(m).replace(/"/g,'&quot;')})">
            ${isPinned?'ðŸ“Œ PINNED':'ðŸ“Œ PIN'}
          </button>
          ${tokens[0] ? `<button class="card-btn" onclick="openOrderBook('${tokens[0]}')">ðŸ“– BOOK</button>` : ''}
          <button class="card-btn trade" onclick="openTradeModal(${JSON.stringify(m).replace(/"/g,'&quot;')})">â†’ TRADE</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
}

// â”€â”€ Patch single card in-place (silent refresh) â”€â”€
function patchCard(cardEl, m) {
  const prices   = m.outcomePrices || ['0.5','0.5'];
  const yesPrice = parseFloat(prices[0]) || 0.5;
  const noPrice  = parseFloat(prices[1]) || 0.5;
  const yesPct   = Math.round(yesPrice * 100);
  const noPct    = Math.round(noPrice  * 100);

  const yesFill = cardEl.querySelector('.bar-fill.yes');
  const noFill  = cardEl.querySelector('.bar-fill.no');
  const yesPctEl = cardEl.querySelector('.outcome-pct.yes');
  const noPctEl  = cardEl.querySelector('.outcome-pct.no');
  const prices_els = cardEl.querySelectorAll('.outcome-price');
  const volEl = cardEl.querySelector('.vol-label');

  if (yesFill)  yesFill.style.width = yesPct + '%';
  if (noFill)   noFill.style.width  = noPct  + '%';
  if (yesPctEl) { yesPctEl.textContent = yesPct + '%'; yesPctEl.style.fontWeight = yesPct >= 70 ? '900' : '700'; }
  if (noPctEl)  { noPctEl.textContent  = noPct  + '%'; noPctEl.style.fontWeight  = noPct  >= 70 ? '900' : '700'; }
  if (prices_els[0]) prices_els[0].textContent = `$${yesPrice.toFixed(2)}`;
  if (prices_els[1]) prices_els[1].textContent = `$${noPrice.toFixed(2)}`;
  if (volEl) volEl.textContent = fmtVol(m.volume) + ' vol';
}

// â”€â”€ Reconcile grid in-place (silent refresh, preserves scroll) â”€â”€
function reconcileGrid(newMarkets) {
  const grid = document.getElementById('marketsGrid');
  const newMap = new Map(newMarkets.map(m => [m.id, m]));

  // Update or remove existing cards
  const existing = [...grid.querySelectorAll('.market-card[data-id]')];
  for (const cardEl of existing) {
    const id = cardEl.dataset.id;
    if (!newMap.has(id)) {
      cardEl.remove();
    } else {
      patchCard(cardEl, newMap.get(id));
    }
  }

  // Add new cards not already in DOM
  const existingIds = new Set(existing.map(el => el.dataset.id));
  for (const m of newMarkets) {
    if (!existingIds.has(m.id)) {
      grid.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', buildCard(m));
      attachAiProb(m);
    }
  }

  // Reorder if sequence changed
  const newOrder = newMarkets.map(m => m.id);
  for (let i = 0; i < newOrder.length; i++) {
    const target = grid.querySelector(`[data-id="${newOrder[i]}"]`);
    const current = grid.children[i];
    if (target && target !== current) grid.insertBefore(target, current);
  }
}

// â”€â”€ Load markets â”€â”€
async function loadMarkets(cat, q, silent) {
  const grid = document.getElementById('marketsGrid');
  if (!silent) grid.innerHTML = '<div class="state-msg"><span class="spinner"></span>LOADINGâ€¦</div>';
  try {
    const markets = await fetchMarkets(cat, q);
    currentMarkets = markets;

    const now = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en-US',{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'});
    const lr = document.getElementById('lastRefresh');
    lr.textContent = `Last sync: ${now}`;
    lr.classList.remove('refresh-flash');
    void lr.offsetWidth;
    lr.classList.add('refresh-flash');

    if (!markets.length) {
      grid.innerHTML = '<div class="state-msg">No markets found. Try a different category or search.</div>';
      return;
    }
    if (silent) {
      reconcileGrid(markets);
    } else {
      grid.innerHTML = markets.map(buildCard).join('');
      markets.forEach(m => attachAiProb(m));
    }
  } catch(e) {
    if (!silent) grid.innerHTML = `<div class="state-msg">Failed to load markets: ${escHtml(e.message)}</div>`;
  }
}

// â”€â”€ Countdown auto-refresh â”€â”€
const countdownTick = setInterval(() => {
  refreshCountdown--;
  const btn = document.getElementById('refreshBtn');
  if (btn) btn.textContent = `â†» REFRESH [${refreshCountdown}s]`;
  if (refreshCountdown <= 0) {
    refreshCountdown = 30;
    loadMarkets(activeCategory, currentQuery, true);
  }
}, 1000);

// â”€â”€ Category tabs â”€â”€
document.querySelectorAll('.cat-tab').forEach(tab => {
  tab.addEventListener('click', () => {
    document.querySelectorAll('.cat-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
    tab.classList.add('active');
    activeCategory = tab.dataset.cat;
    refreshCountdown = 30;
    loadMarkets(activeCategory, currentQuery, false);
  });
});

// â”€â”€ Search â”€â”€
document.getElementById('searchInput').addEventListener('input', e => {
  currentQuery = e.target.value.trim();
  clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
  searchTimeout = setTimeout(() => loadMarkets(activeCategory, currentQuery, false), 400);
});

document.getElementById('refreshBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
  currentQuery = document.getElementById('searchInput').value.trim();
  refreshCountdown = 30;
  loadMarkets(activeCategory, currentQuery, false);
});

// â”€â”€ Pin / unpin â”€â”€
function togglePin(market) {
  const pins = readPins();
  const idx  = pins.findIndex(p => p.id === market.id);
  if (idx >= 0) {
    pins.splice(idx, 1);
  } else {
    pins.push({
      id:           market.id,
      question:     market.question,
      clobTokenIds: market.clobTokenIds || [],
      outcomePrices: market.outcomePrices || ['0.5','0.5'],
      pinnedAt:     Date.now(),
    });
  }
  savePins(pins);
  renderPinned();
  const card = document.getElementById(`card-${market.id}`);
  if (card) {
    const m = currentMarkets.find(x => x.id === market.id);
    if (m) { card.outerHTML = buildCard(m); attachAiProb(m); }
  }
}

function renderPinned() {
  const pins = readPins();
  const list = document.getElementById('pinList');
  if (!pins.length) {
    list.innerHTML = '<div class="pin-empty">Pin markets to track odds live</div>';
    return;
  }
  list.innerHTML = pins.map(p => {
    const yPrice = parseFloat((p.outcomePrices||['0.5'])[0]) || 0.5;
    const nPrice = parseFloat((p.outcomePrices||['0.5','0.5'])[1]) || 0.5;
    const yPct   = Math.round(yPrice*100);
    const nPct   = Math.round(nPrice*100);
    return `
      <div class="pin-item" id="pin-${p.id}">
        <div class="pin-question">${escHtml(p.question)}</div>
        <div class="pin-prices">
          <span class="pin-yes">YES ${yPct}%</span>
          <span class="pin-no">NO ${nPct}%</span>
          <span class="pin-change flat" id="pinchg-${p.id}">â€”</span>
        </div>
        <button class="pin-remove" onclick="unpin('${p.id}')">âœ• REMOVE</button>
      </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function unpin(id) {
  savePins(readPins().filter(p => p.id !== id));
  renderPinned();
}

// â”€â”€ Live price refresh for pinned markets â”€â”€
async function refreshPinnedPrices() {
  const pins = readPins();
  for (const p of pins) {
    const tokenId = (p.clobTokenIds||[])[0];
    if (!tokenId) continue;
    try {
      const resp = await fetch(`/api/polymarket?action=prices&token_id=${encodeURIComponent(tokenId)}`);
      const data = await resp.json();
      if (!data.ok) continue;
      const newYesPct = Math.round(data.mid_price * 100);
      const oldYesPct = Math.round(parseFloat((p.outcomePrices||['0.5'])[0]) * 100);
      const diff = newYesPct - oldYesPct;

      const all = readPins();
      const idx = all.findIndex(x => x.id === p.id);
      if (idx >= 0) {
        all[idx].outcomePrices = [String(data.mid_price), String(1 - data.mid_price)];
        savePins(all);
      }

      const chgEl = document.getElementById(`pinchg-${p.id}`);
      if (chgEl) {
        chgEl.textContent = diff > 0 ? `â†‘ +${diff}%` : diff < 0 ? `â†“ ${diff}%` : 'â€”';
        chgEl.className = `pin-change ${diff>0?'up':diff<0?'down':'flat'}`;
      }
      const yesEl = document.querySelector(`#pin-${p.id} .pin-yes`);
      const noEl  = document.querySelector(`#pin-${p.id} .pin-no`);
      if (yesEl) yesEl.textContent = `YES ${newYesPct}%`;
      if (noEl)  noEl.textContent  = `NO ${100-newYesPct}%`;
    } catch { /* ignore */ }
  }
}

// â”€â”€ Order book popout â”€â”€
async function openOrderBook(tokenId) {
  try {
    const resp = await fetch(`/api/polymarket?action=orderbook&token_id=${encodeURIComponent(tokenId)}`);
    const data = await resp.json();
    if (!data.ok) { alert('Order book unavailable'); return; }
    const lines = [
      `ASKS (sell offers):`,
      ...(data.asks||[]).map(a => `  $${parseFloat(a.price).toFixed(3)}  Ã—  ${parseFloat(a.size).toFixed(0)}`),
      ``,
      `BIDS (buy offers):`,
      ...(data.bids||[]).map(b => `  $${parseFloat(b.price).toFixed(3)}  Ã—  ${parseFloat(b.size).toFixed(0)}`),
      data.spread ? `\nSpread: ${data.spread}` : '',
    ].join('\n');
    alert(lines);
  } catch(e) { alert('Order book fetch failed: ' + e.message); }
}

// â”€â”€ Order modal â”€â”€
function openTradeModal(market) {
  if (!hasPolyKeys()) {
    document.getElementById('keyPanel').scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth'});
    return;
  }
  activeOrderMarket = market;
  document.getElementById('modalQuestion').textContent = market.question;

  const outcomes = market.outcomes || ['Yes','No'];
  const sel = document.getElementById('modalOutcome');
  sel.innerHTML = outcomes.map((o,i) =>
    `<option value="${i===0?'yes':'no'}">${escHtml(o)}</option>`
  ).join('');

  const prices = market.outcomePrices || ['0.5','0.5'];
  document.getElementById('modalPrice').value = parseFloat(prices[0]).toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('modalSize').value = '100';
  document.getElementById('modalError').textContent = '';
  updateOrderCost();
  document.getElementById('orderModal').removeAttribute('hidden');
}

function updateOrderCost() {
  const price = parseFloat(document.getElementById('modalPrice').value) || 0;
  const size  = parseFloat(document.getElementById('modalSize').value) || 0;
  const side  = document.getElementById('modalSide').value;
  const cost  = side === 'BUY' ? (price * size).toFixed(2) : ((1-price) * size).toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('modalCost').textContent = `$${cost}`;
}

document.getElementById('modalPrice').addEventListener('input', updateOrderCost);
document.getElementById('modalSize').addEventListener('input', updateOrderCost);
document.getElementById('modalSide').addEventListener('change', updateOrderCost);
document.getElementById('modalOutcome').addEventListener('change', () => {
  if (!activeOrderMarket) return;
  const idx = document.getElementById('modalOutcome').value === 'yes' ? 0 : 1;
  const p   = (activeOrderMarket.outcomePrices||['0.5','0.5'])[idx];
  document.getElementById('modalPrice').value = parseFloat(p).toFixed(2);
  updateOrderCost();
});

document.getElementById('modalCancel').addEventListener('click', () => {
  document.getElementById('orderModal').setAttribute('hidden','');
  activeOrderMarket = null;
});

document.getElementById('modalSubmit').addEventListener('click', async () => {
  if (!activeOrderMarket) return;
  const errEl = document.getElementById('modalError');
  errEl.textContent = '';

  const outcomeIdx = document.getElementById('modalOutcome').value === 'yes' ? 0 : 1;
  const tokenId    = (activeOrderMarket.clobTokenIds||[])[outcomeIdx];
  if (!tokenId) { errEl.textContent = 'No token ID for this outcome.'; return; }

  const side  = document.getElementById('modalSide').value;
  const price = parseFloat(document.getElementById('modalPrice').value);
  const size  = parseFloat(document.getElementById('modalSize').value);
  if (!price || !size) { errEl.textContent = 'Enter valid price and size.'; return; }

  document.getElementById('modalSubmit').textContent = 'SUBMITTINGâ€¦';
  document.getElementById('modalSubmit').disabled = true;

  try {
    const resp = await fetch('/api/polymarket?action=order', {
      method:  'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', ...polyHeaders() },
      body:    JSON.stringify({ token_id: tokenId, side, price, size }),
    });
    const data = await resp.json();
    if (data.ok) {
      errEl.style.color = 'var(--green)';
      errEl.textContent = 'âœ“ Order submitted successfully.';
      setTimeout(() => {
        document.getElementById('orderModal').setAttribute('hidden','');
        errEl.style.color = '';
        activeOrderMarket = null;
      }, 1500);
    } else {
      errEl.textContent = data.error || 'Order failed.';
    }
  } catch(e) {
    errEl.textContent = 'Network error: ' + e.message;
  } finally {
    document.getElementById('modalSubmit').textContent = 'SUBMIT ORDER';
    document.getElementById('modalSubmit').disabled = false;
  }
});

// â”€â”€ Add pin by keyword â”€â”€
document.getElementById('addPinBtn').addEventListener('click', async () => {
  const val = document.getElementById('addPinInput').value.trim();
  if (!val) return;
  try {
    const resp = await fetch(`/api/polymarket?action=markets&q=${encodeURIComponent(val)}&limit=1`);
    const data = await resp.json();
    const m = (data.markets||[])[0];
    if (!m) { alert('Market not found. Try a different keyword.'); return; }
    togglePin(m);
    document.getElementById('addPinInput').value = '';
  } catch(e) { alert('Search failed: ' + e.message); }
});

// â”€â”€ Key status â”€â”€
function updateKeyPanel() {
  const notice = document.getElementById('keyNotice');
  if (hasPolyKeys()) {
    notice.innerHTML = 'âœ“ Polymarket L2 keys configured. Click <strong>â†’ TRADE</strong> on any market to place an order.';
    notice.style.color = 'var(--green)';
    notice.style.borderColor = 'rgba(0,230,118,0.3)';
  }
}

// â”€â”€ Intel bar â”€â”€
async function loadIntelBar() {
  const [haltRes, sweepRes, earnRes] = await Promise.allSettled([
    fetch('/api/halts').then(r => r.json()),
    fetch('/api/options-flow').then(r => r.json()),
    fetch('/api/earnings').then(r => r.json()),
  ]);

  const haltsEl   = document.getElementById('ib-halts');
  const sweepEl   = document.getElementById('ib-sweep');
  const earningsEl = document.getElementById('ib-earnings');

  if (haltRes.status === 'fulfilled' && haltRes.value.ok) {
    const count = haltRes.value.halts?.length || 0;
    haltsEl.textContent = count > 0 ? `${count} ACTIVE` : '0';
    haltsEl.style.color = count > 0 ? 'var(--red)' : 'var(--green)';
  }

  if (sweepRes.status === 'fulfilled' && sweepRes.value.ok) {
    const top = sweepRes.value.sweeps?.[0];
    if (top) {
      const fmtPrem = top.premiumEst >= 1e6
        ? `$${(top.premiumEst/1e6).toFixed(1)}M`
        : `$${(top.premiumEst/1e3).toFixed(0)}K`;
      sweepEl.textContent = `${top.symbol} ${top.type.toUpperCase()} $${top.strike} [${fmtPrem}]`;
      sweepEl.style.color = top.type === 'call' ? 'var(--green)' : 'var(--red)';
    }
  }

  if (earnRes.status === 'fulfilled' && earnRes.value.ok) {
    const next = earnRes.value.earnings?.[0];
    if (next) {
      earningsEl.textContent = `${next.symbol} (${next.dayName} ${next.when.toUpperCase()})`;
    }
  }
}

// â”€â”€ Boot â”€â”€
loadMarkets('', '');
renderPinned();
updateKeyPanel();
loadIntelBar();
pinRefreshInterval = setInterval(refreshPinnedPrices, 10000);
setInterval(loadIntelBar, 60000);

<script>
const moneyFormat = val => {
  const n = Number(val);
  if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return "--";
  const sign = n < 0 ? "-" : "";
  return \`\${sign}$\${Math.abs(n).toFixed(2)}\`;
};

const pctFormat = val => Number.isFinite(Number(val)) ? \`\${Number(val).toFixed(1)}%\` : "--";

function renderPortfolio() {
  const paper = readJson("dtoPaperTradingAccount", { cash: 100000, startingCash: 100000, positions: [], log: [], realized: 0, quotes: {} });
  const journal = readJson("trades", []).map(t => ({
    id: t.id, time: t.date || new Date().toISOString(), symbol: t.ticker, side: t.dir, qty: t.shares, entry: t.entry, exit: t.exit, pnl: Number(t.pnl) || 0, source: 'journal'
  }));
  const paperLog = (paper.log || []).map((t,i) => ({
    id: \`paper-\${i}\`, time: t.time, symbol: t.symbol, side: t.action, qty: t.qty, entry: t.price, exit: t.exitPrice || t.price, pnl: Number(t.pnl) || 0, source: 'paper'
  }));
  
  const history = [...journal, ...paperLog].sort((a,b) => new Date(b.time) - new Date(a.time));
  
  let openPnl = 0;
  const positionsHtml = paper.positions.length ? paper.positions.map(p => {
    const currentPrice = paper.quotes?.[p.symbol]?.price || p.entry;
    const diff = currentPrice - p.entry;
    const unrealized = diff * p.qty * (p.side === "short" ? -1 : 1);
    openPnl += unrealized;
    return \`<tr>
      <td><strong>\${p.symbol}</strong></td>
      <td>\${p.side.toUpperCase()}</td>
      <td>\${p.qty}</td>
      <td>\${moneyFormat(p.entry)}</td>
      <td>\${moneyFormat(currentPrice)}</td>
      <td class="\${unrealized >= 0 ? 'green' : 'red'}">\${moneyFormat(unrealized)}</td>
      <td>Paper</td>
    </tr>\`;
  }).join("") : \`<tr><td colspan="7" class="muted" style="text-align:center">No open positions.</td></tr>\`;
  
  document.querySelector("#openPositionsTable tbody").innerHTML = positionsHtml;

  const historyHtml = history.length ? history.slice(0,50).map(t => \`
    <tr>
      <td>\${new Date(t.time).toLocaleDateString()} \${new Date(t.time).toLocaleTimeString([],{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'})}</td>
      <td><strong>\${t.symbol}</strong></td>
      <td>\${t.side.toUpperCase()}</td>
      <td>\${t.qty || '-'}</td>
      <td>\${moneyFormat(t.entry)}</td>
      <td>\${moneyFormat(t.exit)}</td>
      <td class="\${t.pnl >= 0 ? 'green' : 'red'}">\${moneyFormat(t.pnl)}</td>
      <td>\${t.source}</td>
    </tr>
  \`).join("") : \`<tr><td colspan="8" class="muted" style="text-align:center">No trade history.</td></tr>\`;
  
  document.querySelector("#closedTradesTable tbody").innerHTML = historyHtml;

  const realized = history.reduce((sum, t) => sum + (t.pnl || 0), 0);
  const totalEquity = paper.startingCash + realized + openPnl;
  const wins = history.filter(t => t.pnl > 0).length;

  document.getElementById("totalEquity").textContent = moneyFormat(totalEquity);
  document.getElementById("openPnl").textContent = moneyFormat(openPnl);
  document.getElementById("openPnl").className = openPnl >= 0 ? 'green' : 'red';
  document.getElementById("realizedPnl").textContent = moneyFormat(realized);
  document.getElementById("realizedPnl").className = realized >= 0 ? 'green' : 'red';
  document.getElementById("winRate").textContent = pctFormat(history.length ? (wins / history.length * 100) : 0);

  renderChart(history, paper.startingCash);
}

function renderChart(history, startingCash) {
  const ctx = document.getElementById('equityChart');
  if (window.equityChartInstance) window.equityChartInstance.destroy();
  
  const sorted = [...history].sort((a,b) => new Date(a.time) - new Date(b.time));
  let running = startingCash;
  const dataPoints = [{ x: sorted.length ? new Date(sorted[0].time).getTime() - 86400000 : Date.now() - 86400000, y: startingCash }];
  
  sorted.forEach(t => {
    running += t.pnl;
    dataPoints.push({ x: new Date(t.time).getTime(), y: running });
  });
  
  if (dataPoints.length === 1) {
    dataPoints.push({ x: Date.now(), y: startingCash });
  }

  const isLight = document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light';
  const gridColor = isLight ? 'rgba(0,0,0,0.05)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)';
  const textColor = isLight ? '#64748b' : '#8ea0ba';

  window.equityChartInstance = new Chart(ctx, {
    type: 'line',
    data: {
      datasets: [{
        label: 'Equity Curve',
        data: dataPoints,
        borderColor: '#00d7ff',
        backgroundColor: 'rgba(0, 215, 255, 0.1)',
        borderWidth: 2,
        fill: true,
        tension: 0.2,
        pointRadius: 0,
        pointHitRadius: 10
      }]
    },
    options: {
      responsive: true,
      maintainAspectRatio: false,
      plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
      scales: {
        x: { type: 'time', time: { unit: 'day' }, grid: { color: gridColor }, ticks: { color: textColor } },
        y: { grid: { color: gridColor }, ticks: { color: textColor, callback: v => '$'+v } }
      }
    }
  });
}

function readJson(key, fallback) {
  try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key)) || fallback; } catch { return fallback; }
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', renderPortfolio);
window.addEventListener('storage', e => { if (e.key === 'dtoPaperTradingAccount' || e.key === 'trades') renderPortfolio(); });

// Listen for theme changes to update chart colors
const originalSetAttribute = document.documentElement.setAttribute;
document.documentElement.setAttribute = function(name, value) {
  originalSetAttribute.call(this, name, value);
  if (name === 'data-theme') renderPortfolio();
};

      <form class="form-grid" id="ticketForm">
        <div class="field"><label for="symbol">Symbol</label><input id="symbol" value="AAPL"></div>

<script src="assets/daytrader-os.js?v=20260504-vercel1"></script>
<script>
const $ = id => document.getElementById(id);
const read = (key, fallback) => { try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || JSON.stringify(fallback)); } catch { return fallback; } };
const write = (key, value) => { localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(value)); return value; };
const clean = value => String(value || "").trim().toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9.-]/g, "");
const money = value => "$" + Number(value || 0).toFixed(2);
function account() { return read("dtoPaperTradingAccount", { cash: 100000, startingCash: 100000, positions: [], log: [], realized: 0, quotes: {} }); }
function saveAccount(next) { write("dtoPaperTradingAccount", next); renderAccount(); }
function renderAccount() {
  const acc = account();
  const openPnl = (acc.positions || []).reduce((sum, p) => sum + ((acc.quotes?.[p.symbol]?.price || p.entry || 0) - p.entry) * p.qty * (p.side === "short" ? -1 : 1), 0);
  $("cashOut").textContent = money(acc.cash || 0);
  $("pnlOut").textContent = money(openPnl);
  $("posOut").textContent = (acc.positions || []).length;
  $("equityOut").textContent = money((acc.cash || 0) + openPnl);
  $("positionsList").innerHTML = (acc.positions || []).length ? acc.positions.map(p => `<div class="row"><div><strong>${p.symbol}</strong><span>${p.side} / ${p.qty} @ ${money(p.entry)}</span></div><span>${money(((acc.quotes?.[p.symbol]?.price || p.entry) - p.entry) * p.qty * (p.side === "short" ? -1 : 1))}</span></div>`).join("") : `<div class="note">No open paper positions yet.</div>`;
}
function loadSetup() {
  const setup = window.DTO?.getSetup?.() || {};
  ["symbol","side","entry","stop","target"].forEach(key => {
    const id = key === "entry" ? "price" : key;
    if ($(id) && setup[key] !== undefined && setup[key] !== null) $(id).value = setup[key];
  });
}
$("ticketForm").addEventListener("submit", event => {
  event.preventDefault();
  const acc = account();
  const symbol = clean($("symbol").value), side = $("side").value, qty = Number($("qty").value), price = Number($("price").value);
  if (!symbol || !qty || !price) { $("ticketNote").textContent = "Add symbol, quantity, and price first."; return; }
  const cost = qty * price;
  const position = { symbol, side, qty, entry: price, stop: Number($("stop").value) || null, target: Number($("target").value) || null, openedAt: new Date().toISOString() };
  acc.positions = [position, ...(acc.positions || [])];
  acc.cash = side === "long" ? (acc.cash || 0) - cost : (acc.cash || 0);
  acc.log = [{ action: "open", symbol, side, qty, price, time: new Date().toISOString() }, ...(acc.log || [])].slice(0, 100);
  acc.quotes = { ...(acc.quotes || {}), [symbol]: { price, prev: price, time: new Date().toISOString() } };
  saveAccount(acc);
  $("ticketNote").textContent = `${symbol} paper trade opened. Review it after the session.`;
});
$("loadSetup").addEventListener("click", loadSetup);
$("challengeForm").addEventListener("submit", event => {
  event.preventDefault();
  const item = { symbol: clean($("challengeSymbol").value), type: $("challengeType").value, duration: $("duration").value, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() };
  write("dtoReplayChallenges", [item, ...read("dtoReplayChallenges", [])].slice(0, 20));
  renderChallenges();
  $("openBacktest").href = `backtest_simulator.html?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(item.symbol)}`;
});
function renderChallenges() {
  const list = read("dtoReplayChallenges", []);
  $("challengeList").innerHTML = list.length ? list.slice(0, 5).map(item => `<div class="row"><div><strong>${item.symbol}</strong><span>${item.type} / ${item.duration}</span></div><a class="btn" href="backtest_simulator.html?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(item.symbol)}">Replay</a></div>`).join("") : `<div class="note">No replay challenges saved yet.</div>`;
}
loadSetup();
renderAccount();
renderChallenges();
</script>
</body>
</html>
