<script>
let watchlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('watchlist') || '[]');
let notes = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('prepNotes') || '{}');

// Restore notes
['mktNotes','gamePlan','eodNotes'].forEach(id => {
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el && notes[id]) el.value = notes[id];
  if (el) el.addEventListener('input', () => {
    notes[id] = el.value;
    localStorage.setItem('prepNotes', JSON.stringify(notes));
  });
});

// Clock & market status
function updateClock() {
  const now = new Date();
  const et = new Date(now.toLocaleString('en-US', { timeZone: 'America/New_York' }));
  const h = et.getHours(), m = et.getMinutes(), s = et.getSeconds();
  const pad = n => String(n).padStart(2,'0');
  document.getElementById('clock').textContent = `${pad(h)}:${pad(m)}:${pad(s)} ET`;

  const statusEl = document.getElementById('marketStatus');
  const mins = h * 60 + m;
  if (mins >= 240 && mins < 570) {
    statusEl.textContent = 'PRE-MARKET';
    statusEl.className = 'market-status status-pre';
  } else if (mins >= 570 && mins < 960) {
    statusEl.textContent = 'MARKET OPEN';
    statusEl.className = 'market-status status-open';
  } else {
    statusEl.textContent = 'MARKET CLOSED';
    statusEl.className = 'market-status status-closed';
  }
}

setInterval(updateClock, 1000);
updateClock();

// Checklist
function toggleCheck(item) {
  item.classList.toggle('done');
  updateProgress();
}

function updateProgress() {
  const sections = [
    { items: document.querySelectorAll('.section:nth-of-type(2) .check-item'), prog: 'prog1' },
    { items: document.querySelectorAll('.section:nth-of-type(3) .check-item'), prog: 'prog2' },
    { items: document.querySelectorAll('.section:nth-of-type(4) .check-item'), prog: 'prog3' },
  ];

  sections.forEach(s => {
    if (!s.items.length) return;
    const done = [...s.items].filter(i => i.classList.contains('done')).length;
    const pill = document.getElementById(s.prog);
    if (pill) pill.textContent = `${done}/${s.items.length}`;
  });
}

function resetAll() {
  document.querySelectorAll('.check-item').forEach(i => i.classList.remove('done'));
  updateProgress();
}

// Watchlist
function addWatch() {
  const ticker = document.getElementById('wlTicker').value.toUpperCase().trim();
  if (!ticker) return;
  watchlist.push({ id: Date.now(), ticker, support:'', resistance:'', bias:'LONG', catalyst:'', level:'', notes:'' });
  document.getElementById('wlTicker').value = '';
  saveAndRender();
}

document.getElementById('wlTicker').addEventListener('keypress', e => {
  if (e.key === 'Enter') addWatch();
});

function removeWatch(id) {
  watchlist = watchlist.filter(w => w.id !== id);
  saveAndRender();
}

function updateWatch(id, field, val) {
  const w = watchlist.find(w => w.id === id);
  if (w) { w[field] = val; localStorage.setItem('watchlist', JSON.stringify(watchlist)); }
}

function saveAndRender() {
  localStorage.setItem('watchlist', JSON.stringify(watchlist));
  renderWatchlist();
}

function renderWatchlist() {
  const el = document.getElementById('watchlistContainer');
  if (!watchlist.length) {
    el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-wl">No stocks added yet.<br>Enter a ticker above to build your watchlist.<br><br>Aim for 3â€“5 high-conviction setups only.</div>';
    return;
  }

  el.innerHTML = watchlist.map(w => `
    <div class="wl-card">
      <div>
        <div class="wl-ticker">${w.ticker}</div>
        <div class="bias-badge bias-${w.bias.toLowerCase()}" style="margin-top:8px;">${w.bias}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="wl-fields">
        <div class="wl-field">
          <label>Support $</label>
          <input type="text" value="${w.support}" placeholder="172.50" oninput="updateWatch(${w.id},'support',this.value)">
        </div>
        <div class="wl-field">
          <label>Resistance $</label>
          <input type="text" value="${w.resistance}" placeholder="178.00" oninput="updateWatch(${w.id},'resistance',this.value)">
        </div>
        <div class="wl-field">
          <label>Bias</label>
          <select onchange="updateWatch(${w.id},'bias',this.value)">
            <option ${w.bias==='LONG'?'selected':''}>LONG</option>
            <option ${w.bias==='SHORT'?'selected':''}>SHORT</option>
            <option ${w.bias==='NEUTRAL'?'selected':''}>NEUTRAL</option>
          </select>
        </div>
        <div class="wl-field">
          <label>Catalyst</label>
          <input type="text" value="${w.catalyst}" placeholder="Earnings gap, breakout..." oninput="updateWatch(${w.id},'catalyst',this.value)">
        </div>
        <div class="wl-field full">
          <label>Notes / Entry Plan</label>
          <textarea oninput="updateWatch(${w.id},'notes',this.value)" placeholder="Buy breakout above resistance with volume...">${w.notes}</textarea>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="wl-actions">
        <button class="wl-delete" onclick="removeWatch(${w.id})">âœ•</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  `).join('');
}

renderWatchlist();
updateProgress();
</script>

<script src="assets/daytrader-os.js?v=20260504-vercel1"></script>
<script>
const $ = id => document.getElementById(id);
const read = (key, fallback) => { try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || JSON.stringify(fallback)); } catch { return fallback; } };
const write = (key, value) => { localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(value)); return value; };
const clean = value => String(value || "").trim().toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9.-]/g, "");
const money = value => "$" + Number(value || 0).toFixed(2);
function reviews() { return read("dtoReviewRoomTrades", []); }
function pnl(t) { const mult = t.side === "short" ? -1 : 1; return (t.exit - t.entry) * t.qty * mult; }
function renderStats() {
  const list = reviews();
  const net = list.reduce((sum, t) => sum + pnl(t), 0);
  const wins = list.filter(t => pnl(t) > 0).length;
  const avgDisc = list.length ? list.reduce((sum, t) => sum + Number(t.discipline || 0), 0) / list.length : null;
  $("tradeCount").textContent = list.length;
  $("netPnl").textContent = money(net);
  $("winRate").textContent = list.length ? Math.round(wins / list.length * 100) + "%" : "--";
  $("avgDiscipline").textContent = avgDisc ? avgDisc.toFixed(1) : "--";
  const mistakes = list.filter(t => t.mistake && t.mistake !== "None").map(t => t.mistake);
  const topMistake = mistakes.sort((a, b) => mistakes.filter(x => x === b).length - mistakes.filter(x => x === a).length)[0];
  $("coachNote").textContent = topMistake ? `Repeat mistake to attack next: ${topMistake}. Build tomorrow's rule around that.` : "No repeat mistake detected yet. Keep logging.";
  $("reviewList").innerHTML = list.length ? list.slice(0, 8).map(t => `<div class="row"><div><strong>${t.symbol}</strong><span>${t.setup} / ${t.mistake} / discipline ${t.discipline}/10</span></div><span>${money(pnl(t))}</span></div>`).join("") : `<div class="note">No reviewed trades yet.</div>`;
}
function renderRules() {
  const list = read("dtoAccountabilityRules", []);
  $("ruleList").innerHTML = list.length ? list.slice(0, 5).map(r => `<div class="row"><div><strong>${r.rule}</strong><span>Max loss ${money(r.maxLoss)} / state ${r.emotion}</span></div><span>${new Date(r.savedAt).toLocaleDateString()}</span></div>`).join("") : `<div class="note">No daily rule saved yet.</div>`;
}
function loadSetup() {
  const setup = window.DTO?.getSetup?.() || {};
  if (setup.symbol) $("symbol").value = setup.symbol;
  if (setup.side) $("side").value = setup.side;
  if (setup.entry) $("entry").value = setup.entry;
  if (setup.target) $("exit").value = setup.target;
  if (setup.setupType) $("setup").value = setup.setupType;
}
$("journalForm").addEventListener("submit", event => {
  event.preventDefault();
  const trade = { symbol: clean($("symbol").value), side: $("side").value, qty: Number($("qty").value), setup: $("setup").value, entry: Number($("entry").value), exit: Number($("exit").value), discipline: Number($("discipline").value), mistake: $("mistake").value, notes: $("notes").value, savedAt: new Date().toISOString() };
  if (!trade.symbol || !trade.qty || !trade.entry || !trade.exit) { $("coachNote").textContent = "Add symbol, qty, entry, and exit first."; return; }
  write("dtoReviewRoomTrades", [trade, ...reviews()].slice(0, 100));
  window.DTO?.recordTrade?.({ symbol: trade.symbol, side: trade.side, qty: trade.qty, entry: trade.entry, exit: trade.exit, pnl: pnl(trade), setupType: trade.setup, mistake: trade.mistake, notes: trade.notes });
  renderStats();
});
$("ruleForm").addEventListener("submit", event => {
  event.preventDefault();
  const item = { maxLoss: Number($("maxLoss").value), emotion: $("emotion").value, rule: $("rule").value || "Trade only the plan", savedAt: new Date().toISOString() };
  write("dtoAccountabilityRules", [item, ...read("dtoAccountabilityRules", [])].slice(0, 20));
  renderRules();
});
$("loadSetup").addEventListener("click", loadSetup);
loadSetup();
renderStats();
renderRules();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
function updateRiskLabel() {
  const v = document.getElementById('riskPct').value;
  document.getElementById('riskPctLabel').textContent = `${parseFloat(v).toFixed(2)}%`;
  // Update risk meter color
  const fill = document.getElementById('riskFill');
  const pct = (v - 0.25) / (5 - 0.25) * 100;
  const color = v <= 1 ? '#00e676' : v <= 2 ? '#f0b429' : '#ff1744';
  fill.style.width = `${pct}%`;
  fill.style.background = color;
}

function calc() {
  const account = parseFloat(document.getElementById('account').value) || 0;
  const riskPct = parseFloat(document.getElementById('riskPct').value) / 100;
  const entry = parseFloat(document.getElementById('entry').value) || 0;
  const stop = parseFloat(document.getElementById('stop').value) || 0;
  const target = parseFloat(document.getElementById('target').value) || 0;

  if (!account || !entry || !stop || !target || stop === entry || target === entry) {
    return;
  }

  const isShort = stop > entry || target < entry;
  const dollarRisk = account * riskPct;
  const riskPerShare = Math.abs(entry - stop);
  const profitPerShare = isShort ? entry - target : target - entry;
  if (profitPerShare <= 0) return;
  const shares = Math.floor(dollarRisk / riskPerShare);
  const totalRisk = shares * riskPerShare;
  const totalProfit = shares * profitPerShare;
  const rr = profitPerShare / riskPerShare;
  const positionValue = shares * entry;
  const positionPct = (positionValue / account) * 100;
  const dailyLimit = account * 0.03;
  const tradesLeft = Math.floor(dailyLimit / dollarRisk);

  // Outputs
  document.getElementById('outShares').textContent = shares.toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById('outRisk').textContent = `$${totalRisk.toFixed(0)}`;
  document.getElementById('outProfit').textContent = `$${totalProfit.toFixed(0)}`;
  document.getElementById('outRR').textContent = `${rr.toFixed(2)}x`;
  document.getElementById('outRRSub').textContent = rr >= 2 ? 'âœ“ Good setup' : 'âš  Below 2:1 target';
  document.getElementById('outPosition').textContent = `$${positionValue.toFixed(0)}`;
  document.getElementById('outPct').textContent = `${positionPct.toFixed(1)}%`;
  document.getElementById('outSharesSub').textContent = `$${dollarRisk.toFixed(0)} risked (${(riskPct*100).toFixed(2)}%)`;

  // Breakdown
  document.getElementById('bEntry').textContent = `$${entry.toFixed(2)}`;
  document.getElementById('bStop').textContent = `$${stop.toFixed(2)}`;
  document.getElementById('bRiskPerShare').textContent = `-$${riskPerShare.toFixed(2)}/share`;
  document.getElementById('bTarget').textContent = `$${target.toFixed(2)}`;
  document.getElementById('bProfitPerShare').textContent = `+$${profitPerShare.toFixed(2)}/share`;
  document.getElementById('bDailyLimit').textContent = `-$${dailyLimit.toFixed(0)}`;
  document.getElementById('bTradesLeft').textContent = `${tradesLeft} losing trades`;

  // Scenarios
  const scenarios = [
    { label: '5 Wins', seq: 'W-W-W-W-W', count: [5, 0] },
    { label: '4W / 1L', seq: 'W-W-W-W-L', count: [4, 1] },
    { label: '3W / 2L', seq: 'W-W-W-L-L', count: [3, 2] },
    { label: '2W / 3L', seq: 'W-W-L-L-L', count: [2, 3] },
    { label: '1W / 4L', seq: 'W-L-L-L-L', count: [1, 4] },
    { label: '5 Losses', seq: 'L-L-L-L-L', count: [0, 5] },
  ];

  const fmt = (n) => n >= 0 ? `<span style="color:var(--green)">+$${n.toFixed(2)}</span>` : `<span style="color:var(--red)">-$${Math.abs(n).toFixed(2)}</span>`;
  const fmtAcc = (n) => n >= account ? `<span style="color:var(--green)">$${n.toFixed(2)}</span>` : `<span style="color:var(--red)">$${n.toFixed(2)}</span>`;

  document.getElementById('scenarioBody').innerHTML = scenarios.map(s => {
    const net = (s.count[0] * totalProfit) - (s.count[1] * totalRisk);
    const newAcc = account + net;
    return `<tr>
      <td style="color:var(--gold)">${s.label}</td>
      <td style="color:var(--muted)">${s.seq}</td>
      <td>${fmt(net)}</td>
      <td>${fmtAcc(newAcc)}</td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}

function readLastSetup() {
  try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('dtoLastSetup') || 'null'); }
  catch(e) { return null; }
}

function loadSetupPrefill() {
  const params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
  const saved = readLastSetup() || {};
  const setup = { ...saved };
  ['symbol','side','rating','entry','stop','target'].forEach(key => {
    if (params.has(key)) setup[key] = params.get(key);
  });
  if (setup.entry) document.getElementById('entry').value = Number(setup.entry);
  if (setup.stop) document.getElementById('stop').value = Number(setup.stop);
  if (setup.target) document.getElementById('target').value = Number(setup.target);
  const title = document.querySelector('.top-title');
  if (title && setup.symbol) {
    title.textContent = `RISK CALCULATOR / ${String(setup.symbol).toUpperCase()}`;
  }
}

var currentSetup = {};

function cleanSymbol(value) {
  return String(value || '').trim().toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9.-]/g, '');
}

function detectAssetType(symbol) {
  const clean = cleanSymbol(symbol).replace(/[.-]/g, '');
  const crypto = new Set(['BTC','XBT','ETH','SOL','DOGE','XRP','BNB','AVAX','LINK','SUI','PEPE','SHIB','ADA','LTC','BCH','DOT','MATIC','POL','UNI','AAVE','ATOM','NEAR','OP','ARB','FIL','ETC','TRX','XLM','HBAR','ICP','INJ','APT']);
  if (crypto.has(clean)) return 'crypto';
  if (/^[A-Z0-9]{2,12}(USD|USDT)$/.test(clean)) return 'crypto';
  return 'stock';
}

function money(value, decimals = 2) {
  const n = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return '$--';
  return '$' + n.toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: decimals, maximumFractionDigits: decimals });
}

function qtyPrecision(assetType, price) {
  if (assetType !== 'crypto') return 0;
  if (price >= 10000) return 6;
  if (price >= 1) return 5;
  return 8;
}

function fmtQty(value, assetType, price) {
  const n = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return '--';
  const decimals = qtyPrecision(assetType, price);
  return n.toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: decimals, maximumFractionDigits: decimals });
}

function setText(id, value) {
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el) el.textContent = value;
}

function updateRiskLabel() {
  const v = Number(document.getElementById('riskPct').value) || 0;
  setText('riskPctLabel', `${v.toFixed(2)}%`);
  const fill = document.getElementById('riskFill');
  const pct = ((v - 0.25) / (5 - 0.25)) * 100;
  const color = v <= 1 ? '#00e676' : v <= 2 ? '#f0b429' : '#ff1744';
  fill.style.width = `${Math.max(0, Math.min(100, pct))}%`;
  fill.style.background = color;
}

function readSetupFromUrl() {
  const params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
  const saved = readLastSetup() || {};
  const setup = { ...saved };
  ['symbol','side','rating','entry','stop','target','support','resistance','rr','thesis'].forEach(key => {
    if (params.has(key)) setup[key] = params.get(key);
  });
  return setup;
}

function loadSetupPrefill() {
  currentSetup = readSetupFromUrl();
  if (currentSetup.entry) document.getElementById('entry').value = Number(currentSetup.entry);
  if (currentSetup.stop) document.getElementById('stop').value = Number(currentSetup.stop);
  if (currentSetup.target) document.getElementById('target').value = Number(currentSetup.target);
  const title = document.querySelector('.top-title');
  if (title && currentSetup.symbol) {
    title.textContent = `RISK CALCULATOR / ${cleanSymbol(currentSetup.symbol)}`;
  }
}

function clearOutputs(message) {
  ['outShares','outRisk','outProfit','outRR','outPosition','outPct','bEntry','bStop','bRiskPerShare','bTarget','bProfitPerShare','bDailyLimit','bTradesLeft'].forEach(id => setText(id, '--'));
  setText('outSharesSub', 'Fix setup inputs first');
  setText('outRiskSub', 'No valid stop');
  setText('outProfitSub', 'No valid target');
  setText('outRRSub', 'Risk to reward');
  const scenarios = document.getElementById('scenarioBody');
  if (scenarios) scenarios.innerHTML = '';
  renderTips([{ text: message || 'Add account size, entry, stop, and a valid target to calculate risk.', type: 'bad' }]);
}

function buildSizing({ account, riskPct, entry, stop, target, symbol, side }) {
  const assetType = detectAssetType(symbol);
  const intendedRisk = account * riskPct;
  const riskPerUnit = Math.abs(entry - stop);
  const isShort = side === 'short' || stop > entry || target < entry;
  const profitPerUnit = isShort ? entry - target : target - entry;
  if (!account || !entry || !stop || !target || stop === entry) return { error: 'Entry, stop, and target are required, and stop cannot equal entry.' };
  if (profitPerUnit <= 0) return { error: isShort ? 'For a short setup, target must be below entry.' : 'For a long setup, target must be above entry.' };
  if (!riskPerUnit || !intendedRisk) return { error: 'Account size and risk percent must be above zero.' };

  const rawQty = intendedRisk / riskPerUnit;
  const decimals = qtyPrecision(assetType, entry);
  const qty = assetType === 'crypto' ? Number(rawQty.toFixed(decimals)) : Math.floor(rawQty);
  const cashLimitedRaw = account / entry;
  const cashLimitedQty = assetType === 'crypto' ? Number(cashLimitedRaw.toFixed(decimals)) : Math.floor(cashLimitedRaw);
  const actualRisk = qty * riskPerUnit;
  const totalProfit = qty * profitPerUnit;
  const rr = profitPerUnit / riskPerUnit;
  const positionValue = qty * entry;
  const positionPct = (positionValue / account) * 100;
  const riskEfficiency = intendedRisk ? (actualRisk / intendedRisk) * 100 : 0;
  return { assetType, intendedRisk, riskPerUnit, profitPerUnit, rawQty, qty, cashLimitedQty, actualRisk, totalProfit, rr, positionValue, positionPct, riskEfficiency, isShort };
}

function renderTips(tips) {
  const el = document.getElementById('tipsList');
  if (!el) return;
  el.innerHTML = tips.map(tip => `<div class="rule-line ${tip.type || ''}">${tip.text}</div>`).join('');
}

function tipsForSizing(result, inputs) {
  const tips = [];
  const symbol = cleanSymbol(inputs.symbol || 'SETUP') || 'SETUP';
  if (result.assetType === 'crypto') {
    tips.push({ type: 'good', text: `${symbol} detected as crypto: fractional units enabled, so the risk slider can size below 1 full coin/token.` });
  } else {
    tips.push({ text: `${symbol} detected as stock/ETF: whole-share sizing is used, so actual risk can be below intended risk after rounding.` });
  }
  if (result.rr < 2) {
    tips.push({ type: 'bad', text: `R:R is only ${result.rr.toFixed(2)}R. This setup needs a tighter stop, farther target, or a no-trade decision.` });
  } else {
    tips.push({ type: 'good', text: `R:R is ${result.rr.toFixed(2)}R, which clears the 2R planning threshold.` });
  }
  if ((inputs.riskPct * 100) > 2) {
    tips.push({ type: 'warn', text: `Risk slider is at ${(inputs.riskPct * 100).toFixed(2)}%, which is aggressive for repeated intraday attempts.` });
  }
  if (result.positionValue > inputs.account) {
    tips.push({ type: 'warn', text: `Risk-sized notional is ${money(result.positionValue)}, above the ${money(inputs.account)} account. That requires leverage, margin, or lower size.` });
    tips.push({ text: `Cash-limited reference size is ${fmtQty(result.cashLimitedQty, result.assetType, inputs.entry)} ${result.assetType === 'crypto' ? 'units' : 'shares'}.` });
  }
  if (result.riskEfficiency < 85) {
    tips.push({ type: 'warn', text: `Actual risk uses ${result.riskEfficiency.toFixed(0)}% of intended risk because of sizing constraints. The setup is under-risked versus the slider.` });
  } else if (result.assetType === 'crypto') {
    tips.push({ type: 'good', text: `Fractional sizing is efficient: actual risk is ${money(result.actualRisk)} vs intended ${money(result.intendedRisk)}.` });
  }
  if (inputs.thesis) {
    tips.push({ text: `Imported thesis: ${String(inputs.thesis).slice(0, 150)}${String(inputs.thesis).length > 150 ? '...' : ''}` });
  }
  return tips.slice(0, 6);
}

function calc() {
  const account = Number(document.getElementById('account').value) || 0;
  const riskPct = (Number(document.getElementById('riskPct').value) || 0) / 100;
  const entry = Number(document.getElementById('entry').value) || 0;
  const stop = Number(document.getElementById('stop').value) || 0;
  const target = Number(document.getElementById('target').value) || 0;
  const symbol = cleanSymbol(currentSetup.symbol || new URLSearchParams(location.search).get('symbol') || 'STOCK');
  const side = String(currentSetup.side || '').toLowerCase();
  const result = buildSizing({ account, riskPct, entry, stop, target, symbol, side });

  if (result.error) {
    clearOutputs(result.error);
    return;
  }

  const unitWord = result.assetType === 'crypto' ? 'units' : 'shares';
  const dailyLimit = account * 0.03;
  const tradesLeft = result.intendedRisk ? Math.floor(dailyLimit / result.intendedRisk) : 0;
  const cashPressure = result.positionValue > account;

  setText('qtyLabel', result.assetType === 'crypto' ? 'Crypto Units' : 'Shares to Buy');
  setText('modeNote', `${symbol} detected as ${result.assetType}. ${result.assetType === 'crypto' ? 'Fractional units enabled.' : 'Whole-share rounding enabled.'} Direction: ${result.isShort ? 'SHORT' : 'LONG'}.`);
  setText('outShares', fmtQty(result.qty, result.assetType, entry));
  setText('outRisk', money(result.actualRisk));
  setText('outProfit', money(result.totalProfit));
  setText('outRR', `${result.rr.toFixed(2)}x`);
  setText('outPosition', money(result.positionValue, 0));
  setText('outPct', `${result.positionPct.toFixed(1)}%`);
  setText('outSharesSub', `${money(result.intendedRisk)} intended risk / ${fmtQty(result.rawQty, result.assetType, entry)} raw ${unitWord}`);
  setText('outRiskSub', `${result.riskEfficiency.toFixed(0)}% of slider risk used`);
  setText('outProfitSub', `If target is hit before fees/slippage`);
  setText('outRRSub', result.rr >= 2 ? 'Good setup by R:R' : 'Below 2R target');
  setText('bEntry', money(entry));
  setText('bStop', money(stop));
  setText('bRiskPerShare', `-${money(result.riskPerUnit).replace('$','$')}/${unitWord.slice(0, -1) || 'unit'}`);
  setText('bTarget', money(target));
  setText('bProfitPerShare', `+${money(result.profitPerUnit).replace('$','$')}/${unitWord.slice(0, -1) || 'unit'}`);
  setText('bDailyLimit', `-${money(dailyLimit).replace('$','$')}`);
  setText('bTradesLeft', `${tradesLeft} slider-risk losses`);

  const positionCard = document.getElementById('outPosition')?.closest('.out-card');
  if (positionCard) positionCard.style.borderColor = cashPressure ? 'var(--red)' : 'var(--border)';

  renderTips(tipsForSizing(result, { account, riskPct, entry, symbol, thesis: currentSetup.thesis }));

  const scenarios = [
    { label: '5 Wins', seq: 'W-W-W-W-W', count: [5, 0] },
    { label: '4W / 1L', seq: 'W-W-W-W-L', count: [4, 1] },
    { label: '3W / 2L', seq: 'W-W-W-L-L', count: [3, 2] },
    { label: '2W / 3L', seq: 'W-W-L-L-L', count: [2, 3] },
    { label: '1W / 4L', seq: 'W-L-L-L-L', count: [1, 4] },
    { label: '5 Losses', seq: 'L-L-L-L-L', count: [0, 5] },
  ];
  const fmt = n => n >= 0 ? `<span style="color:var(--green)">+${money(n)}</span>` : `<span style="color:var(--red)">-${money(Math.abs(n)).replace('$','')}</span>`;
  const fmtAcc = n => n >= account ? `<span style="color:var(--green)">${money(n)}</span>` : `<span style="color:var(--red)">${money(n)}</span>`;
  document.getElementById('scenarioBody').innerHTML = scenarios.map(s => {
    const net = (s.count[0] * result.totalProfit) - (s.count[1] * result.actualRisk);
    const newAcc = account + net;
    return `<tr>
      <td style="color:var(--gold)">${s.label}</td>
      <td style="color:var(--muted)">${s.seq}</td>
      <td>${fmt(net)}</td>
      <td>${fmtAcc(newAcc)}</td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}

loadSetupPrefill();
updateRiskLabel();
calc();
</script>

<script src="assets/daytrader-os.js?v=20260504-vercel1"></script>
<script>
const STORAGE_KEY = "dtoScannerWatchlist";
const STOCKS = ["AAPL","TSLA","NVDA","AMD","META","MSFT","SPY","QQQ"];
const CRYPTOS = ["BTC","ETH","SOL","DOGE","XRP","BNB","LINK","SUI"];

function readJson(key, fallback) {
  try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || JSON.stringify(fallback)); }
  catch (error) { return fallback; }
}

function writeJson(key, value) {
  localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(value));
  return value;
}

function safeDTO() {
  return window.DTO || {
    escapeHtml: value => String(value ?? "").replace(/[&<>"']/g, ch => ({ "&":"&amp;", "<":"&lt;", ">":"&gt;", '"':"&quot;", "'":"&#39;" }[ch])),
    saveSetup: setup => {
      localStorage.setItem("dtoSetupPacket", JSON.stringify(setup));
      localStorage.setItem("dtoLastSetup", JSON.stringify(setup));
      return setup;
    },
    getSetup: () => readJson("dtoSetupPacket", null),
    workflowUrl: (page, setup) => `${page}?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(setup?.symbol || "")}`,
    renderMissionControl: () => {}
  };
}

function saved() {
  return readJson(STORAGE_KEY, []);
}

function cleanSymbol(value) {
  return String(value || "").trim().toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9.-]/g, "");
}

function saveCandidate() {
  const dto = safeDTO();
  const symbol = cleanSymbol(document.getElementById("symbol").value);
  const setupType = document.getElementById("setupType").value;
  const level = document.getElementById("level").value;
  const note = document.getElementById("note").value.trim();
  const status = document.getElementById("saveStatus");

  if (!symbol) {
    status.textContent = "Add a symbol first.";
    status.style.color = "#ff5b6e";
    return;
  }

  const item = { symbol, setupType, level, note, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() };
  const next = [item, ...saved().filter(existing => existing.symbol !== symbol)].slice(0, 50);
  writeJson(STORAGE_KEY, next);
  dto.saveSetup({
    symbol,
    rating: "CHECK",
    thesis: note || `${setupType} scanner candidate. Confirm volume, catalyst, support, and resistance before trading.`,
    catalysts: note ? [note] : [],
    sourcePage: "scanner_hub.html",
    createdAt: item.createdAt
  });

  status.style.color = "#00e08a";
  status.textContent = `${symbol} saved to scanner watchlist.`;
  render();
  dto.renderMissionControl();
}

function openSymbol(symbol) {
  const dto = safeDTO();
  const match = saved().find(item => item.symbol === symbol);
  const setup = dto.saveSetup({
    symbol,
    rating: "CHECK",
    thesis: match?.note || "Scanner candidate. Confirm volume, catalyst, and levels before trading.",
    catalysts: match?.note ? [match.note] : [],
    sourcePage: "scanner_hub.html"
  });
  location.href = dto.workflowUrl("index.html", setup);
}

function renderSymbolButtons(targetId, symbols) {
  const dto = safeDTO();
  document.getElementById(targetId).innerHTML = symbols.map(symbol => `<button type="button" data-open-symbol="${dto.escapeHtml(symbol)}">${dto.escapeHtml(symbol)}</button>`).join("");
}

function renderSavedList() {
  const dto = safeDTO();
  const list = saved();
  document.getElementById("savedList").innerHTML = list.length ? list.map(item => `
    <div class="saved-card">
      <strong>${dto.escapeHtml(item.symbol)}</strong>
      <span>${dto.escapeHtml(item.setupType || "Watch")} ${item.level ? "/ level " + dto.escapeHtml(item.level) : ""}</span>
      <span>${dto.escapeHtml(item.note || "No note yet.")}</span>
      <div class="card-actions">
        <button type="button" data-open-symbol="${dto.escapeHtml(item.symbol)}">Analyze</button>
        <a href="${dto.workflowUrl("guided_trade_builder.html", item)}">Trade Builder</a>
      </div>
    </div>`).join("") : `<p class="empty">No symbols saved yet. Add one above and it will appear here instantly.</p>`;
}

function render() {
  renderSavedList();
  renderSymbolButtons("stockList", STOCKS);
  renderSymbolButtons("cryptoList", CRYPTOS);
  document.querySelectorAll("[data-open-symbol]").forEach(button => {
    button.addEventListener("click", () => openSymbol(button.dataset.openSymbol));
  });
}

document.getElementById("saveScannerBtn").addEventListener("click", saveCandidate);
document.getElementById("scanForm").addEventListener("submit", event => {
  event.preventDefault();
  saveCandidate();
});
document.getElementById("symbol").addEventListener("keydown", event => {
  if (event.key === "Enter") {
    event.preventDefault();
    saveCandidate();
  }
});

render();
safeDTO().renderMissionControl();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
let watched = [];
let signalCache = {};
let focusedSymbol = '';
const SCANNER_SYMBOLS = ['SPY','QQQ','AAPL','TSLA','NVDA','AMD','META','MSFT','BTC','ETH','SOL','DOGE'];
const TIMEFRAMES = [
  {label:'15M', interval:'15m', limit:120},
  {label:'1H', interval:'1h', limit:160},
  {label:'4H', interval:'4h', limit:160},
  {label:'1D', interval:'1d', limit:180}
];
const CRYPTO_DATA = {
  BTC:'BTCUSDT',XBT:'BTCUSDT',BITCOIN:'BTCUSDT',ETH:'ETHUSDT',ETHEREUM:'ETHUSDT',
  SOL:'SOLUSDT',SOLANA:'SOLUSDT',DOGE:'DOGEUSDT',DOGECOIN:'DOGEUSDT',
  XRP:'XRPUSDT',ADA:'ADAUSDT',CARDANO:'ADAUSDT',BNB:'BNBUSDT',
  AVAX:'AVAXUSDT',AVALANCHE:'AVAXUSDT',LINK:'LINKUSDT',CHAINLINK:'LINKUSDT',
  LTC:'LTCUSDT',LITECOIN:'LTCUSDT',BCH:'BCHUSDT',DOT:'DOTUSDT',POLKADOT:'DOTUSDT',
  MATIC:'MATICUSDT',POLYGON:'MATICUSDT',POL:'POLUSDT',UNI:'UNIUSDT',
  AAVE:'AAVEUSDT',ATOM:'ATOMUSDT',COSMOS:'ATOMUSDT',NEAR:'NEARUSDT',
  OP:'OPUSDT',OPTIMISM:'OPUSDT',ARB:'ARBUSDT',ARBITRUM:'ARBUSDT',
  FIL:'FILUSDT',FILECOIN:'FILUSDT',ETC:'ETCUSDT',TRX:'TRXUSDT',
  XLM:'XLMUSDT',STELLAR:'XLMUSDT',HBAR:'HBARUSDT',ICP:'ICPUSDT',
  INJ:'INJUSDT',SUI:'SUIUSDT',APT:'APTUSDT',APTOS:'APTUSDT',
  PEPE:'PEPEUSDT',SHIB:'SHIBUSDT',WIF:'WIFUSDT',BONK:'BONKUSDT',
  FET:'FETUSDT',RENDER:'RENDERUSDT',RNDR:'RENDERUSDT',TAO:'TAOUSDT'
};
function cryptoPairFor(raw){
  let key=String(raw||'').trim().toUpperCase();
  key=key.replace(/^BINANCE:/,'').replace(/[-/_\s]/g,'');
  if(CRYPTO_DATA[key]) return CRYPTO_DATA[key];
  if(/^[A-Z0-9]{2,12}USDT$/.test(key)) return key;
  if(/^[A-Z0-9]{2,12}USD$/.test(key)) return key.replace(/USD$/,'USDT');
  return null;
}
function cryptoBaseFor(raw){
  const pair=cryptoPairFor(raw);
  return pair ? pair.replace(/USDT$/,'') : null;
}

// â”€â”€ CLOCK â”€â”€
function updateClock() {
  const et = new Date(new Date().toLocaleString('en-US',{timeZone:'America/New_York'}));
  const [h,m,s] = [et.getHours(),et.getMinutes(),et.getSeconds()];
  const p = n => String(n).padStart(2,'0');
  document.getElementById('clock').textContent = `${p(h)}:${p(m)}:${p(s)} ET`;
  const pill = document.getElementById('marketPill');
  const mins = h*60+m, wd = et.getDay();
  if(wd===0||wd===6){pill.textContent='WEEKEND';pill.className='market-pill pill-closed';}
  else if(mins>=240&&mins<570){pill.textContent='PRE-MARKET';pill.className='market-pill pill-pre';}
  else if(mins>=570&&mins<960){pill.textContent='â— OPEN';pill.className='market-pill pill-open';}
  else if(mins>=960&&mins<1200){pill.textContent='AFTER-HRS';pill.className='market-pill pill-after';}
  else{pill.textContent='CLOSED';pill.className='market-pill pill-closed';}
}
setInterval(updateClock,1000); updateClock();

// â”€â”€ CLAUDE API â”€â”€
function cleanSymbol(s){return String(s||'AAPL').trim().toUpperCase().replace(/^BINANCE:/,'').replace(/[^A-Z0-9.\-/_\s]/g,'').trim()||'AAPL';}
function displaySymbol(s){return cleanSymbol(s).replace(/[-/_\s]/g,'');}
function money(n){n=Number(n); if(!Number.isFinite(n)) return '--'; return '$'+n.toFixed(n>=100?2:n>=1?3:5).replace(/\.?0+$/,'');}
function avg(a){return a.length?a.reduce((s,v)=>s+v,0)/a.length:null;}
function calcRsi(closes,p=14){if(closes.length<=p)return null;let g=0,l=0;for(let i=closes.length-p;i<closes.length;i++){const d=closes[i]-closes[i-1];if(d>=0)g+=d;else l-=d;}if(l===0)return 100;const rs=g/l;return 100-(100/(1+rs));}
function aggregateCandles(candles,size){
  const out=[];
  for(let i=0;i<candles.length;i+=size){
    const group=candles.slice(i,i+size).filter(c=>Number.isFinite(c.close));
    if(group.length<2) continue;
    out.push({
      open:group[0].open,
      high:Math.max(...group.map(c=>c.high)),
      low:Math.min(...group.map(c=>c.low)),
      close:group[group.length-1].close,
      volume:group.reduce((sum,c)=>sum+(Number(c.volume)||0),0)
    });
  }
  return out;
}
function isStaticOnlyHost(){
  const host=location.hostname||'';
  return /\.github\.io$/i.test(host)||/\.pages\.dev$/i.test(host)||host===''||location.protocol==='file:';
}
async function fetchJson(url){
  const controller=new AbortController();
  const timeout=setTimeout(()=>controller.abort(),12000);
  try{
    const r=await fetch(url,{signal:controller.signal});
    if(!r.ok) throw new Error(`${r.status} ${r.statusText}`.trim());
    return r.json();
  }finally{clearTimeout(timeout);}
}
async function fetchPublicApiJson(path){
  const cleanPath=String(path||'').replace(/^\/+/,'');
  const urls=[`/api/${cleanPath}`,`/.netlify/functions/${cleanPath}`];
  let lastError=null;
  for(const url of urls){
    try{
      return await fetchJson(url);
    }catch(e){
      lastError=e;
    }
  }
  throw lastError||new Error('Public API unavailable');
}
async function fetchText(url){
  const controller=new AbortController();
  const timeout=setTimeout(()=>controller.abort(),12000);
  try{
    const r=await fetch(url,{signal:controller.signal});
    if(!r.ok) throw new Error(`${r.status} ${r.statusText}`.trim());
    return r.text();
  }finally{clearTimeout(timeout);}
}
async function fetchBackendCandles(raw){
  if(!/^https?:$/.test(location.protocol)) throw new Error('Backend candle proxy is only available when hosted');
  const sym=displaySymbol(raw);
  const data=await fetchPublicApiJson(`candles?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(sym)}&limit=160`);
  const candles=(data?.candles||[])
    .map(c=>({time:c.time,open:+c.open,high:+c.high,low:+c.low,close:+c.close,volume:+c.volume}))
    .filter(c=>Number.isFinite(c.close)&&Number.isFinite(c.high)&&Number.isFinite(c.low));
  if(!candles.length) throw new Error(data?.error||'No backend candles returned');
  candles.source=data?.source||'Public candle proxy';
  candles.delayed=Boolean(data?.delayed);
  return candles;
}
async function fetchCryptoCandles(raw,limit=160,interval='1h'){
  const pair=cryptoPairFor(raw), base=cryptoBaseFor(raw);
  if(!pair) return null;
  const errors=[];
  const binanceUrls=[
    `https://data-api.binance.vision/api/v3/klines?symbol=${pair}&interval=${interval}&limit=${limit}`,
    `https://api.binance.us/api/v3/klines?symbol=${pair}&interval=${interval}&limit=${limit}`,
    `https://api.binance.com/api/v3/klines?symbol=${pair}&interval=${interval}&limit=${limit}`
  ];
  for(const url of binanceUrls){
    try{
      const rows=await fetchJson(url);
      const candles=rows.map(x=>({open:+x[1],high:+x[2],low:+x[3],close:+x[4],volume:+x[5]})).filter(c=>Number.isFinite(c.close)&&Number.isFinite(c.high)&&Number.isFinite(c.low));
      if(candles.length) return candles;
    }catch(e){errors.push(e.message);}
  }
  if(base){
    try{
      const granularityMap={'15m':900,'1h':3600,'4h':21600,'1d':86400};
      const rows=await fetchJson(`https://api.exchange.coinbase.com/products/${base}-USD/candles?granularity=${granularityMap[interval]||3600}`);
      const candles=rows
        .map(x=>({time:+x[0],low:+x[1],high:+x[2],open:+x[3],close:+x[4],volume:+x[5]}))
        .filter(c=>Number.isFinite(c.close)&&Number.isFinite(c.high)&&Number.isFinite(c.low))
        .sort((a,b)=>a.time-b.time)
        .slice(-limit);
      if(candles.length) return candles;
    }catch(e){errors.push(e.message);}
  }
  throw new Error(`Crypto candle feed unavailable for ${displaySymbol(raw)}. Tried Binance market data, Binance.US, and Coinbase. Some smaller coins may not exist on all feeds.`);
}
function yahooRangeFor(interval){
  if(interval==='15m') return '5d';
  if(interval==='1h') return '1mo';
  if(interval==='4h') return '3mo';
  if(interval==='1d') return '6mo';
  return '1mo';
}
function yahooIntervalFor(interval){return interval==='4h'?'1h':interval;}
function parseStooqCandles(csv){
  const lines=String(csv||'').trim().split(/\r?\n/).filter(Boolean);
  if(lines.length<20||!/^date,/i.test(lines[0])) throw new Error('No Stooq candles returned');
  return lines.slice(1).map(line=>{
    const [date,open,high,low,close,volume]=line.split(',');
    return {time:Math.floor(new Date(`${date}T16:00:00-05:00`).getTime()/1000),open:+open,high:+high,low:+low,close:+close,volume:+volume};
  }).filter(c=>Number.isFinite(c.close)&&Number.isFinite(c.high)&&Number.isFinite(c.low));
}
async function fetchStooqDailyCandles(raw){
  const sym=displaySymbol(raw).toLowerCase();
  const url=`https://stooq.com/q/d/l/?s=${encodeURIComponent(sym+'.us')}&i=d`;
  const sources=[
    url,
    `https://api.allorigins.win/raw?url=${encodeURIComponent(url)}`,
    `https://corsproxy.io/?${encodeURIComponent(url)}`
  ];
  let lastError=null;
  for(const source of sources){
    try{
      const candles=parseStooqCandles(await fetchText(source)).slice(-180);
      if(candles.length){candles.source='Stooq delayed daily candles'; candles.delayed=true; return candles;}
    }catch(e){lastError=e;}
  }
  throw lastError||new Error('Stooq delayed daily feed unavailable');
}
async function fetchCandles(raw,interval='1h',limit=160){
  const sym=displaySymbol(raw);
  let backendError=null;
  try{
    return await fetchBackendCandles(sym);
  }catch(e){
    backendError=e;
  }
  const cryptoPair=cryptoPairFor(raw);
  try {
    if(cryptoPair){
      return await fetchCryptoCandles(sym,limit,interval);
    }
    const yahooUrl=`https://query1.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/${encodeURIComponent(sym)}?range=${yahooRangeFor(interval)}&interval=${yahooIntervalFor(interval)}&includePrePost=true`;
    let data;
    try {
      const r=await fetch(yahooUrl);
      if(!r.ok) throw new Error('direct feed blocked');
      data=await r.json();
    } catch(e) {
      const proxy=await fetch(`https://api.allorigins.win/raw?url=${encodeURIComponent(yahooUrl)}`);
      if(!proxy.ok) throw new Error('Stock candle feed unavailable');
      data=await proxy.json();
    }
    const res=data.chart?.result?.[0], q=res?.indicators?.quote?.[0];
    if(!q?.close?.length) throw new Error('No candles returned');
    const candles=q.close.map((close,i)=>({open:+q.open?.[i],high:+q.high?.[i],low:+q.low?.[i],close:+close,volume:+q.volume?.[i]})).filter(c=>Number.isFinite(c.close)&&Number.isFinite(c.high)&&Number.isFinite(c.low));
    candles.source='Yahoo/proxy intraday candles';
    return interval==='4h'?aggregateCandles(candles,4):candles;
  } catch(e) {
    try{
      return await fetchStooqDailyCandles(sym);
    }catch(fallbackError){
      throw backendError && /^https?:$/.test(location.protocol) ? backendError : fallbackError || e;
    }
  }
}
function nearest(vals,price,dir){const f=vals.filter(v=>dir==='above'?v>price:v<price); if(!f.length)return null; return f.reduce((b,v)=>Math.abs(v-price)<Math.abs(b-price)?v:b,f[0]);}
function pctDistance(from,to){return Number.isFinite(from)&&Number.isFinite(to)&&from?(((to-from)/from)*100).toFixed(2)+'%':'--';}
function avgRange(candles){const ranges=candles.map(c=>Math.abs(c.high-c.low)).filter(Number.isFinite);return avg(ranges.slice(-14))||0;}
function plannedLevels(signal,price,support,resistance,candles){
  const atr=avgRange(candles), buffer=Math.max(price*0.0025,atr*0.35);
  const bullish=signal.includes('BUY'), bearish=signal.includes('SELL');
  let entry=price, stop=bullish?support-buffer:bearish?resistance+buffer:support-buffer, target=bullish?resistance:bearish?support:resistance;
  if(bullish&&target<=price) target=price+Math.max(buffer*2,Math.abs(price-stop)*2);
  if(bearish&&target>=price) target=price-Math.max(buffer*2,Math.abs(stop-price)*2);
  const risk=Math.abs(entry-stop), reward=Math.abs(target-entry);
  return {entry,stop,target,riskReward:risk?reward/risk:null,buffer,atr};
}
function analyzeCandles(raw,candles){
  const sym=displaySymbol(raw), cryptoPair=cryptoPairFor(raw), recent=candles.slice(-80), closes=recent.map(c=>c.close), highs=recent.map(c=>c.high), lows=recent.map(c=>c.low), vols=recent.map(c=>c.volume).filter(Number.isFinite);
  const price=closes[closes.length-1], prev=closes[closes.length-2]||price, top=Math.max(...highs), bottom=Math.min(...lows), sma20=avg(closes.slice(-20)), sma50=avg(closes.slice(-50)), rv=calcRsi(closes);
  const pivotHighs=recent.slice(2,-2).filter((c,i)=>c.high>recent[i+1].high&&c.high>recent[i+3].high).map(c=>c.high);
  const pivotLows=recent.slice(2,-2).filter((c,i)=>c.low<recent[i+1].low&&c.low<recent[i+3].low).map(c=>c.low);
  const resistance=nearest(pivotHighs.length?pivotHighs:highs,price,'above')||top, support=nearest(pivotLows.length?pivotLows:lows,price,'below')||bottom;
  const change=((price-prev)/prev)*100, avgVol=avg(vols.slice(-50)), vol=vols[vols.length-1]||0, volRatio=avgVol?vol/avgVol:null;
  let score=50, reasons=[];
  if(sma20&&price>sma20){score+=10;reasons.push(`Price is above the 20-period average (${money(sma20)}), supporting bullish momentum.`);}
  if(sma20&&price<sma20){score-=10;reasons.push(`Price is below the 20-period average (${money(sma20)}), weakening the setup.`);}
  if(sma50&&price>sma50){score+=8;reasons.push(`Price is above the 50-period average (${money(sma50)}), keeping the short-term trend constructive.`);}
  if(sma50&&price<sma50){score-=8;reasons.push(`Price is below the 50-period average (${money(sma50)}), so trend confirmation is weaker.`);}
  if(change>0.5){score+=6;reasons.push(`Recent candle change is positive (${change.toFixed(2)}%), showing buying pressure.`);}
  if(change<-0.5){score-=6;reasons.push(`Recent candle change is negative (${change.toFixed(2)}%), showing selling pressure.`);}
  if(rv!==null&&rv>=55&&rv<=68){score+=7;reasons.push(`RSI near ${rv.toFixed(0)} shows momentum without being extremely stretched.`);}
  if(rv!==null&&rv>72){score-=7;reasons.push(`RSI near ${rv.toFixed(0)} is stretched, so chasing is higher risk.`);}
  if(rv!==null&&rv<35){score-=5;reasons.push(`RSI near ${rv.toFixed(0)} shows weakness unless a reversal forms.`);}
  reasons.push(`Nearest support is ${money(support)} and nearest resistance is ${money(resistance)}.`);
  const strength=Math.max(5,Math.min(95,Math.round(score)));
  const signal=strength>=76?'STRONG BUY':strength>=62?'BUY':strength<=24?'STRONG SELL':strength<=40?'SELL':'NEUTRAL';
  const levels=plannedLevels(signal,price,support,resistance,recent);
  const bullish=signal.includes('BUY'), bearish=signal.includes('SELL');
  const rangePosition=Math.max(0,Math.min(100,((price-bottom)/(top-bottom||1))*100));
  const entryPlan=bullish
    ? `For a long plan, the cleaner entry is a hold above ${money(support)} with price pushing toward ${money(levels.target)} on expanding volume.`
    : bearish
      ? `For a short plan, the cleaner entry is rejection under ${money(resistance)} with price rotating back toward ${money(levels.target)}.`
      : `For a neutral plan, avoid chasing the middle of the range; wait for either a clean break above ${money(resistance)} or a reclaim from ${money(support)}.`;
  const invalidation=bullish
    ? `Invalidation is a decisive loss of the buffered stop area near ${money(levels.stop)} or a failed breakout that quickly falls back into the prior range.`
    : bearish
      ? `Invalidation is a decisive reclaim of the buffered stop area near ${money(levels.stop)} or a squeeze that holds above that level.`
      : `Invalidation is continued chop with no volume expansion; no-trade is valid until the range resolves.`;
  const analysisBlocks=[
    `<b>Bias:</b> ${signal} with ${strength}/100 confidence. ${reasons.slice(0,3).join(' ')}`,
    `<b>Levels:</b> Current price is ${money(price)}, support is ${money(support)}, resistance is ${money(resistance)}, recent bottom is ${money(bottom)}, and recent top is ${money(top)}. Price is sitting around ${rangePosition.toFixed(0)}% of the recent range.`,
    `<b>Trade plan:</b> ${entryPlan}`,
    `<b>Risk:</b> ${invalidation} Planned entry is ${money(levels.entry)}, stop is ${money(levels.stop)}, target is ${money(levels.target)}, and estimated R:R is ${levels.riskReward?levels.riskReward.toFixed(2)+'R':'--'}.`,
    `<b>Volume/context:</b> Latest volume is ${volRatio?volRatio.toFixed(1)+'x recent average':'not confirmed versus average'}. ${volRatio&&volRatio>1.2?'That gives the move more participation.':'That means the signal needs extra confirmation from the next candle.'}`
  ];
  const catalystText='Check same-day headlines, earnings/calendar events, SEC/company releases, macro news, sector or crypto beta, and Ground News source balance before treating this as actionable.';
  return {
    symbol:sym,name:cryptoPair?`${cryptoPair.replace('USDT','')} / USDT`:sym,price,prev_close:prev,change_pct:change,day_high:top,day_low:bottom,volume:vol,avg_volume:avgVol||0,
    week52_high:top,week52_low:bottom,market_cap:'--',pe_ratio:null,signal,signal_strength:strength,
    support,resistance,stop_loss:levels.stop,target:levels.target,risk_reward:levels.riskReward,
    trend:sma20&&sma50&&sma20>sma50?'uptrend':sma20&&sma50&&sma20<sma50?'downtrend':'sideways',rsi_approx:rv,
    candle_source:candles.source||'Candle feed',
    delayed:Boolean(candles.delayed),
    indicators:[
      {name:'Trend',value:sma20&&sma50&&sma20>sma50?'uptrend':sma20&&sma50&&sma20<sma50?'downtrend':'sideways',signal:sma20&&sma50&&sma20>sma50?'buy':sma20&&sma50&&sma20<sma50?'sell':'neutral',bar:sma20&&sma50?Math.min(95,Math.max(5,50+((sma20-sma50)/price)*500)):50},
      {name:'Momentum',value:`${change.toFixed(2)}%`,signal:change>0.5?'buy':change<-0.5?'sell':'neutral',bar:Math.min(95,Math.max(5,50+change*8))},
      {name:'RSI',value:rv?rv.toFixed(0):'--',signal:rv>60&&rv<72?'buy':rv<40?'sell':'neutral',bar:rv||50},
      {name:'Volume',value:volRatio?`${volRatio.toFixed(1)}x avg`:'--',signal:volRatio>1.2?'buy':'neutral',bar:volRatio?Math.min(95,volRatio*45):50},
      {name:'Range',value:`${money(bottom)}-${money(top)}`,signal:'neutral',bar:((price-bottom)/(top-bottom||1))*100},
      {name:'Levels',value:`S ${money(support)} / R ${money(resistance)}`,signal:'neutral',bar:50}
    ],
    analysis:analysisBlocks.join('<br><br>'),
    catalyst:catalystText
  };
}

// â”€â”€ MARKET OVERVIEW â”€â”€
async function loadMarketOverview() {
  try {
    const items = await Promise.all(['SPY','QQQ','DIA','IWM','GLD','BTC'].map(async symbol => {
      try { const d = await fetchAnalysis(symbol, () => {}); return {symbol, price:d.price, change_pct:d.change_pct}; }
      catch(e) { return {symbol, price:null, change_pct:null}; }
    }));
    document.getElementById('mktGrid').innerHTML = items.map(it=>{
      const chg = parseFloat(it.change_pct||0);
      const cls = chg>0?'up':chg<0?'dn':'neu';
      return `<div class="mkt-item"><div class="mkt-name">${it.symbol}</div><div class="mkt-price">${it.price?money(it.price):'--'}</div><div class="mkt-chg ${cls}">${it.price===null?'--':(chg>=0?'+':'')+chg.toFixed(2)+'%'}</div></div>`;
    }).join('');
    return;
    const raw = await callClaude(
      `You fetch current stock/index prices using web search. Return ONLY a JSON array like: [{"symbol":"SPY","price":582.14,"change_pct":0.42},...]. No markdown, no explanation.`,
      `Search for current prices of SPY, QQQ, DIA, VIX index, IWM, GLD, and Bitcoin (BTC). Return JSON array only.`
    );
    const match = raw.match(/\[[\s\S]*?\]/);
    if(!match) return;
    const legacyItems = JSON.parse(match[0]);
    const labels={'SPY':'SPY','QQQ':'QQQ','DIA':'DIA','VIX':'VIX','IWM':'IWM','GLD':'GLD','BTC-USD':'BTC','BITCOIN':'BTC'};
    document.getElementById('mktGrid').innerHTML = legacyItems.map(it=>{
      const lbl = labels[it.symbol.toUpperCase()]||it.symbol;
      const chg = parseFloat(it.change_pct||0);
      const cls = chg>0?'up':chg<0?'dn':'neu';
      return `<div class="mkt-item"><div class="mkt-name">${lbl}</div><div class="mkt-price">$${parseFloat(it.price).toFixed(2)}</div><div class="mkt-chg ${cls}">${chg>=0?'+':''}${chg.toFixed(2)}%</div></div>`;
    }).join('');
  } catch(e) { console.warn('Overview error',e); }
}

// â”€â”€ STOCK ANALYSIS â”€â”€
async function fetchAnalysis(symbol, onStep) {
  onStep(1);
  const candles = await fetchCandles(symbol);
  onStep(2);
  return analyzeCandles(symbol, candles);
  const sys = `You are an expert day trading analyst. Use web_search to get REAL current data for the requested stock symbol.
Search for: current price, today's change %, day high/low, volume, 52-week range, recent news, and any relevant technical levels.
Then analyze it and return ONLY this JSON object (no markdown, no code blocks, no explanation):
{
  "symbol":"AAPL","name":"Apple Inc.","price":195.50,"prev_close":193.20,
  "change_pct":1.19,"day_high":196.80,"day_low":193.10,
  "volume":52000000,"avg_volume":58000000,
  "week52_high":220.00,"week52_low":164.00,
  "market_cap":"3.0T","pe_ratio":32.5,
  "ext_hours_price":195.80,"ext_hours_change":"+0.15%",
  "signal":"BUY",
  "signal_strength":72,
  "support":190.50,"resistance":200.00,"stop_loss":188.00,"target":203.50,
  "trend":"uptrend","rsi_approx":54,
  "indicators":[
    {"name":"Trend","value":"uptrend","signal":"buy","bar":70},
    {"name":"Momentum","value":"positive","signal":"buy","bar":65},
    {"name":"RSI est","value":"54","signal":"neutral","bar":54},
    {"name":"Volume","value":"0.9x avg","signal":"neutral","bar":45},
    {"name":"vs 52W Hi","value":"11% below","signal":"neutral","bar":55},
    {"name":"News Flow","value":"positive","signal":"buy","bar":68}
  ],
  "analysis":"2-3 sentence plain English analysis of current price action and what a day trader should watch.",
  "catalyst":"Any current news, earnings, or events driving the stock."
}
signal must be one of: STRONG BUY, BUY, NEUTRAL, SELL, STRONG SELL
signal_strength: 0-100 where 100=strongest buy, 0=strongest sell, 50=neutral
Return ONLY the JSON object.`;

  onStep(1);
  const raw = await callClaude(sys, `Get real-time data and analyze ${symbol} as a day trading opportunity right now. Search for current price, technicals, and news.`);
  onStep(2);

  // Robustly parse JSON
  let str = raw.replace(/```json\n?/g,'').replace(/```\n?/g,'').trim();
  const s = str.indexOf('{'), e = str.lastIndexOf('}');
  if(s===-1||e===-1) throw new Error('Could not parse response â€” try again');
  return JSON.parse(str.slice(s,e+1));
}

// â”€â”€ COMMAND CENTER V2 â”€â”€
function signalClass(signal){
  return signal&&signal.includes('BUY')?'up':signal&&signal.includes('SELL')?'dn':'neu';
}
function setupName(data){
  if((data.signal||'').includes('BUY')) return data.signal_strength>=76?'Breakout long':'Long watch';
  if((data.signal||'').includes('SELL')) return data.signal_strength<=24?'Breakdown short':'Short watch';
  return 'Range / wait';
}
function renderDeepDive(data){
  if(!data) return;
  focusedSymbol=data.symbol;
  const rr=data.risk_reward?`${Number(data.risk_reward).toFixed(2)}R`:'--';
  document.getElementById('deepText').innerHTML = `<b style="color:var(--white)">${data.symbol}</b> ${data.signal} ${data.signal_strength}/100. Entry near ${money(data.price)}, stop ${money(data.stop_loss)}, target ${money(data.target)}, R:R ${rr}. ${setupName(data)} until price proves otherwise.`;
}
async function loadTimeframeMatrix(symbol){
  const grid=document.getElementById('timeframeGrid');
  document.getElementById('tfSymbol').textContent=symbol;
  grid.innerHTML=TIMEFRAMES.map(tf=>`<div class="tf-cell"><div class="tf-label">${tf.label}</div><div class="tf-signal neu">LOADING</div><div class="tf-detail">Fetching ${tf.interval} candles...</div></div>`).join('');
  const results=await Promise.allSettled(TIMEFRAMES.map(async tf=>{
    const candles=await fetchCandles(symbol,tf.interval,tf.limit);
    return {tf,data:analyzeCandles(symbol,candles)};
  }));
  grid.innerHTML=results.map((result,i)=>{
    if(result.status!=='fulfilled') return `<div class="tf-cell"><div class="tf-label">${TIMEFRAMES[i].label}</div><div class="tf-signal dn">NO DATA</div><div class="tf-detail">${result.reason?.message||'Feed unavailable'}</div></div>`;
    const {tf,data}=result.value;
    const cls=signalClass(data.signal);
    return `<div class="tf-cell"><div class="tf-label">${tf.label}</div><div class="tf-signal ${cls}">${data.signal}</div><div class="tf-detail">${data.signal_strength}/100<br>Price ${money(data.price)}<br>S ${money(data.support)} / R ${money(data.resistance)}</div></div>`;
  }).join('');
}
function scannerScore(data){
  const conviction=Math.abs((data.signal_strength||50)-50);
  const rr=data.risk_reward?Math.min(35,Number(data.risk_reward)*10):0;
  const dir=(data.signal||'').includes('BUY')||(data.signal||'').includes('SELL')?15:0;
  return Math.round(conviction+rr+dir);
}
async function scanMarket(){
  const list=document.getElementById('scannerList');
  list.innerHTML=`<div class="scan-row"><div class="scan-symbol">SCAN</div><div class="scan-meta">Scanning ${SCANNER_SYMBOLS.length} tickers across stocks and crypto...</div><div class="scan-score neu">...</div></div>`;
  const results=await Promise.allSettled(SCANNER_SYMBOLS.map(async symbol=>fetchAnalysis(symbol,()=>{})));
  const setups=results
    .filter(r=>r.status==='fulfilled')
    .map(r=>({...r.value, scanner_score:scannerScore(r.value)}))
    .sort((a,b)=>b.scanner_score-a.scanner_score)
    .slice(0,8);
  list.innerHTML=setups.length?setups.map(data=>{
    const cls=signalClass(data.signal);
    const rr=data.risk_reward?Number(data.risk_reward).toFixed(2)+'R':'--';
    return `<div class="scan-row">
      <div class="scan-symbol">${data.symbol}</div>
      <div class="scan-meta">${setupName(data)} / ${data.signal} / R:R ${rr}<br>S ${money(data.support)} Â· R ${money(data.resistance)}<br><button class="scan-action" onclick="focusScannerSymbol('${data.symbol}')">OPEN</button></div>
      <div class="scan-score ${cls}">${data.scanner_score}</div>
    </div>`;
  }).join(''):`<div class="scan-row"><div class="scan-symbol">NONE</div><div class="scan-meta">No feed results returned. Try again after refreshing.</div><div class="scan-score dn">0</div></div>`;
}
function focusScannerSymbol(symbol){
  if(!watched.includes(symbol)){
    watched.push(symbol);
    insertLoading(symbol);
    loadCard(symbol);
  } else {
    refreshCard(symbol);
  }
}
function readPaperAccount(){
  try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('dtoPaperTradingAccount'))||{cash:100000,positions:[],quotes:{},realized:0};}
  catch(e){return {cash:100000,positions:[],quotes:{},realized:0};}
}
function paperPositionLast(account,position){return account.quotes?.[position.symbol]?.price||position.entry||0;}
function paperPositionPnl(account,position){
  const direction=position.side==='long'?1:-1;
  return (paperPositionLast(account,position)-position.entry)*position.qty*direction;
}
function renderPaperSnapshot(){
  const el=document.getElementById('paperSnapshot');
  const account=readPaperAccount();
  const positions=account.positions||[];
  const openPnl=positions.reduce((sum,p)=>sum+paperPositionPnl(account,p),0);
  const longValue=positions.filter(p=>p.side==='long').reduce((sum,p)=>sum+p.qty*paperPositionLast(account,p),0);
  const shortPnl=positions.filter(p=>p.side==='short').reduce((sum,p)=>sum+paperPositionPnl(account,p),0);
  const equity=(account.cash||0)+longValue+shortPnl;
  el.innerHTML=`<div class="paper-stats">
    <div class="paper-stat"><div class="paper-label">Equity</div><div class="paper-val">${money(equity)}</div></div>
    <div class="paper-stat"><div class="paper-label">Open P&L</div><div class="paper-val ${openPnl>=0?'up':'dn'}">${money(openPnl)}</div></div>
  </div>
  ${positions.length?positions.slice(0,4).map(p=>{
    const pnl=paperPositionPnl(account,p);
    return `<div class="position-mini"><span>${p.symbol} ${String(p.side).toUpperCase()}</span><span class="${pnl>=0?'up':'dn'}">${money(pnl)}</span></div>`;
  }).join(''):`<div class="scan-meta">No open paper positions. Use the Paper Arena to test setups with fake money.</div>`}
  <div style="margin-top:10px"><button class="scan-action" onclick="location.href='paper_trading_simulator.html'">OPEN PAPER ARENA</button></div>`;
}

// â”€â”€ BUILD CARD â”€â”€
function startupSymbolFromCommandCenter(){
  const params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
  const fromQuery = params.get('symbol') || params.get('ticker') || params.get('asset');
  if(fromQuery) return String(fromQuery).toUpperCase().trim();
  try {
    const setup = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('dtoSetupPacket') || localStorage.getItem('dtoLastSetup') || 'null');
    return setup?.symbol ? String(setup.symbol).toUpperCase().trim() : '';
  } catch(e) {
    return '';
  }
}

function syncSignalToCommandCenter(data){
  if(!data || !data.symbol) return;
  const side = String(data.signal || '').includes('SELL') ? 'short' : 'long';
  const rating = String(data.signal || '').includes('BUY') ? 'BUY' : String(data.signal || '').includes('SELL') ? 'SELL' : 'HOLD';
  const setup = {
    id: `signal-${data.symbol}-${Date.now()}`,
    symbol: data.symbol,
    assetType: cryptoPairFor(data.symbol) ? 'crypto' : 'stock',
    side,
    rating,
    entry: Number(data.price) || null,
    stop: Number(data.stop_loss) || null,
    target: Number(data.target) || null,
    support: Number(data.support) || null,
    resistance: Number(data.resistance) || null,
    rr: Number(data.risk_reward) || null,
    confidence: Number(data.signal_strength) || null,
    timeframe: 'intraday',
    thesis: `${data.symbol} ${data.signal || 'signal'} ${data.signal_strength || '--'}/100. ${String(data.analysis || '').replace(/<[^>]+>/g,' ').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim()}`,
    catalysts: data.catalyst ? [data.catalyst] : [],
    sourcePage: 'signal_dashboard.html',
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString()
  };
  try {
    localStorage.setItem('dtoSetupPacket', JSON.stringify(setup));
    localStorage.setItem('dtoLastSetup', JSON.stringify(setup));
    const list = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('dtoSetupPackets') || '[]');
    localStorage.setItem('dtoSetupPackets', JSON.stringify([setup, ...list.filter(item => item.id !== setup.id)].slice(0, 30)));
  } catch(e) {}
}

function buildCard(d) {
  const chg = parseFloat(d.change_pct||0);
  const cls = chg>0?'up':chg<0?'dn':'neu';
  const sig = d.signal||'NEUTRAL';
  const cardCls = sig.includes('BUY')?'bull':sig.includes('SELL')?'bear':'neutral';
  const badgeMap={'STRONG BUY':'sb-strong-buy','BUY':'sb-buy','NEUTRAL':'sb-neutral','SELL':'sb-sell','STRONG SELL':'sb-strong-sell'};
  const badgeCls = badgeMap[sig]||'sb-neutral';
  const sigIcon = sig.includes('BUY')?'â–²':sig.includes('SELL')?'â–¼':'â—';
  const str = d.signal_strength||50;
  const scoreColor = str>=65?'var(--green)':str<=35?'var(--red)':'var(--gold)';
  const now = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en-US',{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit',second:'2-digit'});

  const inds = (d.indicators||[]).map(i=>{
    const bc=i.signal==='buy'?'var(--green)':i.signal==='sell'?'var(--red)':'var(--gold)';
    const sc=i.signal==='buy'?'up':i.signal==='sell'?'dn':'neu';
    const sl=i.signal==='buy'?'BUY':i.signal==='sell'?'SELL':'HOLD';
    return `<div class="ind-row"><span class="ind-name">${i.name}</span><div class="ind-bar-bg"><div class="ind-bar-fill" style="width:${Math.max(4,i.bar||50)}%;background:${bc}"></div></div><span class="ind-val">${i.value}</span><span class="ind-sig ${sc}">${sl}</span></div>`;
  }).join('');

  const extHrs = d.ext_hours_price
    ? `<div class="lev-item"><div class="lev-label">EXT HRS</div><div class="lev-val neu">$${parseFloat(d.ext_hours_price).toFixed(2)}</div></div>`
    : `<div class="lev-item"><div class="lev-label">EST R:R</div><div class="lev-val">${d.risk_reward?parseFloat(d.risk_reward).toFixed(2)+'R':'â€”'}</div></div>`;

  const analysisHtml = (d.analysis||'No analysis available.').replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g,'<b>$1</b>');
  const catalystHtml = d.catalyst ? `<div style="margin-top:10px;font-size:0.88em;color:var(--muted);line-height:1.65"><b style="color:var(--gold)">MARKET CONTEXT:</b> ${d.catalyst}</div>` : '';
  const feedHtml = d.candle_source ? `<div style="margin-top:10px;font-size:0.82em;color:${d.delayed?'var(--gold)':'var(--muted)'};line-height:1.55"><b>DATA FEED:</b> ${d.candle_source}${d.delayed?' (delayed fallback; use hosted Alpaca/backend for live intraday candles)':''}</div>` : '';

  return `<div class="scard ${cardCls}" id="card-${d.symbol}">
    <div class="card-top">
      <div><div class="c-ticker">${d.symbol}</div><div class="c-name">${(d.name||'').substring(0,32)}</div></div>
      <div><div class="c-price">$${parseFloat(d.price||0).toFixed(2)}</div><div class="c-chg ${cls}">${chg>=0?'+':''}${chg.toFixed(2)}% today</div></div>
    </div>
    <div class="card-signal">
      <div class="sig-badge ${badgeCls}">${sigIcon} ${sig}</div>
      <div><div class="sig-score-label">SIGNAL SCORE</div><div class="sig-score-val" style="color:${scoreColor}">${str}/100</div></div>
    </div>
    <div class="card-inds">${inds}</div>
    <div class="card-levels">
      <div class="lev-item"><div class="lev-label">SUPPORT</div><div class="lev-val up">$${parseFloat(d.support||0).toFixed(2)}</div></div>
      <div class="lev-item"><div class="lev-label">RESIST</div><div class="lev-val dn">$${parseFloat(d.resistance||0).toFixed(2)}</div></div>
      ${extHrs}
      <div class="lev-item"><div class="lev-label">STOP LOSS</div><div class="lev-val" style="color:var(--orange)">$${parseFloat(d.stop_loss||0).toFixed(2)}</div></div>
      <div class="lev-item"><div class="lev-label">TARGET</div><div class="lev-val" style="color:var(--cyan)">$${parseFloat(d.target||0).toFixed(2)}</div></div>
      <div class="lev-item"><div class="lev-label">RECENT RANGE</div><div class="lev-val" style="font-size:0.75em">$${(d.week52_low||0).toFixed(0)}â€“$${(d.week52_high||0).toFixed(0)}</div></div>
    </div>
    <div class="card-analysis">
      <div class="analysis-header">SIGNAL ANALYSIS <span class="ai-tag">PLAN + LEVELS</span></div>
      <div class="analysis-body">${analysisHtml}${catalystHtml}${feedHtml}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="card-footer">
      <span class="footer-time">Updated ${now}</span>
      <div class="footer-actions">
        <button class="refresh-card-btn" onclick="location.href='paper_trading_simulator.html?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(d.symbol)}&price=${encodeURIComponent(d.price || '')}'">PAPER TRADE</button>
        <button class="refresh-card-btn" onclick="refreshCard('${d.symbol}')">â†» REFRESH</button>
        <button class="remove-btn" onclick="removeCard('${d.symbol}')">âœ• REMOVE</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>`;
}

// â”€â”€ LOADING CARD â”€â”€
function loadingHtml(sym) {
  return `<div class="scard loading-card" id="card-${sym}">
    <div class="card-top"><div class="c-ticker">${sym}</div></div>
    <div class="loading-body">
      <div class="loading-ticker">ANALYZING ${sym}</div>
      <div class="loading-bar"><div class="loading-bar-fill"></div></div>
      <div class="loading-step" id="s1-${sym}"><div class="step-dot" id="d1-${sym}"></div>Searching live market data...</div>
      <div class="loading-step" id="s2-${sym}"><div class="step-dot" id="d2-${sym}"></div>Running technical analysis...</div>
      <div class="loading-step" id="s3-${sym}"><div class="step-dot" id="d3-${sym}"></div>Generating AI signal...</div>
    </div>
  </div>`;
}

function setStep(sym, step) {
  for(let i=1;i<=3;i++){
    const d=document.getElementById(`d${i}-${sym}`);
    if(!d) return;
    d.className='step-dot'+(i<step?' done':i===step?' active':'');
  }
}

// â”€â”€ TICKER MANAGEMENT â”€â”€
async function addTicker() {
  const inp = document.getElementById('tickerInput');
  const sym = inp.value.toUpperCase().trim().replace(/^BINANCE:/,'').replace(/[^A-Z0-9.\-/_\s^]/g,'').trim();
  if(!sym||watched.includes(sym)) { inp.value=''; return; }
  inp.value='';
  watched.push(sym);
  insertLoading(sym);
  await loadCard(sym);
}

function quickAdd(sym) {
  if(watched.includes(sym)) return;
  watched.push(sym);
  insertLoading(sym);
  loadCard(sym);
}

function insertLoading(sym) {
  const grid = document.getElementById('cardsGrid');
  const empty = grid.querySelector('.empty-state');
  if(empty) empty.remove();
  const el = document.createElement('div');
  el.innerHTML = loadingHtml(sym);
  grid.appendChild(el.firstElementChild);
}

async function loadCard(sym) {
  try {
    const data = await fetchAnalysis(sym, step => setStep(sym, step));
    signalCache[data.symbol]=data;
    syncSignalToCommandCenter(data);
    renderDeepDive(data);
    setStep(sym, 4);
    const old = document.getElementById(`card-${sym}`);
    if(old) { const n=document.createElement('div'); n.innerHTML=buildCard(data); old.replaceWith(n.firstElementChild); }
    loadTimeframeMatrix(data.symbol);
    renderPaperSnapshot();
    attachPriceStream(data.symbol);
  } catch(e) {
    const old = document.getElementById(`card-${sym}`);
    if(old) old.innerHTML = `<div class="card-top"><div class="c-ticker">${sym}</div></div>
      <div class="error-body">Failed to analyze ${sym}.<div class="error-detail">${e.message}</div>
      <div style="margin-top:10px"><button class="refresh-card-btn" onclick="refreshCard('${sym}')" style="margin-right:8px">â†» RETRY</button><button class="remove-btn" onclick="removeCard('${sym}')">âœ• REMOVE</button></div></div>`;
  }
}

async function refreshCard(sym) {
  const old = document.getElementById(`card-${sym}`);
  if(old) { const n=document.createElement('div'); n.innerHTML=loadingHtml(sym); old.replaceWith(n.firstElementChild); }
  await loadCard(sym);
}

function removeCard(sym) {
  watched = watched.filter(s=>s!==sym);
  const c = document.getElementById(`card-${sym}`);
  if(c) c.remove();
  if(window.stopStream) window.stopStream(sym);
  if(watched.length===0) document.getElementById('cardsGrid').innerHTML=`<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-icon">ðŸ“¡</div><div class="empty-text">Add any ticker â€” stocks, ETFs, crypto.<br>Live candle analysis generates signals 24/7.<br>Works pre-market, after-hours, weekends, any time.</div><div class="empty-hint">Powered by live candle analysis + technical levels</div></div>`;
}

function attachPriceStream(sym) {
  const isCrypto = Boolean(cryptoPairFor(sym));
  function onTick(price) {
    const card = document.getElementById(`card-${sym}`);
    if (!card) { if (window.stopStream) window.stopStream(sym); return; }
    const el = card.querySelector('.c-price');
    if (!el) return;
    const decimals = price >= 100 ? 2 : price >= 1 ? 3 : 5;
    el.textContent = `$${price.toFixed(decimals)}`;
  }
  if (isCrypto && window.streamCryptoPrice) window.streamCryptoPrice(sym, onTick);
  else if (!isCrypto && window.streamStockPrice) window.streamStockPrice(sym, onTick);
}

// Enter key
document.getElementById('tickerInput').addEventListener('keypress',e=>{ if(e.key==='Enter') addTicker(); });

// Boot
loadMarketOverview();
renderPaperSnapshot();
scanMarket();
const startupSymbol = startupSymbolFromCommandCenter();
if(startupSymbol) {
  document.getElementById('tickerInput').value = startupSymbol;
  quickAdd(startupSymbol);
}
setInterval(loadMarketOverview, 5*60*1000);
setInterval(renderPaperSnapshot, 5000);
</script>

<script>
const ids = ["name","market","timeframe","rr","conditions","entry","stop","targets","review"];
function buildPlan() {
  const v = Object.fromEntries(ids.map(id => [id, document.getElementById(id).value.trim()]));
  return `STRATEGY: ${v.name}
MARKET: ${v.market}
TIMEFRAME: ${v.timeframe}
MINIMUM R:R: ${v.rr}

SETUP CONDITIONS
${v.conditions}

ENTRY TRIGGER
${v.entry}

STOP / INVALIDATION
${v.stop}

TARGETS / MANAGEMENT
${v.targets}

REVIEW QUESTIONS
${v.review}

EXECUTION RULE
If the entry, stop, and target cannot be defined before the trade, skip it.`;
}
function render() { document.getElementById("preview").textContent = buildPlan(); }
function savePlan() {
  localStorage.setItem("strategyBuilderPlan", JSON.stringify(Object.fromEntries(ids.map(id => [id, document.getElementById(id).value]))));
  render();
  alert("Strategy plan saved in this browser.");
}
function restore() {
  const saved = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("strategyBuilderPlan") || "{}");
  ids.forEach(id => { if (saved[id]) document.getElementById(id).value = saved[id]; });
  ids.forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).addEventListener("input", render));
  render();
}
restore();
</script>

<title>Strategy Playbook â€” Day Trader OS</title>
<link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Barlow+Condensed:wght@500;600;700;800&family=JetBrains+Mono:wght@300;400;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">

function readImportedSetup() {
  let saved = null;
  try { saved = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("dtoLastSetup") || "null"); }
  catch(e) { saved = null; }
  const params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
  const setup = { ...(saved || {}) };
  ["symbol","side","rating","entry","stop","target","support","resistance","rr","thesis"].forEach(key => {
    if (params.has(key)) setup[key] = params.get(key);
  });
  return setup.symbol ? setup : null;
}

function escapeHtml(value) {
  return String(value ?? "").replace(/[&<>"']/g, char => ({
    "&": "&amp;",
    "<": "&lt;",
    ">": "&gt;",
    '"': "&quot;",
    "'": "&#39;"
  }[char]));
}

function setupParams(setup) {
  const params = new URLSearchParams();
  ["symbol","side","rating","entry","stop","target","support","resistance","rr","thesis"].forEach(key => {
    if (setup?.[key] !== undefined && setup?.[key] !== null) params.set(key, setup[key]);
  });
  return params.toString();
}

function renderImportedSetup() {
  const setup = readImportedSetup();
  const el = document.getElementById("setupImport");
  if (!setup || !el) return;
  el.classList.remove("hidden");
  const params = setupParams(setup);
  el.innerHTML = `
    <div class="eyebrow">Loaded from Command Center</div>
    <h2>${escapeHtml(setup.symbol)} ${escapeHtml(setup.rating || "Setup")}</h2>
    <p class="sub">${escapeHtml(setup.thesis || "Use the playbook below to match this signal to a repeatable setup before sizing risk.")}</p>
    <div class="import-grid">
      <div class="import-stat"><span>Side</span><strong>${escapeHtml(String(setup.side || "long").toUpperCase())}</strong></div>
      <div class="import-stat"><span>Entry</span><strong>${escapeHtml(setup.entry ? "$" + Number(setup.entry).toFixed(2) : "--")}</strong></div>
      <div class="import-stat"><span>Stop</span><strong>${escapeHtml(setup.stop ? "$" + Number(setup.stop).toFixed(2) : "--")}</strong></div>
      <div class="import-stat"><span>Target</span><strong>${escapeHtml(setup.target ? "$" + Number(setup.target).toFixed(2) : "--")}</strong></div>
      <div class="import-stat"><span>R:R</span><strong>${escapeHtml(setup.rr ? Number(setup.rr).toFixed(2) + "R" : "--")}</strong></div>
    </div>
    <div class="actions">
      <a class="action primary" href="risk_calculator.html?${params}">Size This Setup</a>
      <a class="action" href="paper_trading_simulator.html?${params}">Paper Trade It</a>
      <a class="action" href="index.html">Back To Command Center</a>
    </div>`;
}

function renderSetup(key) {
  const s = setups[key];
  const imported = readImportedSetup();
  const importedParams = imported ? setupParams(imported) : "";
  document.getElementById("content").innerHTML = `
    <article class="panel">
      <div class="eyebrow">Setup module</div>
      <h2>${s.title}</h2>
      <p class="sub">${s.thesis}</p>
      <div class="setup-grid">
        <div class="stat"><span>Best Window</span><strong>${s.best}</strong></div>
        <div class="stat"><span>Bias Type</span><strong>${s.bias}</strong></div>
        <div class="stat"><span>Stop Logic</span><strong>${s.stop}</strong></div>
        <div class="stat"><span>Avoid When</span><strong>${s.avoid}</strong></div>
      </div>
      <div class="cols">
        ${block("Conditions", s.conditions)}
        ${block("Entry Plan", s.entry)}
        ${block("Risk Rules", s.risk)}
      </div>
      <div class="cols" style="margin-top:12px;grid-template-columns:1fr;">
        ${block("Review Prompts", s.review)}
      </div>
      <div class="actions">
        <a class="action primary" href="risk_calculator.html${importedParams ? "?" + importedParams : ""}">Open Risk Calculator</a>
        <a class="action" href="premarket_prep.html">Open Pre-Market Prep</a>
        <a class="action" href="trade_journal.html">Open Journal</a>
      </div>
    </article>`;
}

function block(title, items) {
  return `<div class="rule"><h3>${title}</h3><ul>${items.map(item => `<li>${item}</li>`).join("")}</ul></div>`;
}

document.querySelectorAll(".nav-btn").forEach(button => {
  button.addEventListener("click", () => {
    document.querySelectorAll(".nav-btn").forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove("active"));
    button.classList.add("active");
    renderSetup(button.dataset.setup);
  });
});
renderImportedSetup();
renderSetup("orb");
</script>

    color: var(--muted);
    font-size: 0.75em;
  }

  @media (max-width: 1000px) {
    .dashboard { grid-template-columns: repeat(3,1fr); }
    .form-grid { grid-template-columns: repeat(3,1fr); }
  }
</style>
