<script>
let trades = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('trades') || '[]');
let currentFilter = 'all';

function escapeHtml(value) {
  return String(value ?? '').replace(/[&<>"']/g, ch => ({
    '&': '&amp;',
    '<': '&lt;',
    '>': '&gt;',
    '"': '&quot;',
    "'": '&#39;'
  }[ch]));
}

function parseCSV(text) {
  const rows = [];
  let row = [];
  let cell = '';
  let quoted = false;

  for (let i = 0; i < text.length; i++) {
    const ch = text[i];
    const next = text[i + 1];
    if (ch === '"' && quoted && next === '"') {
      cell += '"';
      i++;
    } else if (ch === '"') {
      quoted = !quoted;
    } else if (ch === ',' && !quoted) {
      row.push(cell);
      cell = '';
    } else if ((ch === '\n' || ch === '\r') && !quoted) {
      if (ch === '\r' && next === '\n') i++;
      row.push(cell);
      if (row.some(v => v.trim() !== '')) rows.push(row);
      row = [];
      cell = '';
    } else {
      cell += ch;
    }
  }

  row.push(cell);
  if (row.some(v => v.trim() !== '')) rows.push(row);
  return rows;
}

// Set today's date as default
document.getElementById('f-date').valueAsDate = new Date();

function loadSetupIntoJournal() {
  const params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
  const setup = window.DTO?.getSetup?.() || {};
  const symbol = params.get('symbol') || setup.symbol;
  const side = params.get('side') || setup.side;
  const entry = Number(params.get('entry') || setup.entry);
  const stop = Number(params.get('stop') || setup.stop);
  const thesis = params.get('thesis') || setup.thesis;
  if (symbol) document.getElementById('f-ticker').value = String(symbol).toUpperCase();
  if (String(side || '').toLowerCase().includes('short')) document.getElementById('f-dir').value = 'SHORT';
  if (String(side || '').toLowerCase().includes('long')) document.getElementById('f-dir').value = 'LONG';
  if (Number.isFinite(entry) && entry > 0) document.getElementById('f-entry').value = entry;
  if (Number.isFinite(stop) && stop > 0) document.getElementById('f-stop').value = stop;
  if (thesis) document.getElementById('f-notes').value = String(thesis).slice(0, 240);
}

function addTrade() {
  const ticker = document.getElementById('f-ticker').value.toUpperCase().trim();
  const date = document.getElementById('f-date').value;
  const dir = document.getElementById('f-dir').value;
  const shares = parseFloat(document.getElementById('f-shares').value);
  const entry = parseFloat(document.getElementById('f-entry').value);
  const exit = parseFloat(document.getElementById('f-exit').value);
  const stop = parseFloat(document.getElementById('f-stop').value);
  const setup = document.getElementById('f-setup').value;
  const emotion = document.getElementById('f-emotion').value;
  const notes = document.getElementById('f-notes').value;

  if (!ticker || !date || isNaN(shares) || isNaN(entry) || isNaN(exit)) {
    alert('Please fill in: Ticker, Date, Shares, Entry, and Exit.');
    return;
  }

  const mult = dir === 'SHORT' ? -1 : 1;
  const pnl = (exit - entry) * shares * mult;
  const rr = stop ? Math.abs((exit - entry) / (entry - stop)).toFixed(2) : 'â€”';

  const trade = { id: Date.now(), ticker, date, dir, shares, entry, exit, stop, pnl, rr, setup, emotion, notes };
  trades.push(trade);
  if (window.DTO) DTO.recordTrade({
    source: "journal",
    symbol: ticker,
    side: dir,
    qty: shares,
    entry,
    exit,
    pnl,
    rr,
    setupType: setup,
    mistake: emotion,
    notes,
    closedAt: date
  });
  saveTrades();
  clearForm();
  render();
}

function deleteTrade(id) {
  trades = trades.filter(t => t.id !== id);
  saveTrades();
  render();
}

function saveTrades() {
  localStorage.setItem('trades', JSON.stringify(trades));
}

function clearForm() {
  ['f-ticker','f-shares','f-entry','f-exit','f-stop','f-notes'].forEach(id => {
    document.getElementById(id).value = '';
  });
  document.getElementById('f-date').valueAsDate = new Date();
}

function setFilter(f, btn) {
  currentFilter = f;
  document.querySelectorAll('.filter-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  btn.classList.add('active');
  renderTable();
}

function render() {
  renderStats();
  renderTable();
  renderEquity();
}

function renderStats() {
  const wins = trades.filter(t => t.pnl > 0);
  const losses = trades.filter(t => t.pnl <= 0);
  const total = trades.length;
  const totalPnl = trades.reduce((s, t) => s + t.pnl, 0);
  const winRate = total > 0 ? (wins.length / total * 100).toFixed(1) : null;
  const avgWin = wins.length > 0 ? wins.reduce((s,t) => s+t.pnl,0) / wins.length : null;
  const avgLoss = losses.length > 0 ? losses.reduce((s,t) => s+t.pnl,0) / losses.length : null;
  const expectancy = total > 0 ? totalPnl / total : null;

  const fmt = n => n >= 0 ? `+$${n.toFixed(2)}` : `-$${Math.abs(n).toFixed(2)}`;

  // Dashboard
  const pnlEl = document.getElementById('totalPnl');
  pnlEl.textContent = fmt(totalPnl);
  pnlEl.className = 'card-value' + (totalPnl < 0 ? ' loss' : '');
  document.getElementById('totalPnlSub').textContent = `${total} trades logged`;

  const wrEl = document.getElementById('winRate');
  wrEl.textContent = winRate ? `${winRate}%` : 'â€”';
  wrEl.className = 'card-value' + (winRate >= 55 ? '' : winRate ? ' loss' : ' neutral');
  document.getElementById('winRateSub').textContent = `${wins.length} wins / ${losses.length} losses`;

  document.getElementById('avgWin').textContent = avgWin ? fmt(avgWin) : 'â€”';
  document.getElementById('avgLoss').textContent = avgLoss ? fmt(avgLoss) : 'â€”';
  const expEl = document.getElementById('expectancy');
  expEl.textContent = expectancy !== null ? fmt(expectancy) : 'â€”';
  expEl.className = 'card-value' + (expectancy < 0 ? ' loss' : ' neutral');

  // Header
  document.getElementById('hNetPnl').textContent = fmt(totalPnl);
  document.getElementById('hNetPnl').className = 'hstat-value' + (totalPnl < 0 ? ' negative' : '');
  document.getElementById('hWinRate').textContent = winRate ? `${winRate}%` : 'â€”';
  document.getElementById('hTrades').textContent = total;
}

function renderTable() {
  const body = document.getElementById('tableBody');

  let filtered = trades;
  if (currentFilter === 'win') filtered = trades.filter(t => t.pnl > 0);
  if (currentFilter === 'loss') filtered = trades.filter(t => t.pnl <= 0);

  if (filtered.length === 0) {
    body.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state">
      <div class="icon">ðŸ“‹</div>
      <p>No trades logged yet.<br>Fill in the form above and click LOG TRADE.<br>Every great trader started with their first entry.</p>
    </div>`;
    return;
  }

  const sorted = [...filtered].reverse();
  body.innerHTML = `<table>
    <thead>
      <tr>
        <th>Date</th><th>Ticker</th><th>Dir</th><th>Shares</th>
        <th>Entry</th><th>Exit</th><th>Stop</th><th>R:R</th>
        <th>P&L</th><th>Setup</th><th>Emotion</th><th>Notes</th><th></th>
      </tr>
    </thead>
    <tbody>
      ${sorted.map(t => {
        const pnlStr = t.pnl >= 0 ? `+$${t.pnl.toFixed(2)}` : `-$${Math.abs(t.pnl).toFixed(2)}`;
        const pnlClass = t.pnl >= 0 ? 'pnl-win' : 'pnl-loss';
        return `<tr>
          <td>${escapeHtml(t.date)}</td>
          <td><strong style="color:#fff">${escapeHtml(t.ticker)}</strong></td>
          <td><span class="badge badge-${String(t.dir || '').toLowerCase()}">${escapeHtml(t.dir)}</span></td>
          <td>${t.shares}</td>
          <td>$${parseFloat(t.entry).toFixed(2)}</td>
          <td>$${parseFloat(t.exit).toFixed(2)}</td>
          <td>${t.stop ? '$'+parseFloat(t.stop).toFixed(2) : 'â€”'}</td>
          <td style="color:var(--accent3)">${t.rr}x</td>
          <td class="${pnlClass}">${pnlStr}</td>
          <td><span class="setup-badge">${escapeHtml(t.setup)}</span></td>
          <td style="color:var(--muted);font-size:0.8em">${escapeHtml(t.emotion)}</td>
          <td class="notes-cell" title="${escapeHtml(t.notes)}">${escapeHtml(t.notes || 'â€”')}</td>
          <td><button class="delete-btn" onclick="deleteTrade(${t.id})">âœ•</button></td>
        </tr>`;
      }).join('')}
    </tbody>
  </table>`;
}

function renderEquity() {
  const section = document.getElementById('equitySection');
  if (trades.length < 2) { section.style.display = 'none'; return; }
  section.style.display = 'block';

  // Build cumulative equity
  let equity = [0];
  trades.forEach(t => equity.push(equity[equity.length-1] + t.pnl));
  const min = Math.min(...equity);
  const max = Math.max(...equity);
  const range = max - min || 1;

  const W = 800, H = 80;
  const pts = equity.map((v, i) => {
    const x = (i / (equity.length - 1)) * W;
    const y = H - ((v - min) / range) * (H - 10) - 5;
    return `${x},${y}`;
  });

  const color = equity[equity.length-1] >= 0 ? '#00ffa3' : '#ff4757';
  const svg = document.getElementById('equitySvg');
  svg.innerHTML = `
    <defs>
      <linearGradient id="eg" x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
        <stop offset="0%" stop-color="${color}" stop-opacity="0.3"/>
        <stop offset="100%" stop-color="${color}" stop-opacity="0"/>
      </linearGradient>
    </defs>
    <polyline points="${pts.join(' ')}" fill="none" stroke="${color}" stroke-width="2"/>
    <polygon points="0,${H} ${pts.join(' ')} ${W},${H}" fill="url(#eg)"/>
  `;

  // Streak dots
  const streak = document.getElementById('streakDisplay');
  const last10 = trades.slice(-10);
  streak.innerHTML = last10.map(t =>
    `<div class="streak-dot ${t.pnl > 0 ? 'win' : 'loss'}" title="${t.ticker}: ${t.pnl>0?'+':''}$${t.pnl.toFixed(2)}"></div>`
  ).join('') + `<span style="margin-left:8px;font-size:0.7em;color:var(--muted);font-family:'IBM Plex Mono',monospace;">Last ${last10.length} trades</span>`;
}

function exportCSV() {
  if (!trades.length) { alert('No trades to export.'); return; }
  const headers = ['Date','Ticker','Direction','Shares','Entry','Exit','Stop','PnL','RR','Setup','Emotion','Notes'];
  const csvCell = value => `"${String(value ?? '').replace(/"/g, '""')}"`;
  const rows = trades.map(t =>
    [t.date,t.ticker,t.dir,t.shares,t.entry,t.exit,t.stop||'',t.pnl.toFixed(2),t.rr,t.setup,t.emotion,t.notes||''].map(csvCell).join(',')
  );
  const csv = [headers.join(','), ...rows].join('\n');
  const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: 'text/csv' });
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  a.download = 'trade_journal.csv';
  a.click();
}

function importCSV(event) {
  const file = event.target.files[0];
  event.target.value = '';
  if (!file) return;

  const reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = () => {
    const rows = parseCSV(String(reader.result || ''));
    if (rows.length < 2) { alert('No trade rows found in that CSV.'); return; }

    const headers = rows[0].map(h => h.trim().toLowerCase());
    const index = name => headers.indexOf(name.toLowerCase());
    const imported = rows.slice(1).map(row => {
      const get = name => {
        const idx = index(name);
        return idx >= 0 ? row[idx] || '' : '';
      };
      const date = get('Date') || new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
      const ticker = get('Ticker').toUpperCase().trim();
      const dir = (get('Direction') || 'LONG').toUpperCase().trim();
      const shares = parseFloat(get('Shares'));
      const entry = parseFloat(get('Entry'));
      const exit = parseFloat(get('Exit'));
      const stop = parseFloat(get('Stop'));
      const pnl = Number.isFinite(parseFloat(get('PnL')))
        ? parseFloat(get('PnL'))
        : ((exit - entry) * shares * (dir === 'SHORT' ? -1 : 1));
      const rr = get('RR') || (Number.isFinite(stop) ? Math.abs((exit - entry) / (entry - stop)).toFixed(2) : '-');

      if (!ticker || !Number.isFinite(shares) || !Number.isFinite(entry) || !Number.isFinite(exit)) return null;
      return {
        id: Date.now() + Math.floor(Math.random() * 100000),
        ticker, date, dir, shares, entry, exit,
        stop: Number.isFinite(stop) ? stop : '',
        pnl, rr,
        setup: get('Setup'),
        emotion: get('Emotion'),
        notes: get('Notes')
      };
    }).filter(Boolean);

    if (!imported.length) { alert('No valid trades found.'); return; }
    trades = trades.concat(imported);
    saveTrades();
    render();
    alert(`Imported ${imported.length} trade${imported.length === 1 ? '' : 's'}.`);
  };
  reader.readAsText(file);
}

function backupJSON() {
  const payload = {
    exportedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    version: 1,
    trades
  };
  const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  a.download = 'trade_journal_backup.json';
  a.click();
}

function restoreJSON(event) {
  const file = event.target.files[0];
  event.target.value = '';
  if (!file) return;

  const reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = () => {
    try {
      const payload = JSON.parse(String(reader.result || '{}'));
      const restored = Array.isArray(payload) ? payload : payload.trades;
      if (!Array.isArray(restored)) throw new Error('Missing trades array.');
      if (!confirm(`Restore ${restored.length} trades? This replaces the current journal.`)) return;
      trades = restored.map(t => ({ ...t, id: t.id || Date.now() + Math.floor(Math.random() * 100000) }));
      saveTrades();
      render();
    } catch (error) {
      alert('That JSON backup could not be restored.');
    }
  };
  reader.readAsText(file);
}

loadSetupIntoJournal();
render();
</script>

      <form class="form-grid" id="setupForm">
        <div class="field"><label for="symbol">Symbol</label><input id="symbol" value="AAPL"></div>

        <div class="field"><label for="rating">Bias</label><select id="rating"><option>CHECK</option><option>BUY</option><option>HOLD</option><option>SELL</option><option>STRONG BUY</option><option>STRONG SELL</option></select></div>

        <div class="field"><label for="resistance">Resistance</label><input id="resistance" type="number" step="0.0001"></div>

<script src="assets/daytrader-os.js?v=20260504-vercel1"></script>
<script>
const $ = id => document.getElementById(id);
const read = (key, fallback) => { try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || JSON.stringify(fallback)); } catch { return fallback; } };
const write = (key, value) => { localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(value)); return value; };
const clean = value => String(value || "").trim().toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9.-]/g, "");
const number = value => value === "" || value === null || value === undefined ? null : Number(value);
const cryptoRe = /^(BTC|ETH|SOL|DOGE|XRP|BNB|ADA|AVAX|LINK|SUI|PEPE|SHIB|[A-Z0-9]{2,12}(USDT|USD))$/;

function packetFromForm() {
  const entry = number($("entry").value);
  const stop = number($("stop").value);
  const target = number($("target").value);
  const rr = entry && stop && target && entry !== stop ? Math.abs(target - entry) / Math.abs(entry - stop) : null;
  const symbol = clean($("symbol").value);
  return {
    symbol,
    assetType: $("assetType").value,
    side: $("side").value,
    rating: $("rating").value,
    entry,
    stop,
    target,
    support: number($("support").value),
    resistance: number($("resistance").value),
    rr,
    confidence: number($("confidence").value),
    timeframe: $("timeframe").value,
    thesis: $("thesis").value,
    catalysts: $("catalysts").value.split(/\n|\|/).map(x => x.trim()).filter(Boolean),
    setupType: $("setupType").value,
    sourcePage: "trade_planner.html",
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString()
  };
}

function loadPacket(setup) {
  if (!setup) return;
  $("symbol").value = setup.symbol || "AAPL";
  $("assetType").value = setup.assetType || (cryptoRe.test(clean(setup.symbol)) ? "crypto" : "stock");
  $("side").value = setup.side || "long";
  $("rating").value = setup.rating || "CHECK";
  $("entry").value = setup.entry ?? "";
  $("stop").value = setup.stop ?? "";
  $("target").value = setup.target ?? "";
  $("support").value = setup.support ?? "";
  $("resistance").value = setup.resistance ?? "";
  $("confidence").value = setup.confidence ?? 50;
  $("timeframe").value = setup.timeframe || "intraday";
  $("thesis").value = setup.thesis || "";
  $("catalysts").value = Array.isArray(setup.catalysts) ? setup.catalysts.join("\n") : (setup.catalysts || "");
  grade();
}

function workflowUrl(page, setup) {
  const params = new URLSearchParams();
  Object.entries(setup).forEach(([key, value]) => {
    if (Array.isArray(value)) value = value.join("|");
    if (value !== null && value !== undefined && value !== "") params.set(key, value);
  });
  return `${page}?${params.toString()}`;
}

function grade() {
  const setup = packetFromForm();
  const grade = window.DTO?.gradeSetup ? window.DTO.gradeSetup(setup) : { score: 0, label: "No Grade", warnings: ["Shared grader unavailable."], notes: [] };
  $("gradeScore").textContent = `${grade.score}/100`;
  $("gradeLabel").textContent = grade.label;
  $("gradeNotes").innerHTML = [...(grade.warnings || []), ...(grade.notes || [])].slice(0, 5).map((note, index) => `<div class="note ${index >= (grade.warnings || []).length ? "good-note" : ""}">${note}</div>`).join("");
  $("openRisk").href = workflowUrl("risk_calculator.html", setup);
  $("openPaper").href = workflowUrl("paper_trading_simulator.html", setup);
}

const presets = [
  ["Breakout", "Price is pressing against resistance with volume expansion. Confirm break and hold above level before entry.", "Volume expansion | clean resistance break | sector/index confirmation"],
  ["Pullback", "Trend is intact and price is pulling into support or VWAP. Wait for buyers to defend before entry.", "Support defense | higher low | no major headline conflict"],
  ["VWAP reclaim", "Price lost VWAP, reclaimed it, and is holding above. Entry needs confirmation candle and defined invalidation.", "VWAP reclaim | volume return | failed breakdown"],
  ["Reversal", "Trend is extended and momentum is shifting. Use smaller size until reversal confirmation is real.", "Exhaustion candle | RSI stretch | support/resistance rejection"]
];

function renderPresets() {
  $("playbookList").innerHTML = presets.map(([name, thesis, catalysts]) => `
    <button class="row" type="button" data-preset="${name}"><div><strong>${name}</strong><span>${thesis}</span></div><span>Use</span></button>
  `).join("");
  document.querySelectorAll("[data-preset]").forEach(button => button.addEventListener("click", () => {
    const preset = presets.find(item => item[0] === button.dataset.preset);
    $("setupType").value = preset[0];
    $("thesis").value = preset[1];
    $("catalysts").value = preset[2].replaceAll(" | ", "\n");
    grade();
  }));
}

function renderRules() {
  const list = read("dtoStrategies", []);
  $("rulesList").innerHTML = list.length ? list.slice(0, 5).map(rule => `<div class="row"><div><strong>${rule.name}</strong><span>${rule.side} / minimum ${rule.minRr}R</span></div><span>${rule.createdAt ? new Date(rule.createdAt).toLocaleDateString() : ""}</span></div>`).join("") : `<div class="note">No saved strategy rules yet.</div>`;
}

$("setupForm").addEventListener("input", event => {
  if (event.target.id === "symbol") $("assetType").value = cryptoRe.test(clean(event.target.value)) ? "crypto" : "stock";
  grade();
});
$("setupForm").addEventListener("submit", event => {
  event.preventDefault();
  const setup = packetFromForm();
  const saved = window.DTO?.saveSetup ? window.DTO.saveSetup(setup) : write("dtoLastSetup", setup);
  write("dtoSetupPacket", saved);
  $("packetState").textContent = `${saved.symbol} saved`;
  setTimeout(() => $("packetState").textContent = "Live grade", 1000);
});
$("loadActive").addEventListener("click", () => loadPacket(window.DTO?.getSetup?.() || read("dtoLastSetup", null)));
$("rulesForm").addEventListener("submit", event => {
  event.preventDefault();
  const item = { name: $("ruleName").value || "Untitled Strategy", minRr: $("minRr").value, side: $("ruleSide").value, entryRules: $("entryRules").value, exitRules: $("exitRules").value, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() };
  write("dtoStrategies", [item, ...read("dtoStrategies", [])].slice(0, 30));
  renderRules();
});
renderPresets();
renderRules();
loadPacket(window.DTO?.getSetup?.() || read("dtoLastSetup", null) || { symbol: "AAPL" });
</script>
</body>
</html>

function reviews(){return DTO.readJson("dtoTradeReviews",[])}
function render(){const list=reviews();const avg=list.length?list.reduce((s,r)=>s+Number(r.discipline||0),0)/list.length:null;const mistakes=list.reduce((m,r)=>(m[r.mistake]=(m[r.mistake]||0)+1,m),{});const top=Object.entries(mistakes).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1])[0];document.getElementById("coachBox").innerHTML=`<div class="dto-panel-kicker">Coach Read</div><h3>${avg?avg.toFixed(1)+"/10":"No Score Yet"}</h3><p>${top?`Most common tag: ${DTO.escapeHtml(top[0])}. Build tomorrow's rules around avoiding that.`:"Review a trade to generate your focus point."}</p><div class="dto-warning">${avg&&avg<7?"Discipline is below target. Reduce size and paper trade until execution stabilizes.":"Good process beats one lucky result. Keep tagging every trade."}</div>`;document.getElementById("historyBox").innerHTML=`<div class="dto-panel-kicker">Recent Reviews</div>${list.length?list.slice(0,10).map(r=>`<div class="dto-list-row"><strong>${DTO.escapeHtml(r.symbol)} ${DTO.money(r.pnl)}</strong><span>${DTO.escapeHtml(r.setupType)} / ${DTO.escapeHtml(r.mistake)} / ${r.discipline}/10</span></div>`).join(""):"<p>No reviews yet.</p>"}`;}
document.getElementById("reviewForm").addEventListener("submit",e=>{e.preventDefault();const r={symbol:document.getElementById("symbol").value.toUpperCase(),pnl:Number(document.getElementById("pnl").value||0),setupType:document.getElementById("setupType").value,mistake:document.getElementById("mistake").value,notes:document.getElementById("notes").value,discipline:Number(document.getElementById("discipline").value),closedAt:new Date().toISOString()};DTO.writeJson("dtoTradeReviews",[r,...reviews()].slice(0,100));DTO.recordTrade({...r,source:"review"});render();});render();

                            <th>Feature</th>

                </div>

        </div>

        <!-- MODULE 2: CHART TYPES -->
        <div id="charttypes" class="module">
            <div class="section">
                <div class="section-title">ðŸ“Š Module 2: Chart Types</div>

                <div class="lesson">
                    <div class="lesson-title">Candlestick Chart (BEST FOR DAY TRADING)</div>
                    <div class="lesson-content">
                        Each "candle" represents one time period (1 minute, 5 minutes, 1 hour, etc.)
                        <div class="visual-demo">
                            <div style="font-size: 1.2em; color: #00d4ff; line-height: 2;">
                                ðŸŸ© GREEN (bullish) = Close > Open<br>
                                ðŸŸ¥ RED (bearish) = Close < Open<br>
                                ðŸ“ Wick = High & Low of period
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="code-block">
                            <strong>Anatomy of a Candle:</strong><br>
                            â”Œâ”€ HIGH (top of upper wick)<br>
                            â”‚  <br>
                            â”‚  â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”  â† CLOSE<br>
                            â”‚  â”‚  BODY   â”‚<br>
                            â”‚  â”‚ (green) â”‚<br>
                            â”‚  â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜  â† OPEN<br>
                            â”‚  <br>
                            â””â”€ LOW (bottom of lower wick)
                        </div>
                        <p class="chart-label">
                            <strong>Green candles = Buyers in control</strong><br>
                            <strong>Red candles = Sellers in control</strong><br>
                            <strong>Long wicks = Rejection at that price</strong>
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="lesson">
                    <div class="lesson-title">Other Chart Types (Less Important)</div>
                    <div class="lesson-content">
                        <strong>Line Chart:</strong> Just connects closing prices. Too simple for day trading.<br><br>
                        <strong>Renko/Heiken-Ashi:</strong> Filtered versions of candles. Nice but not required.<br><br>
                        <strong>Volume Bars:</strong> Shows buying/selling force. Use WITH candlesticks (not alone).
                        <div class="tip">
                            <strong>âœ“ Recommendation:</strong> Use CANDLESTICK charts. They show everything you need.
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <!-- MODULE 3: CANDLESTICK PATTERNS -->
        <div id="patterns" class="module">
            <div class="section">
                <div class="section-title">ðŸ•¯ï¸ Module 3: Candlestick Patterns</div>

                <div class="lesson">
                    <div class="lesson-title">The 4 Patterns You NEED to Know</div>
                    <div class="lesson-content">
                        <strong>1. DOJI (Indecision)</strong><br>
                        Open â‰ˆ Close | Long wicks on both sides<br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">Meaning:</span> Nobody in control. Next candle shows direction.<br><br>

                        <strong>2. HAMMER (Bullish Reversal)</strong><br>
                        Small body at top | Long lower wick<br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">Meaning:</span> Rejection of lower prices. Buyers stepping in.<br><br>

                        <strong>3. SHOOTING STAR (Bearish Reversal)</strong><br>
                        Small body at bottom | Long upper wick<br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">Meaning:</span> Rejection of higher prices. Sellers stepping in.<br><br>

                        <strong>4. ENGULFING (Reversal)</strong><br>
                        Current candle fully covers previous candle<br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">Meaning:</span> Momentum change. Strong conviction.<br><br>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="warning">
                    <strong>âš ï¸ Important:</strong> These patterns ONLY matter at support/resistance levels or with volume confirmation. 
                    A hammer in the middle of a down-trend is just noise.
                </div>

                <div class="tip">
                    <strong>ðŸ’¡ For Day Trading:</strong> Ignore individual patterns. Focus on candlestick REJECTION at support/resistance. 
                    If price touches a support level and bounces with a hammer, THAT matters.
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <!-- MODULE 4: INDICATORS -->
        <div id="indicators" class="module">
            <div class="section">
                <div class="section-title">ðŸ“ˆ Module 4: Technical Indicators</div>

                <div class="lesson">
                    <div class="lesson-title">The ONLY 3 Indicators You Need</div>
                    <div class="lesson-content">
                        <strong>1. Moving Average (MA)</strong><br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">What it is:</span> Average price over last N candles<br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">Why you need it:</span> Shows the trend direction<br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">Setting:</span> 20-period (good for day trading)<br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">How to use:</span> If price is ABOVE the MA, bias is bullish. Below = bearish.<br><br>

                        <strong>2. Support & Resistance (Manual Drawing)</strong><br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">What it is:</span> Price levels where buyers (support) or sellers (resistance) are strong<br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">Why you need it:</span> Shows where to enter and where to stop loss<br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">Setting:</span> Use the drawing tool to mark past lows (support) and highs (resistance)<br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">How to use:</span> ENTER when price breaks resistance. RISK when price breaks support.<br><br>

                        <strong>3. Volume</strong><br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">What it is:</span> Number of shares traded in each candle<br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">Why you need it:</span> Confirms if a move has conviction<br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">Setting:</span> Volume bars show at bottom of chart (usually on by default)<br>
                        <span style="color: #ff9600;">How to use:</span> Breakouts on HIGH volume are more likely to hold. Breakouts on LOW volume fail often.<br><br>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="warning">
                    <strong>âš ï¸ Avoid These Traps:</strong><br>
                    âŒ Don't add 10 indicators (they'll all say different things)<br>
                    âŒ Don't rely on RSI, Stochastic, MACD alone (lagging)<br>
                    âŒ Don't confuse "indicator signal" with "entry signal"<br>
                    <br>
                    Your entries come from PRICE ACTION (breakouts, bounces, support/resistance), 
                    not from an indicator crossing over.
                </div>

                <div class="lesson">
                    <div class="lesson-title">How to Add Indicators in TradingView</div>
                    <div class="lesson-content">
                        <div class="step-box">
                            <span class="step-number">1</span>
                            Click "Indicators" button (top toolbar)
                        </div>
                        <div class="step-box">
                            <span class="step-number">2</span>
                            Search "Moving Average"
                        </div>
                        <div class="step-box">
                            <span class="step-number">3</span>
                            Choose "SMA" (Simple Moving Average)
                        </div>
                        <div class="step-box">
                            <span class="step-number">4</span>
                            Set period to 20
                        </div>
                        <div class="step-box">
                            <span class="step-number">5</span>
                            Change color to orange (easier to see)
                        </div>
                        <div class="step-box">
                            <span class="step-number">6</span>
                            Click "Add to Chart"
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <!-- MODULE 5: SETUP & TRADE -->
        <div id="setup" class="module">
            <div class="section">
                <div class="section-title">âš¡ Module 5: Setting Up Your First Trade</div>

                <div class="lesson">
                    <div class="lesson-title">Step-by-Step: Paper Trade Your First Setup</div>
                    <div class="lesson-content">
                        <div class="step-box">
                            <span class="step-number">1</span>
                            <strong>Pick a stock:</strong> Search AAPL (Apple) on TradingView
                        </div>
                        <div class="step-box">
                            <span class="step-number">2</span>
                            <strong>Set timeframe:</strong> Click "1h" (1-hour chart)
                        </div>
                        <div class="step-box">
                            <span class="step-number">3</span>
                            <strong>Add indicator:</strong> Add 20-period moving average (orange line)
                        </div>
                        <div class="step-box">
                            <span class="step-number">4</span>
                            <strong>Draw levels:</strong> Use pencil tool to mark the last 5 days' highs and lows
                        </div>
                        <div class="step-box">
                            <span class="step-number">5</span>
                            <strong>Identify setup:</strong> Is price above the MA? Is there a clear support and resistance?
                        </div>
                        <div class="step-box">
                            <span class="step-number">6</span>
                            <strong>Wait for signal:</strong> Watch for price to break above resistance or bounce from support
                        </div>
                        <div class="step-box">
                            <span class="step-number">7</span>
                            <strong>Place order:</strong> Click "Trade" â†’ Choose entry price, stop loss, target
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="lesson">
                    <div class="lesson-title">Real Example: TSLA Breakout</div>
                    <div class="lesson-content">
                        <strong>Setup Details:</strong><br>
                        â€¢ Chart: TSLA 1-hour<br>
                        â€¢ Price: $240 (above 20-day MA âœ“)<br>
                        â€¢ Support: $238 (previous low)<br>
                        â€¢ Resistance: $244 (previous high)<br>
                        â€¢ Volume: Above average<br><br>

                        <strong>Signal:</strong> Price breaks above $244 on high volume<br><br>

                        <strong>Your Order:</strong><br>
                        â€¢ BUY 10 shares at $244.50<br>
                        â€¢ STOP LOSS at $242.50 (protect if wrong)<br>
                        â€¢ TAKE PROFIT at $249.00 (2% gain target)<br><br>

                        <strong>Result (hypothetical):</strong><br>
                        Price rallies â†’ hits $249.00 â†’ Sell automatically â†’ +$45 profit<br>
                        (You just made $45 on a $2,450 position. Log it. Repeat.)
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="tip">
                    <strong>ðŸ’¡ Paper Trading Rule:</strong> Treat paper trades like REAL trades. 
                    Same rules, same discipline. If you don't follow rules on fake money, 
                    you won't follow them on real money.
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <!-- MODULE 6: CHECKLIST -->
        <div id="checklist" class="module">
            <div class="section">
                <div class="section-title">âœ… Module 6: Pre-Trade Checklist</div>

                <div class="lesson">
                    <div class="lesson-title">Your Daily Setup Checklist</div>
                    <div class="lesson-content">
                        Run this checklist EVERY time before entering a trade:
                        <ul class="checklist">
                            <li>Is the stock trading above its 20-day moving average?</li>
                            <li>Have I identified at least 2 support/resistance levels?</li>
                            <li>Is my entry at a level (not randomly in the middle)?</li>
                            <li>Is my stop loss 1-2% below entry (tight)?</li>
                            <li>Is my target at least 2x my risk?</li>
                            <li>Do I see volume confirmation on the entry candle?</li>
                            <li>Am I risking <1% of my account on this trade?</li>
                            <li>Have I already taken 3-5 trades today? (Time to stop)</li>
                            <li>Am I in a good emotional state? (Not revenge trading)</li>
                            <li>Is it before 2 PM? (Not trading the last hour of the day)</li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="lesson">
                    <div class="lesson-title">If ANY Box is Unchecked...</div>
                    <div class="lesson-content">
                        <div class="warning">
                            <strong>DO NOT TRADE.</strong><br>
                            Wait for the next setup. Quality > Quantity. One great trade beats 
                            ten mediocre ones.
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="lesson">
                    <div class="lesson-title">Your 30-Day Practice Plan</div>
                    <div class="lesson-content">
                        <strong>Days 1-5:</strong> Paper trade with 1-hour charts only. Practice 5-10 trades.<br><br>
                        <strong>Days 6-10:</strong> Mix 1-hour and 15-minute charts. Paper trade 10-15 setups.<br><br>
                        <strong>Days 11-20:</strong> Log every trade in a journal. Calculate win rate. Adjust rules if needed.<br><br>
                        <strong>Days 21-30:</strong> Complete 30+ paper trades. Review journal. If 55%+ win rate, consider real money.<br><br>

                        <div class="tip">
                            <strong>ðŸŽ¯ Goal:</strong> 55%+ win rate on 30+ trades. Not 100%, not gambling. 
                            Just proven consistency.
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

    <script>
        function switchModule(moduleId) {
            // Hide all modules
            const modules = document.querySelectorAll('.module');
            modules.forEach(m => m.classList.remove('active'));

            // Remove active from all buttons
            const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('.nav-btn');
            buttons.forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));

            // Show selected module
            document.getElementById(moduleId).classList.add('active');

            // Highlight selected button
            event.target.classList.add('active');
        }
    </script>
